### [36] [Dynamics of Biased Domain Walls: The Rocket Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09432)
*R. B. Vilhena,P. P. Avelino,C. dos Santos*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有简并真空（degenerate vacua）的标量场理论中畴壁（domain walls）的动力学，发现标量场质量对真空态的依赖会导致标量辐射的各向异性发射，产生反冲（rocket）效应，从而偏向低质量真空并促进畴壁网络的衰变。该机制解释了此前归因于势垒不对称性的偏置演化，并构成非简并真空情形下额外的动力学偏置源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解具有简并真空的标量场理论中畴壁网络的演化机制，特别是识别控制网络衰变偏置的真正物理来源。

Method: 采用解析论证（analytical arguments）与数值模拟（numerical simulations）相结合的方法，分析标量场质量随真空态变化时畴壁的辐射发射与反冲效应。

Result: 标量场质量的真空依赖性导致标量辐射从畴壁各向异性发射，优先向标量场质量较小的区域辐射；由此产生的反冲效应使畴壁网络演化偏向低质量真空，促进网络衰变。此外，该反冲机制在非简并真空理论中构成额外的动力学偏置源。

Conclusion: 简并真空理论中畴壁网络的偏置演化主要受标量场质量的真空依赖性控制，而非此前认为的势垒不对称性；在非简并真空情形下，该反冲机制可加速或延缓网络衰变，超越仅基于真空能量密度差异的标准预期。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of domain walls in scalar field theories with degenerate vacua (i.e., vacua of equal energy density) in which the scalar field mass depends on the vacuum state. Using analytical arguments and numerical simulations, we show that this vacuum dependence of the scalar field mass renders the emission of scalar radiation from domain walls anisotropic, preferentially toward regions with smaller scalar field mass. We further show that the resulting recoil (rocket) effect biases the evolution of cosmological domain wall networks in favor of the lower-mass vacuum, thereby promoting network decay. We also demonstrate that the biased evolution of domain walls in theories with degenerate vacua, previously attributed to asymmetries of the potential barrier near the local maximum, is instead primarily controlled by the vacuum dependence of the scalar field mass. More generally, in theories with non-degenerate vacua, this recoil mechanism constitutes an additional source of dynamical bias that can either hasten or delay network decay relative to the standard expectation based solely on differences in vacuum energy density.

</details>


### [37] [Cosmological Constraints on the DGP Model in light of DESI DR2 2025 Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09240)
*Xinyi Dai,Yupeng Yang,Yicheng Wang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文利用最新的重子声学振荡（BAO）数据（来自DESI DR2）、宇宙计时器（CC）、Ia型超新星（SNIa）以及宇宙微波背景（CMB）距离先验，对平坦和非平坦的Dvali-Gabadadze-Porrati（DGP）宇宙学模型给出了更新的约束，结果表明DGP框架无法缓解哈勃常数（Hubble tension）危机，且当前观测数据严重不利于该模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Dvali-Gabadadze-Porrati（DGP）模型作为修正引力的一种替代方案，被提出用于解释宇宙加速膨胀，但其与观测数据的兼容性仍需进一步检验。

Method: 利用Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument Data Release 2（DESI DR2）提供的最新重子声学振荡（BAO）测量数据，并结合宇宙计时器（CC）、Ia型超新星（SNIa）以及宇宙微波背景（CMB）距离先验，在一个统一分析框架下分别对平坦和非平坦DGP模型进行参数约束。

Result: 非平坦DGP模型得到的约束结果为：哈勃常数H0 = 64.05 ± 0.27 km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹，物质密度参数Ωm = 0.3264 ± 0.0043，曲率参数Ωk = 0.0088 ± 0.0016，对应过渡红移（transition redshift）zt ≈ 0.41。平坦DGP模型的约束结果为H0 = 63.28 ± 0.25 km s⁻¹ Mpc⁻¹，Ωm = 0.3303 ± 0.0036。两种情况下的哈勃常数均显著低于Planck ΛCDM模型下的数值。

Conclusion: DGP框架无法缓解哈勃常数（Hubble tension）危机，且当前观测数据（尤其是DESI BAO与CMB的联合约束）严重不利于该模型。这一工作为DGP场景提供了更新且更严格的限制，并在当前宇宙学数据背景下给出了其可行性的综合评估。

Abstract: We present updated constraints on both flat and non-flat Dvali-Gabadadze-Porrati (DGP) cosmological models using the latest baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) measurements from the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument Data Release 2 (DESI DR2), in combination with cosmic chronometer (CC), Type Ia supernova (SNIa), and cosmic microwave background (CMB) distance priors. For the non-flat DGP model, we obtain $H_0 = 64.05 \pm 0.27\, \rm{kms^{-1}Mpc^{-1}}$, $Ω_m = 0.3264 \pm 0.0043$, and $Ω_k = 0.0088 \pm 0.0016$, corresponding to a transition redshift $z_t \sim 0.41$. For the flat case, the constraints are $H_0 = 63.28 \pm 0.25\, \rm{kms^{-1}Mpc^{-1}}$ and $Ω_m = 0.3303 \pm 0.0036$. In both scenarios, the inferred Hubble constant is significantly lower than the Planck $\mathrmΛ$CDM value, indicating that the DGP framework does not alleviate the Hubble tension. Current observations strongly disfavor the DGP framework, primarily due to its inability to simultaneously accommodate DESI BAO and CMB constraints.By incorporating the latest high-precision DESI observations within a unified analysis framework, this work provides updated and more stringent limits on the DGP scenario, offering a consolidated assessment of its viability in the context of current cosmological data.

</details>

### [38] [A note on the stability of surfaces along null cones under area-preserving variations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09325)
*Markus Wolff*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了零锥（null cone）类空截面（spacelike cross section）在保面积变分（area preserving variations）下的稳定性概念，证明了在主导能量条件（dominant energy condition）下，稳定截面的Hawking能量（Hawking energy）存在非负下界；并指出在额外假设下，Hawking能量为零当且仅当该稳定截面等距嵌入（isometrically embed）到Minkowski光锥（Minkowski lightcone）中。主要结果表明，标准Minkowski光锥中仅有的稳定截面是圆球面（round spheres）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 延续Kröncke与作者先前提出的零锥类空截面在保面积变分下的稳定性概念，进一步探讨该稳定性与Hawking能量之间的关系，并试图在特定的时空设定下（4维时空、球面截面）刻画稳定截面的几何特征。

Method: 在4维时空中考虑具有球面截面的零锥，应用主导能量条件，通过数学分析建立稳定截面Hawking能量的非负下界。借鉴Peñuela Diaz近期工作的思路，引入额外假设以推导Hawking能量为零的充要条件。最后，对标准Minkowski光锥进行具体分析，证明其稳定截面只能是圆球面。

Result: 证明了在主导能量条件成立时，稳定截面的Hawking能量具有非负下界。在额外假设下，Hawking能量为零等价于该稳定截面等距嵌入到Minkowski光锥中。此外，标准Minkowski光锥中唯一的稳定截面是圆球面。

Conclusion: 稳定截面与Hawking能量之间的关联在广义相对论（general relativity）的拟局域能量（quasi-local energy）研究中具有重要意义。该结果对Minkowski光锥中稳定截面的分类给出了完整刻画，为后续在更一般时空背景下的稳定性分析提供了理论基础。

Abstract: In this note we investigate a notion of stability for spacelike cross sections of a null cone under area preserving variations that has been introduced in previous work by Kröncke and the author. Here, we consider null cones with spherical cross sections in a $4$-dimensional spacetime and show that the Hawking energy of a stable cross section admits a non-negative lower bound provided the dominant energy condition holds. Similar to a recent work by Peñuela Diaz, we show that under an additional assumption the Hakwing energy is zero if and only if the stable cross section embeds isometrically into the Minkowski lightcone. As a main result, we show that the only stable cross sections of the standard Minkowski lightcone are round spheres.

### [39] [A Self-Consistent Exact Solution from Einstein Gravity: Black Hole in King $\left(2,3,0\right)$ Dark Matter Halos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08792)
*David Senjaya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过完整爱因斯坦场方程构建了由Dehnen (2,3,0)暗物质晕（dark matter halo）包围的静态球对称黑洞解，系统分析了暗物质环境对时空几何、光学现象、准正则模（quasinormal modes）及热力学性质的影响，发现暗物质晕会增大光子球半径和阴影、扩展热力学稳定区域并产生非平凡相结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近年来天体物理暗物质环境中的黑洞解引起广泛关注，本文旨在构造被Dehnen暗物质晕包围的黑洞精确解，并系统研究暗物质环境对黑洞时空几何及可观测效应的物理后果。

Method: 通过完整爱因斯坦场方程（full Einstein field equations）构造由Dehnen (2,3,0)暗物质晕作为源项的静态球对称黑洞精确解；利用零测地线（null geodesics）分析光学效应；计算不稳定零测地线的Lyapunov指数以确定eikonal区域无质量准正则模行为；通过计算守恒质量、Hawking温度、熵、热容和Gibbs自由能评估热力学稳定性。

Result: 暗物质晕显著改变了光子轨迹，位移了圆形光子轨道并变形引力透镜结构；增大了光子球半径和视阴影；扩展了热力学稳定区域；产生了真空Schwarzschild情形不存在的非平凡相结构；准正则模的振荡和阻尼谱出现由暗物质晕诱导的显式修正。

Conclusion: 真实暗物质环境能够导致与孤立黑洞几何可观测的偏差和热力学偏差，可能提供暗物质晕诱导引力效应的新特征信号。

Abstract: Motivated by the growing recent interest in black hole solutions immersed in astrophysical dark matter environments, we construct an exact static, spherically symmetric black hole solution sourced by a Dehnen $\left(2,3,0\right)$ dark matter halo through the full Einstein field equations and investigate the physical consequences of the surrounding halo on the resulting spacetime geometry. The influence of the halo on optical phenomena is analyzed via null geodesics, where we show that the dark matter environment substantially modifies photon trajectories, displaces the circular photon orbits, and deforms the associated gravitational lensing structure. By evaluating the Lyapunov exponent of unstable null geodesics, we further determine the corresponding behavior of massless quasinormal modes in the eikonal regime, revealing explicit corrections to the oscillation and damping spectrum induced by the halo. We then explore the thermodynamic properties of the black hole--halo system by computing the conserved mass, Hawking temperature, entropy, heat capacity, and Gibbs free energy, allowing for a detailed assessment of both local and global thermal stability. Our analysis demonstrates that the dark matter halo increases the radius of the photon sphere and the apparent shadow, enlarges the domain of thermodynamic stability, and generates nontrivial phase structures absent in the vacuum Schwarzschild case. These results highlight that realistic dark matter environments can produce observable and thermodynamic deviations from isolated black hole geometries, potentially offering novel signatures of halo-induced gravitational effects.

### [40] [Novel Kerr-Hernquist Black Hole: Quasibound State, Scalar Cloud, Bomb, Superradiant Scattering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08796)
*David Senjaya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过在Schwarzschild–Hernquist时空中应用Newman–Janis算法，构造了一种被Hernquist暗物质晕包围的旋转黑洞解（Kerr–Hernquist几何），并利用解析渐近匹配方法研究了标量场动力学，揭示了暗物质晕对准束缚态谱、标量云形成、黑洞炸弹不稳定性及超辐射散射的调控机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞解未纳入现实暗物质环境，缺乏一个自洽的轴对称背景用于研究旋转黑洞在暗物质晕中的标量场动力学行为。

Method: 采用Newman–Janis算法将精确的Schwarzschild–Hernquist时空扩展为旋转的Kerr–Hernquist几何；利用解析渐近匹配方法（analytical asymptotic matching method）推导准束缚态（quasibound-state）能谱，并分析超辐射散射（superradiant scattering）放大因子。

Result: 暗物质晕保留了类氢结构的准束缚态谱，但引入由组合参数ρ₀r₀³控制的修正；增加晕密度与尺度半径会增大标量场结合能、降低标量云形成的临界场质量、抑制共转模（m_ℓ>0）的超辐射不稳定性增长率、加速反转模（m_ℓ<0）的衰减；暗物质晕同时削弱了超辐射放大的幅度和频率范围。

Conclusion: Kerr–Hernquist几何为研究准束缚态、标量云、黑洞炸弹和超辐射散射提供了统一框架，并揭示了Hernquist暗物质晕如何在旋转黑洞的能谱与稳定性上留下可观测印记。

Abstract: We present a novel rotating black hole solution surrounded by a Hernquist dark matter halo, obtained by applying the Newman--Janis algorithm to the exact Schwarzschild--Hernquist spacetime. The resulting Kerr--Hernquist geometry provides an axisymmetric background for investigating scalar-field dynamics in realistic dark matter environments. Using the analytical asymptotic matching method, we derive the quasibound-state spectrum, identify the conditions for scalar cloud formation and the black hole bomb instability, and obtain an analytic expression for the superradiant scattering amplification factor. We show that the halo preserves the hydrogen-like structure of the quasibound-state spectrum while introducing corrections governed by the combination $ρ_0 r_0^3$. Increasing the halo density and scale radius enhances the scalar-field binding energy, lowers the critical field mass for scalar cloud formation, suppresses the growth rate of the superradiant instability for co-rotating modes ($m_\ell>0$), and accelerates the decay of counter-rotating modes ($m_\ell<0$). Furthermore, the dark matter halo reduces both the magnitude and frequency range of superradiant amplification, thereby weakening energy extraction from the black hole. These results demonstrate that the Kerr--Hernquist geometry provides a unified framework for studying quasibound states, scalar clouds, black hole bombs, and superradiant scattering, while revealing how a Hernquist dark matter halo leaves observable imprints on the spectrum and stability of rotating black holes.

</details>


### [41] [Einstein--Gauss--Bonnet Inflationary Cosmology in Phase-$θ$ Formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08807)
*Gevorg D. Manucharyan,Igor V. Fomin,Shivam Kumar Mishra,B. Mishra*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦-高斯-波内特（Einstein–Gauss–Bonnet, EGB）引力框架下，提出了一种基于相位θ参数化的暴胀动力学描述方法，使得背景演化与标量、张量扰动系数仅由单调相位变量和哈勃参数表达，从而建立从模型参数到暴胀可观测量（inflationary observables）的解析映射。该方法在全暴胀时期（包括慢滚近似失效的暴胀结束阶段）保持正则性。以Starobinsky型势加线性高斯-波内特耦合为例，所得预言与ACT DR6和BICEP/Keck最新数据一致，并进一步计算了随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational-wave background）及其可探测性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 利用宇宙微波背景（CMB）数据检验暴胀模型的核心挑战在于：在慢滚近似（slow-roll regime）失效的区域，标准的一致性关系（consistency relations）不再适用，难以获得精确的可观测预言。本文旨在克服这一困难，在EGB引力中发展一种在暴胀全程（包括结束阶段）均保持有效的参数化方法。

Method: 引入相位θ参数化（phase-θ parametrization），将背景演化与标量、张量扰动系数完全表达为单调相位变量和哈勃参数（Hubble parameter）的函数，从而建立从模型背景参数到暴胀可观测量的闭式解析映射。该方法在包括暴胀结束在内的整个暴胀时期保持正则性。

Result: 以带有线性高斯-波内特耦合的Starobinsky型势为例，利用该形式得出预言与ACT DR6及BICEP/Keck的最新约束一致，明确展示了非最小高斯-波内特耦合对宇宙学扰动参数预期值的影响。此外，计算了对应的残余随机引力波背景（relic stochastic gravitational-wave background），并评估了其在当前及未来引力波观测站中的可探测性。

Conclusion: 所提出的相位θ参数化为EGB引力中超出慢滚近似的暴胀模型提供了一种全程正则的解析分析工具，能有效连接模型参数与CMB及引力波观测，具有广泛的适用性和观测检验潜力。

Abstract: A central challenge in testing inflationary scenarios with cosmic microwave background (CMB) data is to derive predictions for cosmological observables that remain accurate beyond the slow-roll regime, where the standard consistency relations are no longer applicable. We address this issue in the context of Einstein--Gauss--Bonnet (EGB) gravity by introducing a phase-$θ$ parametrization of the inflationary dynamics. Within this framework, the background evolution and the coefficients governing scalar and tensor perturbations are expressed entirely in terms of a single monotonic phase variable and the Hubble parameter. This construction provides a closed, analytical mapping between the background parameters of a given model and the associated inflationary observables. A notable advantage of the proposed parametrization is that it remains regular throughout the inflationary epoch, including the end-of-inflation regime, in which the conventional slow-roll consistency relations no longer hold. As an illustrative application, we consider a Starobinsky-type potential supplemented by a linear coupling between the inflaton and the Gauss--Bonnet invariant. Using the proposed formalism, we demonstrate that the resulting predictions of the Starobinsky model are consistent with the most recent constraints from ACT DR6 and BICEP/Keck, explicitly incorporating the impact of the non-minimal Gauss--Bonnet coupling on the expected values of the cosmological perturbation parameters. Finally, we compute the corresponding relic stochastic gravitational-wave background and evaluate its detectability with current and forthcoming gravitational-wave observatories.

</details>


### [42] [A Small-Throat Boundary Condition for the Tunneling Wave Function of the Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08815)
*Masaki Yamada*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在洛伦兹路径积分（Lorentzian path integral）框架下，提出了一种闭合宇宙波函数的小喉（small-throat）方案，通过引入小辐射分量并施加诺伊曼边界条件（Neumann condition）与喉域限制，将隧穿波函数（tunneling wave function）作为从极小宇宙隧穿的极限形式导出，而非直接在零几何上施加边界条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准隧穿波函数要求直接在消失几何（vanishing geometry）上施加边界条件，这在概念上不够自然。本文受“宇宙创生可作为通过小喉与另一宇宙连接的隧穿几何的解耦（decoupling）或缩颈（pinch-off）极限”这一想法的启发，试图在洛伦兹路径积分框架下更自然地导出隧穿波函数。

Method: 在具有正宇宙学常数（positive cosmological constant）的闭合极小超空间（minisuperspace）模型中引入一个由参数 ε 参数化的小辐射分量，产生两个转折点：内转折点 q_-∼O(ε) 和外转折点 q_+∼H^{-2}。在喉的初始端点施加诺伊曼条件 \dot q(0)=0，并将初始尺度 q_i 限制在小喉域 0<|q_i|<√ε/H（包含内转折点）。通过这一有限喉鞍点问题（finite-throat saddle problem）的定义，再取 ε→0 极限，使小喉域坍缩至 q_i→0。

Result: 该方案通过限制鞍点选择的黎曼（Riemann）片层及其Picard–Lefschetz循环，保留了小喉隧穿鞍点（small-throat tunneling saddle），排除了与外转折点相关的不受抑制的鞍点。取 ε→0 极限后，鞍点作用量（saddle action）约化为标准隧穿鞍点作用量。改变陡线（lapse）围道可选择哈特尔-霍金（Hartle–Hawking）型增长分支。

Conclusion: 隧穿波函数可以被视为洛伦兹路径积分中从一个任意小的宇宙隧穿的极限形式，而非直接在消失几何上施加边界条件的结果。这为宇宙波函数的边界条件提供了更自然的路径积分理解。

Abstract: We propose a small-throat prescription for the wave function of a closed universe in the Lorentzian path integral formalism, motivated by the idea that universe creation may be obtained as the decoupling, or pinch-off, limit of a tunneling geometry connected to another universe through a small throat. Instead of retaining the parent-universe side explicitly, we describe the remaining half-geometry by a minisuperspace path integral with boundary conditions imposed at the throat. To model the finite throat, we introduce a small radiation component parametrized by $ε$ in a closed minisuperspace model with a positive cosmological constant. The radiation term produces two turning points, an inner one $q_-\sim O(ε)$ and an outer one $q_+\sim H^{-2}$, where $q$ is the square of the scale factor. Our prescription imposes the Neumann condition $\dot q(0)=0$ at the initial endpoint and restricts the initial size $q_i=q(0)$ to a small-throat domain $0<|q_i|<\sqrtε/H$ that contains $q_-$. This restriction selects the Riemann sheet containing the small-throat tunneling saddle and its Picard--Lefschetz cycle, while excluding the unsuppressed saddle associated with the outer turning point $q_+$. Taking the limit $ε\to0$ after this finite-throat saddle problem has been defined, the small-throat domain collapses to $q_i \to 0$, and the saddle action reduces to that of the standard tunneling saddle. Other choices of lapse contour can instead select Hartle--Hawking-type growing branches. In this sense, the tunneling wave function can be obtained as the limiting form of tunneling from an arbitrarily small universe in a Lorentzian path integral, rather than by imposing a boundary condition directly at a vanishing geometry.

</details>


### [43] [Generalized Fisher-Janis-Newman-Winicour (FJNW) and Yilmaz-Rosen solutions in the higher-dimensional scalar-tensor theory with nonminimal coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08880)
*K. K. Ernazarov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于高阶标量-张量引力理论（higher-dimensional scalar-tensor theories），系统重构了两种静态球对称解——FJNW度规（Fisher-Janis-Newman-Winicour metric）和广义Yilmaz-Rosen度规——对应的耦合函数$f(φ)$与标量势$U(φ)$，发现前者在特定维度下对应正则标量场，后者在所有高维情形下均对应幻象标量场（phantom scalar field）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高阶维标量-张量引力理论中非最小耦合情形下的精确球对称解重构，旨在揭示不同度规族对应的耦合函数$f(φ)$与势$U(φ)$的性质。

Method: 采用先前工作中发展的形式化方法（formalism），利用Jordan框架（Jordan frame）下的主方程形式（master equation formalism），系统推导FJNW度规和广义Yilmaz-Rosen度规两类解的耦合函数与标量势的关系式。

Result: 对于FJNW度规，在$s=2$、$D=6$的特殊情形下，耦合函数$f(φ)$在区域$u^3 > M$内为正，对应引力吸引与正则标量场（canonical scalar field），势$U(φ)=0$；对于广义Yilmaz-Rosen度规，在任意维度$D > 4$下，重构的耦合函数恒为负$f(φ) < 0$，对应幻象标量场（phantom scalar field）与排斥引力（repulsive gravity）。

Conclusion: 不同球对称度规族在标量-张量理论框架下表现出截然不同的标量场性质：FJNW度规可在特定条件下实现正则标量场，而广义Yilmaz-Rosen度规则在所有高维情形下必然导致幻象标量场。

Abstract: This paper investigates higher-dimensional scalar-tensor theories of gravity with nonminimal coupling, focusing on the reconstruction of exact spherically symmetric solutions. We systematically apply the formalism developed in previous works, which demonstrates that any static spherically symmetric metric can be represented as an exact solution of a scalar-tensor theory with specific coupling functions $f(φ)$ and potential $U(φ)$. Our analysis centers on two important classes of solutions in arbitrary spacetime dimensions: the Fisher-Janis-Newman-Winicour (FJNW) metric and its limiting case, the generalized Yilmaz-Rosen metric.
  We derive the key relations for the coupling function $f(φ)$ and the scalar field potential $U(φ)$ for both solution families using the master equation formalism in the Jordan frame. For the FJNW metric, we find that in the special case $s = 2$, $D = 6$, the coupling function $f(φ)$ is positive in the domain $u^3 > M$, corresponding to gravitational attraction and a canonical scalar field with vanishing potential $U(φ) = 0$. In contrast, for the generalized Yilmaz-Rosen metric in arbitrary dimensions $D > 4$, the reconstructed coupling function is always negative, $f(φ) < 0$, indicating a phantom scalar field with negative kinetic energy and repulsive gravity.

</details>


### [44] [Probing Rotating Einstein-Power-Yang-Mills Black Holes through Shadows and Quasinormal Modes: Prospects for Event Horizon Telescope Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08884)
*I. Ezzaki,A. El Boukili,H. Lekbich,A. Benami*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在爱因斯坦幂杨-米尔斯引力（Einstein power-Yang-Mills gravity, EPYM）框架下，通过Newman-Janis方法构建旋转黑洞，分析其视界结构、光子区域及阴影，并利用M87*和Sgr A*的事件视界望远镜（Event Horizon Telescope）观测数据约束杨-米尔斯电荷与幂参数，同时计算了该背景上的标量场准正则模（quasinormal modes）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在修正引力理论中检验黑洞可观测特征（阴影与准正则模）对非阿贝尔规范场电荷及非线性幂参数的依赖关系，并利用实际天文观测对其进行参数约束。

Method: 采用Newman-Janis方法从球对称静态种子度规构造旋转黑洞解；通过求解测地线方程分析阴影；利用事件视界望远镜（EHT）对M87*和Sgr A*的角大小与史瓦西偏差δ的测量数据进行贝叶斯似然估计与参数约束；通过WKB近似（Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin）求解Teukolsky型径向势上的无质量标量场准正则模。

Result: 在Maxwell点q=1处，联合双源的自旋边缘化似然将电荷约束为Q≲0.26M（1σ）；固定自旋a=0.7M时仅由M87*角大小给出较弱约束Q≲0.52M。当q→3/2时阴影直径对电荷几乎不敏感。电荷和近极端自旋抑制能量发射率，幂参数增强之。准正则模的振荡频率随电荷或自旋增加而上升，衰减率下降。

Conclusion: EPYM旋转黑洞的阴影与准正则模对杨-米尔斯电荷和幂参数敏感，当前观测数据可对电荷给出有效约束，但幂参数在准正则谱中的偏移低于现有探测器分辨率。

Abstract: Within Einstein power-Yang-Mills gravity (EPYM), we build a rotating black hole via the Newman-Janis procedure applied to the spherically symmetric static seed, obtaining a Kerr-like metric controlled by the spin \(a\), the magnetic Yang-Mills charge \(Q\), and the power parameter \(q\). We analyse the horizon structure and the photon region, and we compute the shadow as it appears to a remote observer for different values of these parameters. Using the published Event Horizon Telescope measurements of M87\(^*\) and Sgr A\(^*\), we constrain the Yang-Mills charge and the power parameter from the angular size and the Schwarzschild deviation \(δ\) of the observed images. At the Maxwell point \(q = 1\) the spin marginalized likelihood combining both sources bounds the charge to \(Q \lesssim 0.26\,M\) at \(1σ\), while the fixed-spin band intersection at \(a = 0.7\,M\) gives the weaker \(Q \lesssim 0.52\,M\) from the M87\(^*\) angular size alone. The bound weakens as \(q \to 3/2\), where the shadow diameter becomes nearly insensitive to the charge. The shadow radius also fixes the limiting absorption cross section at high frequencies and hence the energy emission rate, which is suppressed by the charge, enhanced by the power parameter, and suppressed at near-extremal spin. We then compute the quasinormal modes of a massless scalar on the rotating background from the leading-order Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin (WKB) conditions on the Teukolsky type radial potential, finding that the oscillation frequency rises and the damping rate falls as the charge or spin increases. The power parameter leaves an imprint on the shadow size and its charge sensitivity and in the quasinormal spectrum the shift is in principle present but lies below the resolution of current detectors.

</details>


### [45] [A Physical space derivation of Morawetz-Energy estimates in Kerr spacetimes with large angular momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08958)
*Lili He,Sergiu Klainerman*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Kerr时空中重新推导了标量波动方程的Morawetz能量估计，发展了一套适用于推广到Kerr实际扰动的物理空间方法。证明结合了条件性Morawetz估计、Stogin的低频处理技巧、Hardy型不等式、物理空间版本的Whiting变换以及Andersson–Blue不变算子方法，最终得到无条件全局时间Morawetz估计。结果限于|a|/m ≤ 0.75的自旋0标量波，但预期可推广到Teukolsky方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Kerr时空的外通讯区域（domain of outer communication）中重新推导标量波动方程的Morawetz能量估计，目标是发展稳健的物理空间方法（physical-space methods），使其能够适用于Kerr时空真实扰动（realistic perturbations）的扩展研究。

Method: 首先推导条件性Morawetz估计，利用物理空间表征（physical-space characterization）完整r范围内的陷俘零测地线（trapped null geodesics），扩展了Andersson–Blue及本团队前期工作的技术。其次，引入Stogin在轴对称情形下处理低频困难的思想；在一般情况下，通过充分利用Morawetz体范数（bulk norm）中的主陷俘项并结合Hardy型不等式来控制低阶项。进一步，通过物理空间版本的Whiting变换和Andersson–Blue不变算子方法，分别处理边界项和视界通量（horizon flux）的估计。最后，通过连续性论证得到无条件全局时间Morawetz估计，并利用在陷俘集上为Killing场的因果向量场构造新的能量估计。

Result: 在|a|/m ≤ 0.75范围内，针对自旋0的标量波动方程建立了无条件全局时间Morawetz估计（unconditional global-in-time Morawetz estimate）以及新的能量估计。

Conclusion: 本文的结果目前限于标量波方程及|a|/m ≤ 0.75的参数范围，但预期这一限制是技术性的，所发展的方法可以推广到Teukolsky方程（Teukolsky equation）。

Abstract: We revisit the derivation of Morawetz--energy estimates for scalar wave equations in the domain of outer communication of a Kerr spacetime \(\KK(a,m)\). Our goal is to develop robust physical-space methods which are well suited for extension to realistic perturbations of Kerr.
  The proof rests on several ingredients. First, we derive conditional Morawetz estimates which extend the physical-space techniques initiated by Andersson and Blue \cite{AB}, and later adapted in \cite{GKS} to perturbations of slowly rotating Kerr, by exploiting a physical-space characterization of the full \(r\)-range of trapped null geodesics. Second, we use an idea introduced by Stogin \cite{St} in the axially symmetric case to handle the low-frequency difficulties in the Morawetz estimates. In the general case, the control of the lower-order terms also requires making full use of the principal trapping term in the Morawetz bulk norm, together with a new use of Hardy-type inequalities.
  A further new ingredient is the control of the boundary terms generated by the Morawetz estimates. This is based on two additional ideas: physical-space versions of Whiting's transform \cite{W}, developed in a forthcoming paper \cite{H-K2}, which yield a flux-independent energy estimate; and an adaptation of the Andersson--Blue invariant-operator method, which turns that estimate into a bound for the horizon flux. Finally, a continuity argument yields an unconditional global-in-time Morawetz estimate, while a new energy estimate is obtained from the construction of a causal vectorfield which is Killing on the trapping set.
  The results proved here are restricted to scalar wave equations, corresponding to spin \(0\), in the range \(|a|/m\leq 0.75\). We expect this restriction to be technical, and the methods developed in this paper to extend to the Teukolsky equation.

### [46] [Repetitive Penrose Process in Rotating 4D Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08989)
*Mohammad Reza Alipour,Mohammad Ali S. Afshar,Saeed Noori Gashti*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了旋转四维爱因斯坦-高斯-博内黑洞中的重复彭罗斯过程，发现高斯-博内耦合在迭代中自放大，抑制了强耦合区域的提取过程，并导致效率景观出现耦合驱动的四区到三区重组，这在已知黑洞解中未见先例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高斯-博内（Gauss–Bonnet）耦合对重复彭罗斯过程（repetitive Penrose process）的影响，特别是在旋转四维爱因斯坦-高斯-博内（Einstein–Gauss–Bonnet, EGB）黑洞背景下，该过程是否因耦合自放大而表现出与Kerr黑洞不同的新特征。

Method: 采用修正的Newman–Janis算法构造旋转EGB黑洞，建立非线性迭代方案，每轮提取后更新质量、角动量和不可约质量；施加三重转折点条件求解能量、角动量和径向动量的守恒方程，得到闭式解。

Result: 耦合增大降低极限自旋、收缩能层并减少允许衰变次数，强耦合下近黑洞视界处过程被禁止且未提取粒子控制终止条件；能量投资回报随无量纲耦合单调递减，不可约质量增长受抑制；效率在临界耦合以下呈四区结构（含EGB优于Kerr的窗口），临界耦合以上塌缩为三区结构。

Conclusion: EGB黑洞中的重复彭罗斯过程展现出耦合驱动的效率景观重组，该现象在Kerr、Reissner–Nordström、Kerr–de Sitter、加速Kerr或Kerr–Newman黑洞中均无对应，表明高斯-博内耦合在该过程中引入了本质上的新物理行为。

Abstract: We investigate the repetitive Penrose process for neutral particles in a rotating four-dimensional Einstein--Gauss--Bonnet black hole obtained through the modified Newman--Janis algorithm, developing a nonlinear iterative scheme in which the mass, angular momentum, and irreducible mass are updated after each extraction event. Imposing the triple turning-point condition, we obtain a closed-form solution of the conservation equations for energy, angular momentum, and radial momentum that reduces to the Kerr result in the limit of vanishing coupling. The distinctive feature of this background is that, although the Gauss--Bonnet coupling $α$ is a fixed constant of the action and is not carried by the infalling fragments, the dimensionless coupling $\hatα=α/M^{2}$ grows at every iteration as the mass decreases, so that the effective Gauss--Bonnet correction is self-amplified along the sequence. We find that a larger coupling lowers the extremal spin, contracts the ergosphere, and reduces the number of admissible decays, forbidding the process near the horizon at strong coupling while permitting it at larger decay radii; the termination is controlled throughout by the incident particle. The energy return on investment decreases monotonically with $\hatα$ and the growth of the irreducible mass is suppressed relative to Kerr, whereas the energy utilization efficiency is non-monotonic: below a critical coupling the parameter space exhibits a four-region structure with a bounded window in which the EGB black hole is more efficient than Kerr; this four-region structure collapses into a three-region one above a critical coupling. This coupling-driven reorganization of the efficiency landscape has no analogue in the Kerr, Reissner--Nordström, Kerr--de~Sitter, accelerating Kerr, or Kerr--Newman cases.

### [47] [Thermodynamic Consistency of Logarithmic Entropy Corrections on the Schwarzschild Branch of $f(\mathbb{Q})$ Gravity and a Superradiance No-Go Result](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09041)
*Wen-Xiang Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文对称遥平行引力（symmetric teleparallel gravity）的Schwarzschild分支上，分析了经对数修正的黑洞热力学（logarithmically corrected black-hole thermodynamics）以及标量场散射（scalar scattering）。研究发现，线性分支在动力学上等价于一般相对论（general relativity）加边界项，真空解为Schwarzschild时空。对数修正改变了由修正第一定律定义的温度，但几何Hawking温度保持不变；热容发散出现在对数展开不可靠的区域，因此不能视为物理相变。标量散射方面，中性静态背景下无超辐射放大（superradiant amplification），熵修正对散射振幅无一级影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在对称遥平行引力框架下，对Schwarzschild黑洞解进行对数修正的热力学分析，并考察其对标量场散射的影响，以检验该修正是否引发新的物理效应（如相变或超辐射）。

Method: 将度规（metric）和平直无挠仿射联络（flat, torsion-free affine connection）作为独立变量，构造非度规几何（nonmetricity geometry）和场方程；通过Noether电荷法和经典第一定律导出领头阶熵，而后引入对数修正；在固定几何和ADM质量下对比不同温度定义；推导标量径向方程、有效势、守恒Wronskian量和反射-透射关系。

Result: 线性分支动力学等价于一般相对论加边界项，真空解为Schwarzschild时空；对数修正下几何Hawking温度不变，而修正第一定律定义的温度改变；热容发散位于对数展开不可靠区域，非物理相变；中性静态背景下标量场无超辐射放大；熵修正不对散射振幅产生一级改变。

Conclusion: 对称遥平行引力中的Schwarzschild黑洞经对数修正后，其热力学和散射性质与一般相对论定性一致，未出现新的相位转变或超辐射效应；对散射振幅的一级修正需依赖半经典反作用（semiclassical backreaction）或旋转/带电黑洞解。

Abstract: We present a concise and explicit analysis of logarithmically corrected black-hole thermodynamics and scalar scattering on the Schwarzschild branch of symmetric teleparallel gravity. Treating the metric and the flat, torsion-free affine connection as independent variables, we formulate the relevant nonmetricity geometry and field equations and show that the linear branch is dynamically equivalent to general relativity up to a boundary term. The vacuum solution is therefore the Schwarzschild spacetime. The leading entropy is derived from both the Noether-charge method and the classical first law, after which a logarithmic correction is introduced. When the geometry and ADM mass are kept fixed, the geometric Hawking temperature remains unchanged, whereas the temperature defined through the corrected first law is modified. The apparent divergence of the heat capacity occurs outside the regime in which the logarithmic expansion is reliable and therefore cannot be interpreted as a physical phase transition. We also derive the scalar radial equation, effective potential, conserved Wronskian, and reflection-transmission relation. For a neutral scalar field on a static neutral background, no superradiant amplification occurs, and the entropy correction produces no first-order change in the scattering amplitudes unless a genuine semiclassical backreaction or an explicit rotating or charged black-hole solution is provided.

Given that such a mission would likely take about a hundred years and require substantial financial and human investment, it is essential to assess whether it could investigate black holes and test General Relativity to a degree that cannot be achieved by Solar System observatories for the foreseeable future. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往关于暗能量有效场论中Vainshtein机制的讨论大多假设球对称性，但实际天体并不严格球对称。本文旨在检验该机制在超越球对称情形下是否仍然有效。

Method: 假设偏离球对称性较小，针对给定的非球形引力源计算引力势的多极矩（multipole moments），并重点关注“beyond Horndeski”型EFT参数的作用。

Result: 对于一般参数选择，当单极分量被屏蔽时，第五力（fifth force）的多极矩未被屏蔽，引力势的多极分量呈现特征性振荡行为。在调节参数使引力子衰变（graviton decay）几乎消失的特殊情形下，多极矩行为虽有质的不同，但Vainshtein机制仍无法有效屏蔽源周围的第五力。

Conclusion: 在超越球对称的背景下，暗能量有效场论中的Vainshtein机制不足以屏蔽非球形引力源周围的第五力，暗示了对该机制适用范围的重要限制。

Abstract: It has been argued that degenerate higher-order scalar-tensor theories and the effective field theory (EFT) of dark energy are endowed with the Vainshtein mechanism, resulting in a screened fifth force in the exterior of a gravitational source. However, spherical symmetry has been assumed in most of the discussions so far. In this paper, we study whether the Vainshtein mechanism operates in the EFT of dark energy beyond spherical symmetry, focusing in particular on the role of the ``beyond Horndeski'' EFT parameters. Assuming that deviations from spherical symmetry are small, we compute multipole moments of the gravitational potential for a given nonspherical source. For a generic choice of the ``beyond Horndeski'' EFT parameters, it is shown that the multipole moments of the fifth force are not screened in the region where the monopole component is screened. Rather, the gravitational potential shows a characteristic oscillatory behavior in its multipole components. In the special case where the EFT parameters are tuned so that graviton decay into dark energy is practically absent, the behavior of the multipole moments is qualitatively different from that in the generic case. However, also in this case, the Vainshtein mechanism is not efficient enough to screen the fifth force around the source.

### [50] [Nonlinear stability of Einstein-de Sitter universes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09326)
*Louie Bernhardt,David Fajman,Zoe Wyatt*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明，在具有多方状态方程（polytropic equation of state）的爱因斯坦-欧拉方程（Einstein-Euler equations）框架下，托环面 $\mathbb{T}^3$ 上近平坦度规（near-flat metric）与正流体能量密度（positive fluid energy density）的初值集（initial data set）会收敛于平坦度规，从而渐近于爱因斯坦-德西特时空（Einstein-de Sitter spacetime）。该结果解决了爱因斯坦-德西特模型在适当物质模型下能否实现非线性稳定性（nonlinear stability）的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 爱因斯坦-德西特宇宙（Einstein-de Sitter universe）是宇宙学中描述冷暗物质主导时期（cold dark matter-dominated epoch）的主流模型，但其在无压流体（pressureless fluid）状态方程下的爱因斯坦-欧拉方程中呈线性不稳定性（linearly unstable）。因此，需要检验该模型在更合适的物质模型（如多方状态方程）下能否实现非线性稳定（nonlinearly stable）。

Method: 研究基于爱因斯坦-欧拉方程，在紧致流形 $\mathbb{T}^3$（三维托环面）上考虑具有多方状态方程（polytropic equation of state）的流体。初值条件设定为近平坦度规（near-flat metric）与正流体能量密度（positive fluid energy density），通过分析该初值下爱因斯坦-欧拉流（Einstein-Euler flow）的长时间行为来检验解的收敛性。

Result: 证明了上述初值集在爱因斯坦-欧拉流作用下会收敛至平坦度规（flat metric），即度规渐近于爱因斯坦-德西特时空。这证实了爱因斯坦-德西特模型在多方状态方程下具有非线性稳定性（nonlinear stability）。

Conclusion: 该研究解决了爱因斯坦-德西特模型能否在适当物质模型下实现非线性稳定的问题。结论表明，当采用多方状态方程时，该模型是稳定的，这为宇宙学中冷暗物质主导时期的稳定性提供了理论支持。

Abstract: The Einstein-de Sitter universe is the prevailing model used in cosmology to describe the cold dark matter-dominated epoch of the universe. This model is a spatially homogeneous and isotropic spacetime undergoing decelerated expansion, and is linearly unstable under the Einstein-Euler equations with a pressureless fluid equation of state. We show that every initial data set for the Einstein-Euler equations on $\mathbb{T}^3$ with a near-flat metric and positive fluid energy density converges to a flat metric under the Einstein-Euler flow with a polytropic equation of state. This means the metric asymptotes to an Einstein-de Sitter spacetime. In particular, this settles the question of whether the Einstein-de Sitter model can be nonlinearly stable for an appropriate matter model.

### [51] [Joint inference for gravitational-wave signal and noise glitch: Method and application](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09111)
*Shun Yin Cheung,Rhiannon Udall,Derek Davis,Paul D. Lasky,Eric Thrane*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文介绍了 bilby_glitch 管道，这是一种用于引力波观测中同时进行引力波信号和噪声瞬变（glitch）贝叶斯推断的模块化分析框架。该管道基于 bilby 框架构建，集成了多种 glitch 模型（慢散射模型、正弦-高斯模型和 chirplet 模型）。通过对模拟和真实数据的测试，以及对 GW191109 和 GW200129 两个引力波事件的重新分析，展示了管道的可靠性，并揭示了波形容限（waveform approximant）与 glitch 模型之间的相互作用会影响天体物理结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波天文台中的非高斯噪声瞬变（non-Gaussian noise transients, 即 glitches）会降低天体物理推断（astrophysical inference）的准确性，因此需要一种能够同时处理引力波信号和 glitch 的联合推断方法。

Method: 提出了 bilby_glitch 管道，该管道基于 bilby 框架构建，采用模块化设计，集成了 transdimensional bilby，并实现了三种 glitch 模型：基于物理的慢散射模型（slow scattering model），以及灵活的 sine-Gaussian 和 chirplet 模型。

Result: 在模拟和真实数据上验证了管道的可靠性。重新分析 GW191109 的结果与先前研究一致。对于 GW200129，使用 NRSur7dq4 波形容限结合小波基 glitch 建模时，自旋进动（spin-precession）证据显著减弱；而使用 IMRPhenomXPHM 结合相同 glitch 建模时，则显示出强烈的自旋进动证据。

Conclusion: GW200129 的天体物理结论取决于波形容限与 glitch 模型之间的相互作用，表明在进行高影响力引力波事件分析时，必须谨慎选择并联合建模波形容限和噪声瞬变模型。

Abstract: Non-Gaussian noise transients ("glitches") in gravitational-wave observatories degrade our ability to accurately perform astrophysical inference. We present the analysis pipeline bilby_glitch, which allows for simultaneous Bayesian inference of gravitational-wave signals and glitches. Our framework is modular and built on top of the popular bilby framework, facilitating future extensions with additional glitch and signal models. We integrate transdimensional bilby into our framework and discuss three glitch models: a physically-motivated slow scattering model, and flexible sine-Gaussian and chirplet models. Using a combination of simulated and real data, we demonstrate that bilby_glitch produces reliable results. We then reanalyse two gravitational-wave events - GW191109 and GW200129 - which show signs of interesting black-hole spins, but which may also be affected by data-quality issues. Our results for GW191109 are consistent with previous analysis. For GW200129, we recover results consistent with Payne et al., where the evidence of spin-precession is much weaker when using the waveform approximant NRSur7dq4 in combination with wavelet-based glitch modeling. Furthermore, we show the astrophysical conclusion of this event is dependent on the interplay between the waveform approximant and glitch model, since in contrast to NRSur7dq4 we find that inference with the waveform approximant IMRPhenomXPHM shows strong evidence of spin-precession when used in combination with wavelet-based glitch modeling.

</details>


### [52] [Influence of chemical potential to explain the maximum mass and tidal love number of strange stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09120)
*Debadri Bhattacharjee,Pradip Kumar Chattopadhyay*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了MIT袋模型（MIT bag model）中袋常数（bag constant）随夸克化学势（chemical potential）变化对奇异夸克物质（strange quark matter）及致密星（compact star）结构性质的影响。通过Bodmer-Witten稳定性判据约束参数空间，并求解Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff方程，发现化学势增大使袋常数有效值降低、物态方程变硬、最大质量增大，且潮汐形变满足GW170817事件约束（Λ<800）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索介质效应（medium effects）对奇异夸克物质的影响，特别是化学势依赖的袋常数如何改变奇异星（strange stars）的最大质量与潮汐形变能力，以更准确地描述致密星内部物质的行为。

Method: 将MIT袋模型物态方程中的袋常数重定义为夸克化学势的函数；基于Bodmer-Witten稳定性判据，通过计算每重子能量（energy per baryon）约束参数空间；求解Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff方程获得最大质量-半径构型；并计算潮汐Love数（tidal Love number）与潮汐形变率（tidal deformability）。

Result: 化学势增大导致袋常数有效值下降，物态方程变硬，最大恒星质量增大；在所选的参数组合下，潮汐形变率始终满足GW170817事件给出的Λ<800的约束。

Conclusion: 化学势（μ）显著影响奇异星的最大质量和潮汐形变能力，引入介质效应后的模型能够同时满足天文观测对质量和潮汐形变的约束。

Abstract: We investigate the influence of medium effects on strange quark matter and their consequences for the structural properties of compact stars. In this study, the bag constant, in the MIT bag model equation of state, is reformulated as a function of the chemical potential of quark. Imposing the Bodmer-Witten stability criterion, the parameter space is constrained by evaluating the energy per baryon. The Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff equations are then solved to obtain the maximum mass-radius configurations. Our analysis shows that an increase in chemical potential leads to a reduction in the effective value of bag constant, resulting in a stiffer equation of state and correspondingly higher value of maximum stellar mass. Furthermore, we examine the chemical potential dependence of the tidal Love number and tidal deformability. The results demonstrate that, for the chosen set of parameters, the constraint from the GW170817 event, namely $Λ< 800$, is consistently satisfied. In this paper, we have tried to establish how chemical potential $(μ)$ affects the maximum mass and tidal deformability of strange stars.

### [53] [Six-Field Rational Extended Thermodynamics of Polyatomic Gases in Curved Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09463)
*L. Gallerani,A. Giusti,A. Mentrelli,T. Ruggeri*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个一般协变的六场理性扩展热力学（RET₆）模型，用于描述相对论性多原子气体，该模型基于玻尔兹曼-切尔尼科夫动力学方程和最大熵（Maximum Entropy）闭合，并将其耦合至爱因斯坦方程。在FLRW时空中，动力学压强修正了膨胀动力学，但一个无干涉定理排除了单纯由RET₆气体驱动的加速；引入宇宙学常数后的ΛRET₆模型在晚期呈现出de Sitter吸引子，数值积分显示其膨胀历史快速接近ΛCDM模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有相对论性理性扩展热力学（Rational Extended Thermodynamics, RET）模型多基于现象学假设，缺乏第一性原理（first-principles）的动力学基础；此外，多原子气体在非平衡状态下的引力效应，特别是动力学压强（dynamical pressure）在宇宙学膨胀中的作用，尚未得到严格的结构性分析。

Method: 该模型基于多原子推广的玻尔兹曼-切尔尼科夫动力学方程（Boltzmann-Chernikov kinetic equation），其中单粒子分布函数额外依赖于内能变量（internal-energy variable），并采用最大熵原理（Maximum Entropy Principle）对相对论性矩层级（moment hierarchy）进行闭合。场方程、闭合关系及产生项均由动力学结构确定，而非现象学假定。模型通过最小耦合处方（minimal coupling prescription）从闵可夫斯基时空延拓至一般弯曲时空，并与爱因斯坦方程耦合。

Result: 证明了多原子RET框架下的动力学无干涉定理（no-go theorem）：任何由非负的相对论性单粒子分布函数诱导的应力-能量张量均满足强能量条件（strong energy condition）。在FLRW时空中，动力学压强修正了理想流体Euler情形下的膨胀动力学，但无干涉定理排除了单纯由RET₆气体驱动的加速。引入宇宙学常数后，ΛRET₆模型在晚期存在一个de Sitter吸引子（de Sitter attractor）并具有局部稳定性。数值积分表明，在物理合理的复合后初始条件和弛豫时间下，膨胀历史迅速趋近ΛCDM模型，非平衡修正量受弛豫时间和动力学压强初值控制。

Conclusion: 动力学压强的非平衡效应虽能修正宇宙膨胀，但无法独立驱动加速，必须引入宇宙学常数才能与观测相符；ΛRET₆模型为研究宇宙学中的非平衡修正提供了一个具有动力学基础的严格框架，且数值结果支持其在后期与ΛCDM模型高度一致。

Abstract: We formulate a generally covariant six-field Rational Extended Thermodynamics model (RET$_6$) for relativistic polyatomic gases, with the dynamical pressure as the only non-equilibrium variable. The model is based on a polyatomic extension of the Boltzmann-Chernikov kinetic equation, where the one-particle distribution depends also on an internal-energy variable, and on the Maximum Entropy closure of the associated relativistic moment hierarchy. The resulting field equations, closure relations, and production term are therefore fixed by the underlying kinetic structure rather than postulated phenomenologically. We extend the RET$_6$ model from Minkowski spacetime to a general curved spacetime by the minimal coupling prescription and couple it to the Einstein equations. As a first structural result, we prove a kinetic-theory no-go theorem in this polyatomic RET setting stating that any stress-energy tensor induced by a non-negative relativistic one-particle distribution function satisfies the strong energy condition. We then specialize the theory to a homogeneous and isotropic Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) spacetime. In this setting the dynamical pressure modifies the expansion dynamics with respect to the perfect-fluid Euler case, but the no-go theorem excludes acceleration driven by the RET$_6$ gas alone. Finally, we reintroduce a cosmological constant and study the combined $Λ$RET$_6$ model, proving the existence and local stability of a de Sitter attractor at late times. Numerical integrations show that, for physically motivated post-recombination initial data and relaxation times, the expansion history rapidly approaches that of $Λ$CDM, with small non-equilibrium corrections controlled by the relaxation time and by the initial value of the dynamical pressure.

### [54] [The gravitational-wave fingerprint of dynamically assembled primordial black hole cluster seeds in JWST's Little Red Dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09201)
*Juan Garcia-Bellido*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出，詹姆斯·韦伯太空望远镜（JWST）发现的“小红点”（Little Red Dots, LRDs）——超高红移（z≈5–9）处致密、红色、质量过大的吸积黑洞——可由量子色动力学（QCD）时期的原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBH）群自然形成。一个中等质量PBH核（10³–10⁵ M☉）被轻质量（~30 M☉）PBH群包围，通过气体动力学摩擦在10–50百万年内快速合并，产生极端质量比的引力波（gravitational wave, GW）信号，形成可探测的随机背景和环形“梳状”频谱特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JWST观测到的LRDs表现为红移z≈5–9、处于近化学原始宿主星系中的致密过量质量吸积黑洞，这与标准重种子模型（heavy-seed models）预测相矛盾，亟需新的理论解释。

Method: 该方法基于QCD时期热历史（QCD-epoch thermal history）预测的、具有宽质量函数（broad mass function）的强成团原初黑洞（PBH）群。模型构型为：一个中等质量PBH核（10³–10⁵ M☉）被数秒差距内约30 M☉的轻PBH群包围，并嵌入致密重子气体中；气体动力学摩擦（gas dynamical friction）使损失锥（loss cone）保持充盈，核心收缩，群聚PBH在10–50百万年内沉入并合并。

Result: 由于从一开始就存在重核（heavy nucleus），每次捕获的极端质量比（extreme mass ratio）q ≈ 10⁻⁴–10⁻²，使剩余体可抵抗引力反冲（gravitational recoil），且每次捕获在引力波（GW）辐射下到达最内稳定轨道，辐射约0.06 m c²能量，聚并效率ζ ≈ 0.06，与M_BH无关。叠加的群聚旋进场（swarm inspirals）形成随机背景Ω_GW h² ≈ 10⁻¹³–10⁻¹¹，呈Ω_GW ∝ f²/³形状，在气体退耦频率以下截断，顶部叠加环形“梳状”频谱（ringdown "comb"）：对10⁵ M☉核约13 mHz，对10³ M☉核约1.3 Hz（在z_f≈12处）。少数可比较质量的核-核并合（nucleus-nucleus coalescences）则是LISA/deci-Hz可单独分辨的源。

Conclusion: 检测并区分这些PBH群聚并特征与同等质量的直接形成PBH种子（directly formed PBH seed）的信号，可将LRDs识别为PBH核种子黑洞（PBH-nucleus seeded black holes），从而为JWST发现的早期过量质量黑洞提供全新形成机制。

Abstract: The James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) has revealed compact, red, overmassive accreting black holes - the so-called ``Little Red Dots'' (LRDs) - in chemically near-pristine hosts at $z\simeq5 - 9$, straining standard heavy-seed models. We show that a population of strongly clustered primordial black holes (PBH) with a broad mass function predicted by a QCD-epoch thermal history naturally realizes the configuration that assembles LRD-scale seeds: an intermediate-mass PBH \emph{nucleus} $M_{\rm BH}\sim10^3$-$10^5\,M_\odot$ surrounded, within a few parsecs, by a swarm of light ($m\sim30\,M_\odot$) PBHs embedded in dense baryonic gas. Gas dynamical friction keeps the loss cone full and lets the core contract, so the swarm sinks and is swallowed on $t_{\rm seed}\sim10$-50 Myr, well inside the cosmic time at $z\sim10$-$15$. Because a heavy nucleus is present \emph{ab initio}, the captures occur at extreme mass ratio $q\sim10^{-4}$-$10^{-2}$: the remnant is retained against gravitational recoil, and each capture reaches the innermost stable orbit under gravitational-wave (GW) emission, radiating $\simeq0.06\,m c^2$ so that the assembly efficiency is $ζ\simeq0.06$ independent of $M_{\rm BH}$. The superposed swarm inspirals form a stochastic background $Ω_{\rm GW} h^2\sim10^{-13}$-$10^{-11}$ with a $Ω_{\rm GW}\propto f^{2/3}$ shape truncated below the gas-decoupling frequency and topped by a ringdown ``comb'' at $f_{\rm ring}(M_{\rm BH})\simeq13$ mHz for $10^5\,M_\odot$ and $\simeq1.3$ Hz for $10^3\,M_\odot$ nuclei at $z_f\simeq12$. The few comparable-mass nucleus-nucleus coalescences are instead individually resolvable LISA/deci-Hz sources. Detection, and discrimination of these signatures from a directly formed PBH seed of the same mass, would identify the LRDs as PBH-nucleus seeded black holes.

### [55] [Eccentricity-Modulated Phase Degeneracy and Distinguishability between Dark Matter and Accretion Disk Environmental Effects in EMRIs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09214)
*Tan-hao Wu,Shu-jun Rong*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了极端质量比旋进（EMRIs）系统中暗物质晕与吸积盘之间的引力波相位简并性，发现两者引发的退相位对初始偏心率的依赖存在显著差异，且LISA能够分辨其波形差异，初始偏心率可作为辅助诊断参量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EMRIs对超大质量黑洞周围的弱环境效应极为敏感，但不同环境（如暗物质晕与吸积盘）对引力波相位的影响可能存在简并性（degeneracy），从而阻碍对环境的准确区分。本文旨在量化这种简并性，并探究能否通过偏心轨道特征实现区分。

Method: 采用NFW和Beta晕轮廓（halo profiles）建模暗物质环境，使用薄α盘（thin α-disk）模型描述吸积盘；通过依赖于偏心率的相位诊断量（eccentricity-dependent phase diagnostics）和LISA频段内的残余信噪比（residual signal-to-noise ratio）来量化两种环境的可区分性。

Result: 暗物质（DM）引发的退相位（dephasing）对初始偏心率e0的依赖性很弱，而吸积盘引发的退相位随e0增大而显著抑制。可区分时间（distinguishability time）在圆轨道时最长，在轻微偏心轨道上迅速缩短。对于所考虑的基准系统，LISA能够探测到DM与吸积盘之间的波形差异。

Conclusion: 初始偏心率e0可作为除观测时长之外的辅助诊断参量，用于区分EMRIs中暗物质晕与吸积盘的环境效应。

Abstract: Extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) are sensitive probes of weak environmental effects around massive black holes, since such effects can accumulate into observable gravitational-wave phase shifts. In this work, we study the phase degeneracy between dark matter halos and accretion disks in eccentric EMRI waveforms. We model the dark matter (DM) environment with NFW and Beta halo profiles, and describe the disk using a thin $α$-disk model. Their distinguishability is quantified through eccentricity-dependent phase diagnostics and residual signal-to-noise ratios in the LISA band. Our results show that DM-induced dephasing depends only weakly on the initial eccentricity $e_0$, whereas disk-induced dephasing is strongly suppressed as $e_0$ increases. The distinguishability time is longest for circular orbits and decreases rapidly for slightly eccentric orbits. For the benchmark systems considered here, the DM--disk waveform difference can be detectable by LISA, and $e_0$ can serve as an auxiliary diagnostic in addition to the observation duration.

### [56] [The significance of first post-adiabatic contributions for scalar charge measurements with intermediate and extreme mass ratio inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09310)
*Susanna Barsanti,Ollie Burke,Andrea Maselli,Thomas P. Sotiriou,Andrew Spiers,Niels Warburton*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个基于自力的、超越广义相对论（beyond-GR）的波形模型，该模型针对含额外标量场（scalar field）引力理论中的中等及极端质量比旋近系统（IMRI/EMRI），引入后绝热（post-adiabatic）轨道演化。研究发现，忽略引力部分的1PA效应会偏差双星内禀参数推断，而标量荷（scalar charge）测量对质量比变化鲁棒；但使用纯GR模板分析携带标量荷的信号会因未建模的关联产生显著偏差与低估的不确定性。此外，次级自旋在质量比≤10⁻⁴时无法被约束，且标量发射的低阶偶极近似引入的系统误差可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的引力波形模型主要基于广义相对论（general relativity, GR），但许多替代引力理论（如含标量场的理论）可能在中、极端质量比旋近（intermediate- and extreme-mass-ratio inspirals）中产生可观测效应。目前缺乏能在beyond-GR框架下同时考虑后绝热轨道演化和标量场效应的波形模型，亟需评估忽略这些效应时对LISA（Laser Interferometer Space Antenna）观测推断的影响。

Method: 针对非旋转主黑洞上的近圆旋近（quasi-circular inspiral）系统，将引力部分的一阶后绝热（first post-adiabatic, 1PA）演化与领先阶标量场效应相结合，构建了波形模型。采用贝叶斯注入-恢复（Bayesian injection-recovery）研究方法，评估波形系统误差（waveform systematics）对LISA标量荷推断的影响，并分析次级自旋（secondary spin）与标量荷之间的关联性。

Result: 忽略引力部分的1PA效应会导致双星内禀参数（intrinsic binary parameters）推断出现偏差，但标量荷测量在广泛质量比范围内保持鲁棒。使用纯GR模板分析携带标量荷的信号时，因未建模的标量荷与双星参数之间的关联，会产生显著偏差且不确定性被低估。次级自旋与标量荷之间无显著关联；当质量比低于10⁻⁴时，次级自旋本身在纯GR情形下也无法被约束。对标量发射采用领先阶偶极后牛顿（dipolar post-Newtonian）近似引入的系统误差与完全相对论性标量通量相比可忽略。

Conclusion: 构建了首个含后绝热轨道演化的beyond-GR波形模型，揭示了在LISA数据分析中忽略1PA引力效应或使用纯GR模板处理带标量荷信号均会带来系统性风险，而标量荷测量本身具有一定鲁棒性。同时澄清了关于次级自旋约束能力的先前争议，并证明了标量发射的低阶近似在准圆旋近场景下足够精确。

Abstract: We present the first self-force-based beyond-GR waveform model incorporating post-adiabatic orbital evolution for intermediate- and extreme-mass-ratio inspirals in theories of gravity with additional scalar fields. Focusing on quasi-circular inspirals into a non-spinning primary, we combine a first post-adiabatic (1PA) gravitational sector with leading-order scalar field effects and use Bayesian injection-recovery studies to assess the impact of waveform systematics on the inference of scalar charges with LISA. We find that neglecting 1PA effects in the gravitational sector can bias the inference of intrinsic binary parameters, while scalar-charge measurements remain robust across a wide range of mass ratios. In contrast, analysing signals from binaries in which the secondary carries a scalar charge using pure-GR templates leads to significant biases and underestimated uncertainties due to unmodelled correlations between the scalar charge and the binary parameters. We also investigate the role of secondary spin and find no significant correlation between the secondary spin and the scalar charge. Notably, up to a mass ratio of $10^{-4}$, the secondary spin itself remains unconstrained even in the pure-GR case, in contrast with previous claims in the literature. Finally, we show that modelling scalar emission with a leading-order dipolar post-Newtonian approximation -- for quasi-circular inspirals into a non-spinning primary -- introduces negligible systematic errors relative to fully relativistic scalar fluxes.

### [57] [Clock-noise subtraction in geometric time-delay interferometry for space-based gravitational-wave parameter estimation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09335)
*Rui Luo,Pan-Pan Wang,Zi-Jiang Yang,Wei-Liang Qian,Cheng-Gang Shao*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在几何时延干涉（geometric-TDI）框架下提出了一种时钟噪声（clock jitter）扣除方案，通过构造广义时钟噪声可观测量，使时钟噪声残差在代数上平行于激光噪声残差，从而实现对任意两条路径的几何TDI观测量的显式扣除。LISA-like轨道仿真表明，该方法能有效抑制时钟噪声，恢复灵敏度并改进参数估计精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 毫赫兹引力波观测需要时间延迟干涉（TDI，time-delay interferometry）可观测量将剩余仪器噪声控制在足够低的水平以支持探测和参数推断。尽管TDI能抑制不等臂和时变臂下的激光相位噪声，但来自星载超稳振荡器的时钟抖动（clock jitter）仍可能高于次级噪声本底，并偏置数据分析中使用的有效噪声加权，因此需要专门的时钟噪声扣除方案。

Method: 在几何TDI（geometric-TDI）框架内直接构建时钟噪声减法方案。该方法引入了针对四种时空链路结构（同时允许延迟算符和时间提前算符）的广义时钟噪声可观测量，使时钟噪声残差在代数上平行于激光噪声残差，从而为任意双路径几何TDI观测量提供显式扣除项。通过使用LISA-like轨道和噪声水平的时域仿真进行验证。

Result: 对于改进的第二代U型几何TDI组合，该减法方案将时钟噪声残差抑制到低于信号区域，恢复了对单色源（monochromatic source）的预期灵敏度，并改善了基于Fisher矩阵和马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov-chain Monte Carlo）对源振幅、频率和相位的参数约束。

Conclusion: 时钟噪声校准（clock-noise calibration）是未来天基引力波探测器精密数据分析中不可或缺的组成部分。

Abstract: Millihertz gravitational-wave observations with space-based interferometers require time-delay interferometry (TDI) observables whose residual instrumental noise is sufficiently controlled for both detection and parameter inference. Although TDI suppresses laser phase noise in unequal and time-dependent arms, clock jitter from onboard ultra-stable oscillators can remain above the secondary-noise floor and bias the effective noise weighting used in data analysis. We formulate a clock-noise subtraction scheme directly in the geometric-TDI framework. The construction introduces generalized clock-noise observables for the four space-time link structures that arise when both delay and time-advance operators are allowed. This makes the clock-noise residual algebraically parallel to the laser-noise residual and yields explicit subtraction terms for arbitrary two-path geometric TDI observables. We illustrate the method with representative first- and second-generation geometric TDI combinations, and test it with time-domain simulations using LISA-like orbits and noise levels. For a modified second-generation U-type observable, the subtraction suppresses the clock-noise residual below the signal region, restores the expected sensitivity to a monochromatic source, and improves the Fisher and Markov-chain Monte Carlo parameter constraints on the source amplitude, frequency and phase. These results show that clock-noise calibration is a necessary component of precision data analysis for future space-based gravitational-wave detectors.

</details>


### [58] [Head-on Collisions of Boson Stars with Bowen-York Type Initial Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09494)
*Jake Doherty,Pablo Laguna*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文采用基于Bowen-York方法的初始数据（initial data）对玻色子星（boson star）与黑洞的头对撞（head-on collision）进行数值相对论（numerical relativity）研究，验证了该初始数据方法的有效性，并发现玻色子星-玻色子星对撞比等效黑洞双星辐射更多引力波能量，而玻色子星-黑洞对撞则辐射更少。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bowen-York初始数据方法在黑洞双星模拟中已取得广泛应用，但尚未系统应用于玻色子星及其与黑洞的碰撞场景。本文旨在将该方法推广至玻色子星系统，以保留其简洁性并兼容早期后牛顿（post-Newtonian）旋近阶段的信息。

Method: 采用受Bowen-York初始数据方法启发的数值相对论方法，首先在有线性动量（linear momentum）的单玻色子星上进行验证，随后将其应用于玻色子星-玻色子星以及玻色子星-黑洞的头对撞模拟。

Result: 玻色子星头对撞在引力波（gravitational wave）中释放的能量高于等效黑洞双星；而玻色子星与黑洞的头对撞则比对应的黑洞-黑洞双星辐射更少的引力波能量。

Conclusion: 该初始数据方法能够有效模拟玻色子星碰撞过程，且结果与已有研究一致，表明该方法在暗物质候选体（如玻色子星）与致密天体交互的引力波研究中有应用潜力。

Abstract: We present a numerical relativity study of head-on collisions involving boson stars using initial data inspired by the Bowen-York initial data used to model black hole binaries with punctures. The initial data method preserves the simplicity of the Bowen-York approach, thus allowing incorporating information from the early, post-Newtonian inspiral phase in binary coalescences. We test the method on a single boson star with linear momentum. We present results from head-on collisions of boson stars as well as encounters of boson stars with black holes. In general, the results are consistent with previous studies, demonstrating the effectiveness of the initial data method. In particular, we show that boson star head-on collisions emit more energy in gravitational waves than the equivalent black hole binaries. On the other hand, head-on collisions of a boson star with a black hole radiate less than their black hole binary counterparts.

</details>


### [59] [Causal Space-Time Structure and non-Hausdorff Extension of Schwarzschild Black Hole Interior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09506)
*Asya Aynbund,V. V. Kiselev*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为严格构造黑洞视界下的未来与过去光锥，并解决测地线运动中的闭合类时圈问题，同时揭示黑洞内部结构的拓扑与热力学性质。

Method: 通过对黑洞外部因果连通时空区域延续的测地线进行完备化（completion of geodesics），严格构造未来与过去光锥；将施瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）处理为赖斯纳-诺德斯特罗姆黑洞（Reissner–Nordstrøm black hole）的零电荷极限，从而将彭罗斯-卡特图（Penrose–Carter diagram）重构为无限带状结构。

Result: 无限带状结构排除了测地线运动下的闭合类时圈；未来与过去光锥之间的边际轨迹构成了黑洞内部紧致非豪斯多夫球面扩展（compact non-Hausdorff spherical extension）的公共路径，该扩展形成了坠入黑洞粒子的热浴（thermal bath）。

Conclusion: 施瓦西黑洞的零电荷极限方法有效重构了时空图拓扑，排除了闭合类时圈，并揭示了黑洞内部非豪斯多夫结构与热浴的关联。

Abstract: Cones of future and past are rigorously constructed under the horizon of black hole by completions of geodesics continued from causally connected space-time regions outside the black hole interior. Treating the Schwarzschild black hole as a zero charge limit of Reissner--Nordsrøm black hole reforms the Penrose--Carter diagram into the infinite band that excludes the closed proper-time cycles under the geodesic motion. The marginal trajectories between the cones of future and past compose paths common with a compact non-Hausdorff spherical extension of black hole interior forming the thermal bath for particles fallen to the black hole.

### [60] [Periodic line-of-sight velocity-driven modulations to gravitational waves emitted by compact binaries in Keplerian outer orbits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09644)
*Avinash Tiwari,Shasvath J. Kapadia,Aditya Vijaykumar,Sourav Chatterjee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文推导了由超大质量黑洞附近或致密星团环境中双致密星并合（CBC）质心（CoM）受周期性非相对论视线速度（LOS velocity）影响而产生的引力波（GW）波形相位和振幅修正，揭示了这些修正出现在4后牛顿（PN）阶，并通过Fisher矩阵分析证明，相较于恒定运动学参数的近似方法，基于本文波形的环境约束精度显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究仅考虑恒定视线加速度及其高阶时间导数对引力波波形的修正，但这些修正基于“观测时长远小于外轨道周期”的近似条件，该条件并非总是成立。因此需要推导更一般的周期性视线速度情形下的波形修正。

Method: 针对双致密星并合质心在圆形或偏心外轨道上的周期性非相对论视线速度，推导出引力波波形的相位和振幅解析修正；采用Fisher矩阵分析（Fisher matrix analysis）预测未来地面和空间引力波探测器对致密环境参数的约束能力。

Result: 周期性视线速度引起的相位和振幅调制出现在4后牛顿（post-Newtonian, PN）阶；在观测时长远小于外轨道周期的极限下，该结果可退化到已知的恒定运动学参数修正。基于本文波形的环境约束效果显著优于基于恒定运动学参数近似方法的约束效果。

Conclusion: 本文推导的周期性视线速度波形修正更普遍地适用于多种天体物理环境（如超大质量黑洞附近或致密星团），且能显著提升未来引力波探测器对相关环境参数的约束精度。

Abstract: The centre of mass (CoM) of compact binary coalescences (CBCs) occurring in the vicinity of a supermassive black hole, through interaction with an arbitrary third body (e.g., of stellar mass), or in a dense stellar environment, will undergo a time-varying line-of-sight (LOS) velocity. This in turn leads to a time-varying Doppler shift and corresponding modulations in the shape of the gravitational waves (GWs). The phase and amplitude corrections arising from constant LOS acceleration and its higher-order time derivatives are already known. Specifically, these effects lead to corrections to the GW waveform at $-4n$ post-Newtonian (PN) order, where $n$ is the $n^{th}$ time derivative of the LOS velocity. In the context of a circular or eccentric outer orbit of the CoM of the CBC, these effects can be thought of as approximations to the LOS velocity in the limit: observation duration $\ll$ period of the outer orbit. However, this condition is not necessarily always satisfied. In this {\it paper}, we present phase and amplitude corrections to the GW waveforms arising from a periodic non-relativistic LOS velocity for circular and eccentric outer orbits of the CBC's CoM. Specifically, these lead to phase and amplitude modulations at 4 PN order, and reduce to the known corrections for constant kinematic parameters under appropriate limits mentioned above. We also perform a Fisher matrix analysis to forecast constraints on the environment that is sourcing the time-varying LOS velocity, for various future ground and space-based detectors. We further show that constraints acquired using GW waveforms derived in this work improve significantly in comparison to those acquired from approximate methods valid for constant kinematic parameters.

Abstract: We consider quasi-one-dimensional (Q1D) continuous waves (CWs) in the two-dimensional (2D) optical system with the cubic-quintic nonlinearity and a Q1D potential trough. In the case of a smooth trough profile, we confirm the known modulational instability (MI) of Q1D CWs with the transverse structure corresponding to the 1D ground state (GS) in the potential trough, and demonstrate the MI of CWs with the dipole-mode (DM) transverse structure, corresponding to the lowest 1D excited state in the potential trough. The CWs of both GS and DM types remain nearly stable close to the edges of their existence regions. Stable stationary states in the form of periodic chains of 2D solitons, trapped in the potential trough, are produced in a numerical form. The dynamics of the soliton chains excited by a localized kick is studied too. For the potential trough with the singular delta-functional profile, we find two species of exact analytical solutions for CWs, one of which is completely stable.

### [62] [A Formalization of the Mean-Field Derivation of the Vlasov Equation: AI-Assisted Lean Formalization as a Strategy Game](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08986)
*Joseph K. Miller*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过数学家指导AI系统，在Lean 4证明助手中将非线性Vlasov方程的LaTeX文档完整形式化为可编译、无漏洞（sorry）、仅依赖Lean公理的自包含数学层，并将这一过程形式化为“形式化游戏”（formalization game）。人类负责定义、分解与排错，AI执行证明，约一个月完成全部开发，其中约六分之一的代码（最优输运相关）可作为独立层并入Mathlib。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索人类数学家与AI系统协作形式化数学证明的新范式，提出“形式化游戏”框架以系统化描述该过程，并通过具体案例验证其可行性。

Method: 提出形式化游戏（formalization game）框架：目标是将LaTeX文档转化为Lean 4代码，获胜条件是代码编译通过、不含sorry、且目标定理仅依赖Lean基本公理。定义“可重用性（reuse）”作为第二重检验标准。人类负责界定定义（scope the definitions）、引导分解（steer the decompositions）和排解库缺口（triage the library’s gaps），AI代理（AI agent）负责执行证明。

Result: 完整形式化了非线性Vlasov方程通过Dobrushin平均场路径的适定性（well-posedness），包括存在性、唯一性、稳定性估计、平均场极限及短时间叠加原理（weak solutions are Lagrangian）。约49 of 299个声明（约六分之一）构成自包含的最优输运层（optimal-transport layer），仅依赖Mathlib，通过22个声明的接口实现无反向依赖。标题定理约一周完成，全部开发约一个月。

Conclusion: 该方法成功验证了人类指导+AI执行的协作模式在形式化复杂数学定理中的有效性。形式化游戏框架独立于具体工具，具有长期方法论意义。形式化保证了每个陈述的证明正确性，但陈述是否对应于预期定理仍属于数学家的判断。

Abstract: We formalize a research result in the Lean 4 proof assistant by having a mathematician direct an AI system, and frame the activity as a formalization game. The objective is to turn a LaTeX document into Lean. The game is won when the development compiles, contains no sorry, and a machine check shows the target theorems rest on Lean's foundational axioms alone. Reuse is a second check, by a definition we introduce: whether the development yields a self-contained layer of general mathematics the wider library could absorb. The case study is a complete, axiom-clean formalization of well-posedness for the nonlinear Vlasov equation via Dobrushin's mean-field route -- existence, uniqueness, the stability estimate and mean-field limit, and a short-window superposition principle (weak solutions are Lagrangian). The human's role was to direct, not to write proofs: to scope the definitions, steer the decompositions, and triage the library's gaps; the AI agent executed. The formalization certifies the proof of each statement as written; whether the written statement is the intended theorem stays the mathematician's judgment. The optimal-transport machinery that fell out of the build (in particular, properties of the Wasserstein-1 metric and the Kantorovich-Rubinstein duality theorem) separates into a self-contained layer that compiles against Mathlib alone: about a sixth of the development (49 of 299 declarations), behind a 22-declaration interface with no reverse dependency. The headline theorems ran in about a week, the full development in about a month. We report the quantitative claims as observations of one game, not as general laws. The game's rules name no particular system, so the methodological framing is meant to outlast the tools of any one run.

</details>

*Izumi Takahara,Teruyasu Mizoguchi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的大语言模型智能体虽具备广泛知识、灵活推理与工具使用能力，能够自主提出假设、测试并修正信念，但这些过程被埋藏在非结构化日志中，缺乏让智能体或人类研究者进行审计（audit）的机制，限制了其作为可靠科学发现工具的可用性与可验证性。

Method: 提出假设演化协议（HEP），一种智能体绑定框架（agent harness），将假设生成（hypothesis generation）、评估（evaluation）与演化（evolution）设计为显式、可审计的操作。该方法将假设-测试-证据-信念（hypothesis-test-evidence-belief）循环作为结构化流程嵌入智能体行为中。

Conclusion: 该结果表明朝向可审计的人工智能科学家（auditable AI scientists）迈出了重要一步，其科学推理过程可被检查、验证并作为后续研究的构建基础。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents are increasingly expected to play a central role in AI-driven scientific discovery. Equipped with broad knowledge, flexible reasoning, and tool use, they have the potential to autonomously explore and solve scientific problems by repeatedly proposing hypotheses, testing them, and revising their beliefs in the light of the evidence. In current agents, however, these hypotheses, tests, and belief updates are buried in unstructured logs, and no mechanism lets the agent or the human researcher audit that process. Here we propose the Hypothesis Evolution Protocol (HEP), an agent harness that provides hypothesis generation, evaluation, and evolution as explicit, auditable operations. On materials-science research tasks, a HEP-equipped agent operates the hypothesis--test--evidence--belief cycle that planning-style agents lack, generalizes across research questions, and exploits the protocol more fully as the base LLM becomes more capable. These results mark a step toward auditable AI scientists, whose scientific reasoning can be inspected, verified, and built upon.

### [64] [Asymptotic stability of solutions to the good Boussinesq equation in dispersive wave region](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09050)
*Yingmin Yang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究 good Boussinesq 方程在色散波区域解的渐近稳定性，利用 Dbar-最速下降法处理 Riemann-Hilbert 问题，获得了直到 $\mathcal{O}(t^{-3/4})$ 阶最优误差的长时渐近展开，并将初始数据从快速衰减的 Schwartz 空间推广到加权 Sobolev 空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对 good Boussinesq 方程长时渐近行为的分析多限于快速衰减的 Schwartz 空间中的初始数据，而更一般加权 Sobolev 空间下的长时行为尚不清楚。因此，本文旨在将该方程的长时渐近分析推广到更广泛的初始数据空间，并证明色散波区域中解的渐近稳定性。

Method: 将 good Boussinesq 方程的解与一个 Riemann-Hilbert 问题（Riemann-Hilbert problem）相关联，然后应用 Dbar-最速下降法（Dbar-steepest descent method）对该问题进行分析，从而推导解的长时渐近行为。

Result: 获得了 good Boussinesq 方程解的长时渐近展开，其误差阶达到最优的 $\mathcal{O}(t^{-3/4})$。将初始数据条件从快速衰减的 Schwartz 空间推广到了加权 Sobolev 空间（weighted Sobolev space），并在色散波区域（dispersive wave region）证明了解的渐近稳定性（asymptotic stability）。

Conclusion: 本文成功将 good Boussinesq 方程的长时渐近分析从较窄的 Schwartz 空间推广到更一般的加权 Sobolev 空间，并在色散波区域建立了解的渐近稳定性。所用 Dbar-最速下降法给出的最优误差阶 $\mathcal{O}(t^{-3/4})$ 也验证了该方法的有效性。

Abstract: This work studies the asymptotic stability of solutions to the good Boussinesq equation in dispersive wave region when the reflection coefficients associated with the initial data belong to weighted Sobolev space. The Dbar-steepest descent method is applied to the Riemann-Hilbert problem and the long-time asymptotic expansion of the solution are obtained up to an optimal error of order $\mathcal{O}(t^{-3/4})$. Compared with previous results, we extend the initial data from the rapidly decaying Schwartz space to a weighted Sobolev space, and prove the asymptotic stability of the solution in dispersive wave region.

### [65] [TokaGrad: End-to-end differentiable tokamak simulator for L-to-H full scenario optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09088)
*Jaemin Seo*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出 TokaGrad——首个端到端可微分的托卡马克输运模拟器，能够自洽地建模包含爬升、L模运行和H模接入的全放电场景。通过将整个模拟流程构建为可微分的计算图（computational graph），TokaGrad 允许基于梯度的优化器直接利用模拟器内部灵敏度进行反应堆设计优化、执行器控制与波形优化，从而替代传统的黑箱试错方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚变能研究正从理论可行性走向商业化，亟需高效的反应堆概念设计、托卡马克自主控制和高性能场景优化方法；传统依赖黑箱实验或仿真的试错法（trial-and-error）及暴力参数搜索成本高昂，亟需更高效的优化范式。

Method: TokaGrad 基于可微分编程（differentiable programming）框架，将整个模拟管线表示为互联的计算图（computational graph），其中机器参数、执行器波形和等离子体响应通过可微分操作链接。该模拟器自洽集成了等离子体平衡、输运、加热、L-H跃迁（L-H transition）和台基（pedestal）形成的可微分模型，可实现全场景动态建模。

Result: TokaGrad 成功实现了对爬升、L模运行和H模接入等全放电场景的端到端可微分建模。当其与基于梯度的优化器耦合时，能够有效支持反应堆设计优化、执行器控制以及全场景波形优化（full-scenario waveform optimization）。

Conclusion: TokaGrad 框架为燃烧等离子体场景和反应堆概念的自动化、可微分优化提供了一条可行路径，有望改变传统数值模拟与优化范式。

Abstract: As fusion energy moves from theoretical feasibility toward commercialization, design of new reactor concepts, autonomous tokamak control, and high-performance scenario optimization are becoming increasingly important. Traditionally, such optimization tasks have relied on costly trial-and-error or brute-force parameter searches, based on black-box experiments or simulations. Recently, advances in differentiable programming are changing the paradigm of numerical simulation. Unlike conventional simulations, which are typically executed as locally connected step-by-step procedures, differentiable simulation represents the entire simulation pipeline as a connected computational graph. In such a framework, machine parameters, actuator waveforms, and plasma responses are linked through differentiable operations, allowing Jacobians to propagate across the full simulation. This enables direct gradient-based control and optimization using the internal sensitivities of the simulator, rather than treating the simulator as a black box. Here, we present TokaGrad, an end-to-end differentiable tokamak transport simulator for full-scenario modeling, including ramp-up, L-mode operation, and H-mode access. TokaGrad self-consistently integrates differentiable models for plasma equilibrium, transport, heating, L-H transition, and pedestal formation. To our knowledge, this is the first differentiable tokamak simulator capable of self-consistently modeling dynamic full-discharge scenarios where actuators and plasma evolve together with equilibrium, pedestal, and confinement-regime transitions. We demonstrate that, when coupled to gradient-based optimizers, TokaGrad enables reactor-design optimization, actuator control, and full-scenario waveform optimization. This framework provides a pathway toward automated, differentiable optimization of burning-plasma scenarios and reactor concepts.

</details>


### [66] [Entanglement entropy of ground states of the Landau Hamiltonian on the half-plane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09467)
*Paul Pfeiffer,Wolfgang Spitzer*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究边界条件下Landau哈密顿量基态纠缠熵的面积律行为，发现即使谱性质从纯点谱变为绝对连续谱，基态纠缠熵仍保持严格面积律，并提出了绝对连续谱需满足何种条件才能导致对数修正面积律的开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究边界条件对基态纠缠熵（entanglement entropy, EE）标度行为的影响，特别关注当哈密顿量谱性质发生剧烈变化时（从纯点谱变为绝对连续谱），纠缠熵是否仍满足面积律（area law）。

Method: 通过对比全平面与半平面上的Landau哈密顿量（Landau Hamiltonian）的谱性质与基态纠缠熵行为；全平面上Landau哈密顿量具有纯点谱（pure point spectrum），半平面上则具有纯绝对连续谱（purely absolutely continuous spectrum），在此基础上分别分析两类情况下基态纠缠熵的标度律。

Result: 全平面上Landau哈密顿量的基态纠缠熵满足严格面积律（strict area law）；半平面上尽管谱性质转变为纯绝对连续谱，基态纠缠熵仍然保持严格面积律，并未出现对数增强行为。

Conclusion: 边界条件可剧烈改变哈密顿量的谱结构与谱类型，但对基态纠缠熵的前导项（leading behaviour）影响有限；提出需进一步研究绝对连续谱满足何种额外或更精细的条件才能导致类似Laplace算子情况下的对数增强面积律（logarithmically enhanced area-law）。

Abstract: We study the entanglement entropy (EE) of ground states of a Hamiltonian defined on a domain with a boundary. Surprisingly, boundary conditions can change the spectrum and the nature of the spectrum drastically but not the leading behaviour of the EE. As is well-known, the Landau Hamiltonian on the full plane has pure point spectrum (the infinitely degenerate Landau levels) and ground states display a so-called strict area law. On the other hand, the Landau Hamiltonian on the half-plane has purely absolutely continuous spectrum and yet we prove a strict area law for its ground states. We raise the question of what extra or finer conditions on the absolutely continuous spectrum are necessary to guarantee a logarithmically enhanced area-law as we have for the Laplace operator.

</details>


### [67] [Extended group analysis and conservation laws of a class of variable coefficient generalized Kawahara equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09482)
*Olena Vaneeva,Alexander Zhalij,Olena Magda,Oksana Brahinets*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文对一类含时系数广义Kawahara方程进行了系统的群分析，包括李对称性（Lie symmetries）的完全分类、李约化（Lie reductions）、精确解构造以及低阶局部守恒律（local conservation laws）的分类，并通过收缩（contractions）研究建立了不同对称性扩展情形之间的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用群分析方法，系统描述了方程的可容许变换（admissible transformations）、等价变换（equivalence transformations）和李对称变换（Lie symmetry transformations）；在不借助等价变换简化系数的情况下完成了完整的李对称性分类（Lie symmetry classification）；通过李约化（Lie reductions）构造精确解；对低阶局部守恒律进行分类。

Result: 完整给出了该类方程的李对称性分类；构造了若干李精确解；分类了低阶局部守恒律，发现该类方程均具有质量守恒律和质量范数（$L^2$-norm）守恒律，而能量型守恒律仅存在于与对称性分类所区分情形一致的特定系数分支中；通过收缩研究将李对称扩展情形、约化及守恒律联系起来。

Conclusion: 本文通过群分析手段为含时系数广义Kawahara方程提供了完整的对称性、解和守恒律分类框架，收缩分析进一步揭示了不同情形之间的内在联系，为后续理论研究和实际应用奠定了基础。

Abstract: We review and extend the results on the group analysis of a class of generalized Kawahara equations with time-dependent coefficients. First, we provide an overview of the existing literature on Lie symmetries and Lie-invariant solutions of such equations. We then present a complete description of the transformation properties of these equations, including admissible, equivalence, and Lie symmetry transformations. For practical applications, the results are further extended by presenting a complete Lie symmetry classification without simplifying the coefficients by equivalence transformations. The Lie reductions are then thoroughly performed and some Lie exact solutions are constructed. The local conservation laws of low order are classified: every equation from the class admits the mass and the $L^2$-norm conservation laws, whereas energy-type conservation laws exist only for distinguished coefficient branches that agree with the cases singled out by the symmetry classification. The classification results are enhanced by a study of contractions, which link cases of Lie symmetry extensions together with the associated reductions and conservation laws.

### [68] [Energy, time, and position resolution measurements of an array of large tapered LYSO crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09226)

Method: 使用放射性源测量六块定制锥形LYSO晶体的纵向响应均匀性；随后在保罗·谢勒研究所（Paul Scherrer Institute）利用20至80 MeV正电子束对晶体阵列的能量分辨率和时间分辨率进行表征；空间分辨率通过实验测量结合Geant4模拟进行外推。

Abstract: We report on the performance of six custom-made tapered LYSO crystals of unprecedented volume, which constitute a sector of the 19 radiation length electromagnetic calorimeter planned for the PIONEER experiment. The longitudinal response uniformity of each crystal was measured using radioactive sources before characterizing the energy and time resolution of the crystals in an array using a 20 to 80 MeV positron beam at the Paul Scherrer Institute. The array demonstrated an energy resolution better than 2 % for energies above 40 MeV and a time resolution better than 130 ps for energies above 30 MeV. The spatial resolution was measured in the central region of the array to be 4.9 mm at 70 MeV, and was extrapolated to 5.4 mm across a 30 mm radius region using Geant4 simulation. The measured properties satisfy the key design parameters of the PIONEER calorimeter for the measurement of rare pion decays.

### [69] [Quantum Oscillation Signatures of $\mathbb{Z}_2$ Monopole Charge in Nodal-Ring Semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08825)
*Aravind Karthigeyan,Yoonseok Hwang,Bohm-Jung Yang,Junyeong Ahn*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出利用磁量子振荡（magnetic quantum oscillations）直接探测拓扑节线半金属（nodal-line semimetals）中节线环（nodal rings）的次级拓扑电荷——$\mathbb{Z}_2$单极电荷（$\mathbb{Z}_2$ monopole charge）$w_2$，该电荷通常难以被标准探针测量。研究发现，沿环轴方向的磁场可诱导出由$w_2$决定的拓扑相移，而垂直方向的磁场则仅反映贝里相位（Berry phase）$w_1\pi$。三维ABC堆叠石墨二炔（graphdiyne）被预测可在现有高磁场设施下观测到该振荡信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑半金属（topological semimetals）中的能带节点（band nodes）由量子化不变量（quantized invariants）表征，其中部分不变量（如次级拓扑电荷（secondary topological charges））无法被标准探测手段揭示，其输运特性尚待探索。本文旨在寻找一种实验上可操作的探针来诊断这类隐藏的拓扑电荷。

Method: 研究聚焦于三维节线半金属，其中节线环同时携带贝里相位（Berry phase）$w_1\pi$和$\mathbb{Z}_2$单极电荷（$\mathbb{Z}_2$ monopole charge）$w_2$。通过分析不同磁场方向下环形费米面（toroidal Fermi surface）的极值轨道（extremal orbits）的磁量子振荡行为，分别提取$w_1$和$w_2$对应的相位信息。

Result: 当磁场沿环轴方向时，环形费米面的内外极值轨道均环绕$w_2$强制的螺纹（thread），在第$\nu$次谐波中产生拓扑相移（topological phase shift）$\nu w_2\pi$。当磁场垂直于环轴时，极值轨道仅呈现出贝里相位$w_1\pi$决定的$\pi$相移，与$w_2$无关。弱掺杂下的三维ABC堆叠石墨二炔被预测可在现有高磁场设施范围内观测到该振荡。

Conclusion: 磁量子振荡可同时诊断节线环的两种拓扑电荷（$w_1$和$w_2$），且信号由磁场方向选择性激发。该发现为探测拓扑半金属中隐藏的次级拓扑不变量提供了一种可行的实验方案。

Abstract: Topological semimetals host band nodes characterized by quantized invariants that can appear in bulk responses, yet some invariants remain hidden from standard probes. In particular, band nodes can carry secondary topological charges whose transport signatures are still largely unexplored. Here we study three-dimensional nodal-line semimetals in which nodal rings carry both the Berry phase $w_1π$ and a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ monopole charge $w_2$. We show that magnetic quantum oscillations, usually treated as a probe of $w_1$, can directly diagnose $w_2$, with the relevant signal selected by the magnetic-field direction. For a field along the ring axis, the inner and outer extremal orbits of the toroidal Fermi surface both encircle the $w_2$-enforced thread and exhibit a topological phase shift $νw_2π$ in the $ν$th harmonic, which is accessible through standard phase-resolved quantum-oscillation analysis. By contrast, for a field applied perpendicular to the ring axis, the relevant extremal orbit exhibits the usual $π$ phase shift associated with the Berry phase $w_1π$, independent of $w_2$. For weak doping, three-dimensional ABC-stacked graphdiyne is predicted to exhibit the proposed oscillations in a field range accessible with present-day high-field facilities.

### [70] [Fermion-mediated Casimir effect on mesoscopic rings implementing non-Clifford SWAP$^α$ gates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08840)
*Liang Du,Qing-Dong Jiang,Yijia Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出在介观环（mesoscopic rings）中，通过阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆效应（Aharonov-Bohm effect）可原位调控费米子介导的卡西米尔相互作用（Casimir interaction）的强度与符号，进而实现远程非克利福德量子门，降低自旋量子比特架构中通用量子计算与纠错的资源开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统卡西米尔效应由材料本征属性决定，缺乏原位可调性（in situ tunability），限制了其在量子调控中的应用。

Method: 在介观环体系中利用阿哈罗诺夫-玻姆效应（Aharonov-Bohm effect）产生的相位，调控费米子介导的卡西米尔相互作用（Casimir interaction）的强度与符号。

Result: 实现了对卡西米尔相互作用幅度与符号的原位调控，该机制能够在空间分离的自旋量子比特（spin qubits）之间实现非克利福德 SWAP^α 门（non-Clifford SWAP^α gate）。

Conclusion: 该机制为工程化长程相互作用（long-range interactions）提供了新途径，有助于降低自旋量子比特架构中通用量子计算与量子纠错（quantum error correction）的额外开销。

Abstract: The Casimir effect is typically governed by intrinsic material properties and lacks in situ tunability. We show that, in mesoscopic rings, both the magnitude and sign of the fermion-mediated Casimir interaction can be controlled via the Aharonov-Bohm effect. The resulting interplay between the Aharonov-Bohm phase and the Casimir interaction provides a route to engineer long-range interactions. In particular, this mechanism enables the implementation of non-Clifford SWAP$^α$ gates between spatially separated spin qubits, thereby reducing the overhead for universal quantum computation and quantum error correction in spin-qubit architectures.
