### [71] [Probing Cooper pair momentum by quasiparticle steering with planar Josephson junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08845)
*Isidora Araya Day,Anton R. Akhmerov,Antonio R. L. Manesco*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和理论证明，在弹道平面约瑟夫森结（ballistic planar Josephson junctions）中，安德烈夫束缚态（Andreev bound states）会以相位控制的角度喷射到相邻的正常区域，该角度标度律为 Θ ∼ √(Δ/μ)，显著大于传统的库珀对动量标度 Δ/μ，从而提供了一种通过动量空间偏转来探测凝聚体动量传递的新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导体中的库珀对动量（Cooper pair momentum）通常远小于费米动量（Fermi momentum），导致其难以直接测量。尽管约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）能产生较大的相位梯度（phase gradient）并通过安德烈夫反射（Andreev reflection）将库珀对动量传递给准粒子，但当前缺乏一种显著且可相控的探测手段。

Method: 本文基于弹道平面约瑟夫森结，研究了安德烈夫束缚态沿结传播并喷射进入相邻正常区域的行为，分析了喷射角度与超导能隙（Δ）和化学势（μ）之间的标度关系 Θ ∼ √(Δ/μ)。

Result: 研究发现喷射角度由相位控制，其标度律为 Θ ∼ √(Δ/μ)，这一角度在参数上远超传统的库珀对动量标度 Δ/μ；即使在安德烈夫近似（Andreev approximation）条件 Δ/μ ≪ 1 下，该现象仍然显著可测。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了相位控制准粒子喷射（phase-controlled quasiparticle ejection）作为凝聚体动量传递的运动学探针（kinematic probe）：与现有探测多普勒能移（Doppler energy shift）的方法不同，该信号表现为喷射准粒子的动量空间偏转（momentum-space deflection）。

Abstract: The Cooper pair momentum in a superconductor is associated with a phase gradient of the superconducting order parameter. In general, this momentum is small compared to the Fermi momentum, which makes it challenging to measure. Josephson junctions, however, enable the creation of large phase gradients and transfer of the Cooper pair momentum to quasiparticles via Andreev reflection. In this work we demonstrate that Andreev bound states propagating along ballistic planar Josephson junctions eject into an adjacent normal region at a phase-controlled angle that scales as $Θ\sim \sqrt{Δ/ μ}$, where $Δ$ is the superconducting gap and $μ$ is the chemical potential. This angle parametrically exceeds the conventional Cooper pair momentum scale $Δ/ μ$, and thus this phenomenon is sizeable even within the Andreev approximation regime $Δ/ μ\ll 1$. Our results establish phase-controlled quasiparticle ejection as a kinematic probe of condensate momentum transfer: unlike existing probes that detect the Doppler energy shift, the signal appears as a momentum-space deflection of emitted quasiparticles.

</details>


### [72] [A new perspective on the anomalous Hall effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09019)
*Jason G. Kattan,Matthew Albert,J. E. Sipe*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文基于微观极化（polarization）、磁化（magnetization）及自由电荷与电流的概念，重新审视了磁性导体中的反常霍尔效应（anomalous Hall effect）及其在有限频率下的推广。利用二次量子化场论（second-quantized field theory）处理电子自由度，将电导率张量（conductivity tensor）分解为Kubo项、金属Drude项和反常霍尔电导率三项，并对体心立方铁进行了数值计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论对磁性导体中反常霍尔效应的微观图像尚不完整，尤其在有限频率（finite frequency）响应下的推广缺乏基于极化、磁化与自由电荷-电流等微观概念的统一形式化处理。

Method: 采用二次量子化场论，在哈密顿量中引入静态且晶胞周期性的磁场以编码晶体中的磁序并破缺时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）。在微观层面上研究束缚与自由载流子对空间均匀的有限频率电场的动力学响应，推导长波极限下的电导率张量。

Result: 电导率张量由三项组成：与极化响应相关的Kubo项、与自由电流响应纵向部分对应的金属Drude项（metallic Drude term）、以及与自由电流响应横向部分对应的反常霍尔电导率（anomalous Hall conductivity）。此外，对铁磁体心立方相铁给出了各项的数值计算结果。

Conclusion: 该形式化框架为理解磁性导体中反常霍尔效应的微观机制及其频率依赖性提供了统一视角，数值结果验证了理论对铁磁铁等实际材料的适用性。

Abstract: We revisit the anomalous Hall effect in magnetic conductors, and its generalization to finite frequencies, using a formalism based on microscopic notions of polarization, magnetization, and free charges and currents. The electronic degrees of freedom are treated within second-quantized field theory, where the Hamiltonian features a static and cell-periodic magnetic field that encodes the magnetic order in the crystal and breaks time-reversal symmetry. We study the dynamics of bound and free charge carriers at the microscopic level as they respond to a spatially uniform electric field at finite frequency. The conductivity tensor describing the long-wavelength response is a sum of three terms, including a Kubo term associated with the polarization response, along with the metallic Drude term and the anomalous Hall conductivity that are associated with the longitudinal and transverse parts of the free current response, respectively. We also present numerical calculations of these contributions for the ferromagnetic body-centered cubic phase of iron.

</details>


### [73] [Negligible current-induced torque from the bulk and interface of Al](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09055)
*Taiyang Zhang,Lujun Zhu,Zhihao Yan,Lijun Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 实验发现轻金属Al的体相和界面均未对相邻Co和FePt层产生可检测的扭矩，表明Al中的轨道-自旋转换极小，轨道霍尔效应、界面轨道Rashba效应和自旋-涡度耦合的扭矩贡献缺乏普适性和有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轻金属Al被理论预测具有显著的轨道霍尔效应（orbital Hall effect）和轨道Rashba效应（orbital Rashba effect），但缺乏实验证据验证这些效应对相邻铁磁层的实际扭矩贡献。

Method: 制备Co/Al、Al/Co和Al/FePt双层薄膜，利用自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect）、自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）以及电阻率失配（resistivity mismatch）条件，实验测量Al的体相和界面对相邻磁性层产生的扭矩。

Result: Al的体相和界面均未对相邻Co和FePt层产生可检测的扭矩；Al中的轨道-自旋转换极弱，轨道输运（orbital transport）和自旋-涡度扭矩（spin-vorticity torque）在Co/Al、Al/Co和Al/FePt双层中均可忽略。

Conclusion: 轨道霍尔效应、界面轨道Rashba效应和自旋-涡度耦合的扭矩贡献缺乏普适性和/或有效性，实验对理论预测提出了重要质疑。

Abstract: The light metal Al was predicted to have strong orbital Hall and Rashba effects from its bulk and interface, respectively. In this letter, we report experimental evidence that neither the bulk nor the interface of the Al contributed a detectable torque on adjacent Co and FePt layers with significant spin Hall effect, spin-orbit coupling, and resistivity mismatch with Al. These results suggest minimal orbital-spin conversion in Al and negligible orbital transport and spin-vorticity torque in Co/Al, Al/Co, and Al/FePt bilayers. Our findings suggest poor generality and/or effectiveness of torque contributions by the orbital Hall effect, the interfacial orbital Rashba effect, and the spin-vorticity coupling.

</details>


### [74] [Quantum Hopfion rings in the cluster mean-field approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09140)
*Vladyslav M. Kuchkin,Thomas L. Schmidt*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究在团簇平均场近似（CMFA）框架下，结合对称化处理与密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）方法，实现了对二维和三维自旋纹理（$k\pi$-斯格明子与hopfion环）中量子涨落的精确计算，揭示了经典微磁模型的局限性，并验证了正则化微磁方程作为改进框架的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有标准方法受限于维度诅咒（curse of dimensionality）且通常只能处理基态性质，难以准确计算大尺寸自旋纹理（spin textures）中的量子涨落以及可靠地访问亚稳态（metastable states）。

Method: 将团簇平均场近似（cluster mean-field approximation, CMFA）与对称化过程（symmetrization procedure）相结合；利用磁构型的柱对称性（cylindrical symmetry）构造一维链状团簇，使用密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法高效模拟团簇内部，团簇间相互作用则在平均场（mean-field）层次处理。

Result: 获得了hopfion环中磁化强度长度局部涨落（local variation of the magnetization length）等量子特征的空间分布，这些结果揭示了经典微磁模型（classical micromagnetic model）的局限性。

Conclusion: 近期提出的正则化微磁方程（regularized micromagnetic equation）为超越经典微磁模型、描述上述量子效应提供了合适的扩展框架。

Abstract: We study the quantum properties of two- and three-dimensional spin textures -- $kπ$-skyrmions and hopfion rings -- within the cluster mean-field approximation (CMFA). By combining the CMFA with a symmetrization procedure, we achieve two key advances: the accurate computation of quantum fluctuations in large spin textures and reliable access to metastable states. These challenges are generally insurmountable using standard methods, which are severely limited by the curse of dimensionality and typically restricted to ground-state properties. Exploiting the cylindrical symmetry of the studied magnetic configurations, we construct one-dimensional chain-like clusters that can be efficiently simulated using the density matrix renormalization group method, while inter-cluster interactions are treated at the mean-field level. The resulting spatial profiles of quantum features such as the local variation of the magnetization length in hopfion rings reveal limitations of the classical micromagnetic model and indicate the necessity of its extension. We demonstrate that the recently proposed regularized micromagnetic equation provides a suitable framework for this purpose.

### [75] [Screening-controlled dynamical criticality in the quantum Hall regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09244)
*Tanima Chanda,Simrandeep Kaur,Anantbir Virk,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,G. J. Sreejith,Yuval Gefen,Aveek Bid*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过结合温度标度（temperature scaling）与电流标度（current scaling），并利用双石墨栅控石墨烯器件调控库仑相互作用范围，在量子霍尔相变（quantum Hall plateau transition）中分离提取了动力学指数 $z$ 和局域化长度指数 $\gamma$，发现栅极屏蔽选择性地修改动力学临界性（dynamical criticality），而 $\gamma$ 保持不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在连续电子相变中，库仑相互作用会改变长度、能量和温度之间的关系，但仅凭有限温度标度只能测得组合指数 $\kappa = 1/(z\gamma)$，无法区分空间临界性（spatial criticality）与动力学临界性（dynamical criticality）。本文旨在突破这一限制，独立提取动力学指数 $z$ 和局域化长度指数 $\gamma$。

Method: 引入两项创新：一是将温度标度与独立的电流标度相结合，分别提取 $z$ 和 $\gamma$，而非假设其中一个推导另一个；二是采用双石墨栅控石墨烯器件，通过改变磁长度（magnetic length）$l_B$ 与石墨栅距离 $d$ 的比值，几何调控有效库仑相互作用范围，从而在同一器件平台上对比屏蔽（screened）与非屏蔽（unscreened）相互作用区间。

Result: 温度标度给出屏蔽区间 $\kappa \simeq 0.21$，非屏蔽区间 $\kappa \simeq 0.41$。结合电流标度后发现，屏蔽使 $z$ 从非屏蔽区间的 $\simeq 1$ 变为屏蔽区间的 $\simeq 2$，而 $\gamma$ 始终接近 $2.4$，实验不确定性范围内不变。

Conclusion: 栅控屏蔽选择性地修改量子霍尔相变中依赖相互作用的动力学部分，而不改变局域化长度指数 $\gamma$。该工作将几何屏蔽（geometric screening）确立为一种调控相互作用的通用工具，可用于解耦相互作用与无序效应，适用于分数量子霍尔态、莫尔材料及其他强局域电子相。

Abstract: At continuous electronic phase transitions, Coulomb interactions can modify the relation between length, energy, and temperature, but experimentally disentangling their effects on spatial versus dynamical criticality has remained difficult, since finite-temperature scaling alone measures only the combined exponent $κ= 1/(zγ)$. Here, we introduce two advances that resolve this limitation. First, by combining temperature scaling with independent current scaling, we separately extract the dynamical exponent $z$ and the localization-length exponent $γ$ at the quantum Hall plateau transition -- rather than inferring one from an assumed value of the other. Second, using dual-graphite-gated graphene devices in which the effective Coulomb interaction range is tuned geometrically by the ratio of the magnetic length $l_B$ to the graphite-gate distance $d$, we track this separation across both screened and unscreened interaction regimes within the same device platform. Temperature scaling gives $κ\simeq 0.21$ in the screened regime and $κ\simeq 0.41$ in the unscreened regime; combining this with current scaling reveals that screening changes $z$ from $\simeq 1$ in the unscreened regime to $\simeq 2$ in the screened regime. In contrast, $γ$ remains close to $2.4$ throughout. Our results establish that gate-controlled screening selectively modifies the interaction-dependent dynamical sector of the quantum Hall transition, leaving the localization-length exponent $γ$ unchanged within experimental uncertainty. More broadly, this work establishes geometric screening as a versatile tool for controlling interactions and disentangling interaction and disorder effects in correlated two-dimensional systems, including fractional quantum Hall states, moiré materials, and other strongly localized electronic phases.

</details>


### [76] [Terahertz field-driven nonlinear Hall effect and other second order transport phenomena in two-dimensional tellurene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09256)
*M. D. Moldavskaya,L. E. Golub,E. Mönch,Chang Niu,Peide D. Ye,J. Wunderlich,S. D. Ganichev*

TL;DR: 本文研究了二维碲烯薄片中太赫兹（THz）场驱动的二阶非线性电子输运现象（包括非线性霍尔效应），实验和理论分析了沿不同晶向的直流电流与电场平方的标度关系，并将其归因于斜散射、侧跃和贝里曲率偶极子等微观机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索太赫兹（terahertz, THz）场驱动下的二阶非线性输运现象（包括非线性霍尔效应）的物理机制，并建立非线性输运电流与线性光电效应（linear photogalvanic effect, LPGE）之间的等价关系。

Method: 采用二维碲烯薄片制备霍尔条样品，沿平行和垂直于晶轴的两种方向测量由线偏振太赫兹辐射激发的直流电流；结合栅极电压调控与变温（室温至4.2 K）及变频实验，同时建立唯象理论和微观理论进行描述。

Result: 直流电流与太赫兹辐射的面内电场平方成正比，并随电场方向变化；电流由非线性霍尔效应（NLHE）、非线性纵向（NLL）和非线性对角（NLD）电流三部分贡献组成；NLH、NLL、NLD 电流与线偏振及非偏振太赫兹辐射吸收引起的线性光电效应贡献等价；电流随降温及辐射频率降低而显著增大；电子导电和空穴导电下电流符号相反。

Conclusion: 太赫兹辐射诱导的电流源于斜散射（skew scattering）、侧跃（side jump）和贝里曲率偶极子（Berry curvature dipole）等微观机制；实验结果与现象学和微观理论吻合良好。

Abstract: We study terahertz field-driven second-order nonlinear electron transport phenomena, including the nonlinear Hall effect (NLHE), in two-dimensional tellurene flakes. The dc current excited by linearly polarized terahertz (THz) radiation in Hall bar samples is investigated in directions both along and perpendicular to the $c$-axis of tellurene. As expected for second-order transport phenomena, the current scales as the square of the in-plane electric field of the radiation $\bf E$, and depends on its orientation. The current results from a combination of three contributions, including the NLHE, the Nonlinear Longitudinal (NLL) and Nonlinear Diagonal (NLD) currents. We established the equivalence between NLH, NLL, and NLD transport currents and Linear photogalvanic effect (LPGE) contributions induced by the absorption of linearly polarized and unpolarized THz radiation. All contributions can be controlled by a gate voltage and have opposite signs for electron and hole conductivity. The magnitude of the current increases drastically when the samples are cooled from room temperature to 4.2 K. It also increases with decreasing radiation frequency. These results are well described by the developed phenomenological and microscopic theories. We show that the THz radiation-induced electric current originates from microscopic mechanisms such as skew scattering, side jump, and the Berry curvature dipole.

Abstract: We measured coherent ultrafast dynamics of exciton complexes in a single strongly-confined InAs quantum dot embedded in a GaAs nanopost. ### [78] [Majorana parity qubit in coupled minimal Kitaev chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09511)
*Francesco Zatelli,Bart Roovers,Nick van Loo,Antonio Lombardi,Juan D. Torres Luna,Sebastian Miles,Vincent P. M. Sietses,Florian J. Bennebroek Evertsz',Pablo Cova Fariña,Alberto Bordin,Ghada Badawy,Erik P. A. M. Bakkers,Michael Wimmer,Leo P. Kouwenhoven*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究在量子点-超导阵列构成的双站点Kitaev链中，实验展示了Majorana奇偶性量子比特（Majorana parity qubit）的相干控制，通过观测全局偶、奇宇称流形中的相干振荡（coherent parity oscillations）证实了Majorana零模（Majorana zero modes）的存在，并系统研究了耦合与失谐参数对振荡频率和退相干的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Majorana零模（Majorana zero modes）通过将信息非定域地编码在费米子奇偶性（fermion parity）中，为容错量子比特提供了一条可行路径。此前研究虽已在短链（如双站点链）中识别出“穷人的Majorana”（poor man's Majoranas）特征，但其仅有有限的拓扑保护；一个关键挑战是如何超越电输运测量中的模式识别，在时域中实现相干量子比特控制（coherent qubit control）。

Method: 实验利用量子点-超导体阵列构建双站点Kitaev链（two-site Kitaev chains），利用总费米子奇偶性守恒将系统划分为全局偶、奇宇称流形（global even and odd parity manifolds）。通过实现链间相干耦合，在两个流形中观测相干奇偶性振荡（coherent parity oscillations），并在Majorana sweet spot处验证振荡频率相等这一理论预言。系统改变链间耦合强度（inter-chain coupling）和量子点失谐（quantum-dot detunings）以测量其对振荡频率和相干性的影响。

Result: 在Majorana sweet spot处，全局偶、奇宇称流形中的相干奇偶性振荡频率相等，符合孤立Majorana零模的理论预期。振荡频率和相干时间随链间耦合和量子点失谐的系统性变化与短、部分保护链（partially protected chains）的模型定量吻合。

Conclusion: 该工作首次实现了对Majorana量子比特的相干控制，该量子比特编码在最小Kitaev链（minimal Kitaev chains）中Majorana零模的费米子奇偶性上。这一结果为基于Majorana零模的容错量子计算提供了关键的时域操控能力。

Abstract: Majorana zero modes provide a route to fault-tolerant qubits by encoding information non-locally in fermion parity. Their sensitivity to noise is expected to decrease exponentially with increasing separation between the Majoranas, a suppression known as topological protection. Kitaev chains engineered in quantum dot-superconductor arrays provide a tunable platform in which separated Majorana zero modes can emerge at the ends of the chain, even in two-site chains. These minimal-chain modes are known as poor man's Majoranas and retain characteristic Majorana properties, including near-zero energy and equal electron-hole character, but have only limited protection. A key outstanding challenge is to move beyond identifying such modes in electrical transport measurements and achieve coherent qubit control in the time domain. Here, we demonstrate a Majorana parity qubit by realizing coherent coupling between two-site Kitaev chains. Since total fermion parity is conserved, the system separates into global even and odd parity manifolds. We observe coherent parity oscillations in both manifolds with equal oscillation frequencies at the Majorana sweet spot, as predicted for isolated Majorana zero modes. We further show that the oscillation frequency and coherence depend systematically on inter-chain coupling and quantum-dot detunings, in close agreement with our model for short, partially protected chains. Our results establish the first coherent control of a Majorana qubit, encoded in the fermion parity of Majorana zero modes in minimal Kitaev chains.

</details>


### [79] [Confinement drives valley splitting above 4K in buried silicon quantum wells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09570)
*Davide Degli Esposti,Emma Catherine Brann,Asser Elsayed,Davide Costa,Mark Friesen,Giordano Scappucci*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文测量了埋层硅量子阱中单电子自旋量子比特（spin qubit）的能量尺度，发现通过静电约束可有效提升谷分裂（valley splitting），为基于自旋的量子计算架构（如shuttling架构）提供了可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硅自旋量子比特中导带谷（conduction-band valley）的近乎简并会产生泄漏通道（leakage channel），阻碍量子比特的规模化扩展和基于shuttling的架构设计。本文旨在通过协同设计低无序度和高谷分裂的埋层硅量子阱，测量并调控相关能量尺度以解决这一瓶颈。

Method: 在四个量子点（quantum dot）构成的线性阵列中，测量单电子谷分裂、轨道能量（orbital energy）以及两电子单重态-三重态分裂（singlet-triplet splitting），并分析谷分裂与轨道能量之间的相关性。

Result: 平均轨道能量为2.4(2) meV，平均单电子谷分裂为0.40(6) meV，平均两电子单重态-三重态分裂为0.24(7) meV。在三个量子点中谷分裂与轨道能量呈强线性相关（系数≈0.22 meV/meV）；一个量子点表现出最高谷分裂0.76(2) meV且相关性低，表明其适合自旋量子比特操作。

Conclusion: 强静电约束可在埋层量子阱中有效提升谷分裂，为在低无序异质结构中实现shuttling和稀疏占据（sparse-occupation）架构奠定了基础。

Abstract: Controlling the energy scales of a quantum system is essential for defining robust qubits. In silicon spin qubits, the nearly degenerate conduction-band valleys create a leakage channel from the single-spin computational basis, posing a challenge to scaling and to shuttling-based architectures. Here, we measure the relevant energy scales of single-electron spin qubits in buried silicon quantum wells co-designed for low disorder and high valley splitting. Across a linear array of four quantum dots with an average orbital energy of 2.4(2) meV, we report an average single-electron valley splitting of 0.40(6) meV and an average two-electron singlet-triplet splitting of 0.24(7) meV. In three dots, we observe a strong correlation between valley splitting and orbital energy, with an average linear coefficient of $\approx 0.22$ (meV/meV), demonstrating that electrostatic confinement can increase the valley splitting by several hundred microelectronvolts. In contrast, the remaining dot exhibits the highest valley splitting of 0.76(2) meV and low correlation, suggesting excellent characteristics for spin-qubit operation. Our findings demonstrate that strong confinement can be exploited in buried quantum wells to effectively enhance the valley splitting, thereby establishing a viable path toward the realization of shuttling and sparse-occupation-based architectures in low-disorder heterostructures.

</details>


### [80] [Silicon-Germanium Heterostructures with Enhanced Valley Splitting for Spin Qubits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09652)
*David W. Kanaar,Efrain Martinez,Peihong Zhang,Mark F. Gyure*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种Si/SiGe异质结器件级优化策略，通过结合窄量子阱、小Ge尖峰和纯Ge帽层的非传统设计，将谷分裂（valley splitting）提升至1–5 meV，远超以往理论结果，并给出较窄的分布，从而为可扩展硅基自旋量子比特（spin qubit）消除谷分裂这一关键障碍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实现远超电子热能的谷分裂并避免谷激发（valley excitations），是栅极定义硅自旋量子比特（gate-defined Si spin qubit）在初始化、操作和读出中保持一致性的关键前提。然而，此前几乎所有理论研究报道的谷分裂值均不足，难以满足规模化量子处理器对可重复性能的要求。

Method: 采用器件级仿真（device-scale simulation），通过一维紧束缚理论（1D tight-binding theory）纳入原子尺度的合金无序（atomistic alloy disorder）；同时结合目标性的原子密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算进行验证。其核心设计思想是采用非传统的Si/SiGe异质结构，包含窄量子阱（narrow quantum well）、小Ge尖峰（small Ge spike）和纯Ge帽层（pure-Ge cap）。

Result: 所提出的优化策略可将谷分裂提升至1–5 meV，远高于此前绝大多数理论研究的数值，并且在多次无序实现（disorder realizations）中呈现紧密分布，满足可扩展量子比特对性能可重复性的严格要求。

Conclusion: 该研究为可扩展的Si/SiGe自旋量子比特器件提供了明确的实现路径。若在实验中得以验证，将有效消除谷分裂作为大规模硅锗基量子处理器（SiGe-based quantum processor）中根本性问题的困境。

Abstract: Achieving valley splittings well in excess of the thermal energy of electrons and avoiding valley excitations is essential for the consistent initialization, operation and readout of gate-defined Si spin qubits. In this work, we present a device-level optimization strategy for pushing valley splittings to between 1 and 5 meV, well beyond values reported in nearly all previous theoretical studies. Using device-scale simulations that incorporate atomistic alloy disorder through a 1D tight-binding theory, we demonstrate that our proposed approach yields large valley splittings with a tight distribution across disorder realizations, a key requirement for reproducible qubit performance at scale. The approach rests on an unorthodox Si/SiGe heterostructure design combining a narrow quantum well, a small Ge spike, and a pure-Ge cap. We corroborate these predictions with targeted atomistic density functional theory calculations. These results offer a clear path forward for scalable Si/SiGe spin qubit devices and, if realized experimentally, effectively eliminate valley splitting as an existential problem for large scale SiGe-based quantum processors.

### [81] [Ferroelastic instability in rutile TiO2 and thermodynamic suppression of the CaCl2-type phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08860)
*Jared Pohlmann,Anjy-Joe Olatunbosun,Kenneth Park*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过全电子密度泛函理论（density functional theory）与密度泛函微扰理论（density functional perturbation theory）计算，证明了金红石TiO2在13.5 GPa下存在与CaCl2型（Pnnm）结构相关的铁弹不稳定性（ferroelastic instability），但由于热力学竞争，该相仅作为瞬态或弱亚稳中间相存在，解释了其实验上难以观测的原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验上金红石TiO2在高压下通常直接转变为更高配位相（如baddeleyite结构），而CaCl2型（Pnnm）中间相的实验信号长期未能明确探测，其作用尚不清楚。本文旨在探究该相在TiO2高压相变中的角色及其未被观测到的原因。

Method: 采用全电子密度泛函框架（all-electron density functional framework）结合密度泛函微扰理论（density functional perturbation theory）进行计算分析。通过考察弹性常数组合C11–C12的软化以及B1g声子模的凝聚，识别铁弹不稳定性；通过焓计算比较不同相的相对稳定性。

Result: 金红石TiO2在13.5 GPa处出现铁弹不稳定性，表现为正交应变（orthorhombic strain）的发展和双势阱能景（double-well energy landscape），伴随C11–C12弹性组合的软化和B1g声子模的凝聚，涉及TiO6八面体的协同旋转，对称性降低至Pnnm结构。然而，CaCl2型相相对于金红石仅微弱稳定，且焓值上不如columbite相和baddeleyite相有利，因此不作为稳定的高压多形存在。

Conclusion: CaCl2型（Pnnm）相是金红石TiO2固有的铁弹响应（intrinsic ferroelastic response），但由于与columbite和baddeleyite等相的热力学竞争而被抑制，仅作为瞬态或弱亚稳中间相存在。该发现为其实验上难以观测提供了自洽统一的解释。

Abstract: We investigate the role of the CaCl2-type (Pnnm) phase in the high-pressure transformation of rutile TiO2, whose experimental signature has remained elusive. While analogies with other rutile-type oxides suggest such an intermediate, TiO2 typically exhibits a direct transformation to higher-coordination phases such as baddeleyite. Using an all-electron density functional framework combined with density functional perturbation theory, we show that rutile TiO2 undergoes a ferroelastic instability characterized by the development of an orthorhombic strain and a double-well energy landscape at 13.5 GPa. This instability is associated with the softening of the C11 - C12 elastic combination and the condensation of a B1g phonon mode, involving coordinated rotations of TiO6 octahedra that lower the symmetry to the Pnnm structure. Despite this clear elastic and dynamical pathway, enthalpy calculations show that the CaCl2-type phase is only weakly stabilized relative to rutile and remains energetically unfavorable compared to competing columbite and baddeleyite phases. Consequently, the Pnnm phase does not emerge as a stable high-pressure polymorph but instead exists as a transient or weakly metastable intermediate. These results demonstrate that the CaCl2-type phase represents the intrinsic ferroelastic response of rutile TiO2, yet is suppressed by thermodynamic competition, providing a consistent and unified explanation for its elusive experimental observation.

</details>


### [82] [Grain-boundary-mediated kinetic arrest in graphite-to-diamond transformation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08868)
*Zuzanna Malinowska-Trzmielak,Vilmos Neuman,Mark Wilson*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 通过大规模分子动力学模拟，发现石墨前驱体的晶粒结构（grain structure）通过解耦金刚石成核与协同转变传播，调控石墨-金刚石转变路径；结构异质性（structural heterogeneity）是除压力、温度之外被忽略的控制参数，介稳态混合产物本质上是前驱体微结构导致的动力学捕获态（kinetically trapped states）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于理想化单晶石墨的原子模型无法解释高压高温（HPHT）条件下部分转变中间态持续存在的原因，亟需揭示前驱体微观结构对转变路径的影响机制。

Method: 采用大规模分子动力学模拟（large-scale molecular dynamics simulations）研究前驱体晶粒结构如何调控石墨到金刚石的转变路径。

Result: 晶界先促进局部的sp³成核，随后金刚石生长在单个晶粒内部传播，但在晶体学不匹配的晶界处被阻止；结构异质的石墨稳定动力学捕获的混合sp²-sp³态，而大尺寸或单晶区域则有利于协同体相转变为金刚石。

Conclusion: 前驱体结晶度（precursor crystallinity）成为控制石墨-金刚石转变路径的实用参数；介稳转变产物应被重新理解为前驱体微结构导致的动力学捕获态，而非热力学中间体。

Abstract: The graphite-to-diamond transition exhibits striking variability under high-pressure, high-temperature (HPHT) conditions, producing diamond, graphitic phases, or metastable, mixed diamond-graphite nanocomposites despite similar synthesis conditions. Existing atomistic models, largely based on idealised single-crystal graphite, do not explain the persistence of partially transformed intermediate states under HPHT conditions. Here, using large-scale molecular dynamics simulations, we show that precursor grain structure governs graphite-to-diamond transformation pathways by decoupling diamond nucleation from cooperative transformation propagation. Grain boundaries first facilitate local sp$^3$ nucleation, after which diamond growth propagates within individual grains but becomes arrested at crystallographically mismatched grain boundaries. As a result, structurally heterogeneous graphite stabilizes kinetically arrested mixed sp$^2$-sp$^3$ states, whereas large or single-crystalline domains favour cooperative bulk transformation into diamond. Our findings identify structural heterogeneity as a missing control parameter alongside pressure and temperature, reframing metastable transformation products as kinetically trapped states arising from precursor microstructure rather than thermodynamic intermediates. Precursor crystallinity therefore emerges as a practical control parameter governing graphite-to-diamond transformation pathways.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: （1）共沉积的NPD和TPD形成了高密度玻璃，且热稳定性增强；（2）密度和稳定性对基底温度（substrate temperature）的依赖关系相互关联；（3）共沉积玻璃的双折射（birefringence）由混合物的约化基底温度（reduced substrate temperature）决定；（4）高稳定性双组分玻璃向过冷液体的转变从自由表面（free surface）开始并以恒定速度向体相传播，与单组分PVD玻璃类似。

Abstract: Physical Vapor Deposition (PVD) is widely utilized for the production of organic semiconductor devices due to its ability to form thin layers with exceptional properties. Although the layers in the device usually consist of two or more components, there is limited understanding about the fundamental characteristics of such multi-component vapor-deposited glasses. Here, spectroscopic ellipsometry was employed to characterize the densities, thermal stabilities and optical properties of co-vapor deposited NPD and TPD glasses across the entire range of composition. We find that co-deposited NPD and TPD form high density glasses with enhanced thermal stability. The dependences of density and stability upon substrate temperature are correlated, and the birefringence of the co-deposited glasses is determined by the reduced substrate temperature of mixtures. Additionally, we observe that the transformation of a highly stable and dense two component glass into its supercooled liquid initiates from the free surface and propagates into the bulk at constant velocity, like single component PVD glasses. All these features are consistent with the surface equilibration mechanism.

### [84] [Hybrid DiffractGPT-Rietveld Refinement Framework for Automated X-ray Diffraction Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08890)

Method: AGAPI-XRD 采用混合框架（hybrid framework），核心组件包括：DiffractGPT（生成式结构预测）、JARVIS-DFT 与 COD 数据库（模式匹配）、自动化 Rietveld 精修以及 ALIGNN-FF 结构弛豫（relaxation），所有功能通过统一 API 集成。首先利用该流水线评估 RRUFF 数据库中实验表征的矿物结构，然后基于 Alexandria PBE-hull 数据集子集和已知晶格参数的 RRUFF 矿物子集进行晶格参数保真度基准测试。

Conclusion: AGAPI-XRD 通过整合多种互补方法，实现了从粉末 XRD 数据到晶体结构的可访问、端到端自动化确定。该框架在基准测试中展现出高成功率，且同时覆盖已知相与数据库缺失的复杂材料，推动了晶体学分析流程的自动化与普及化。

Abstract: X-ray diffraction (XRD) is fundamental to structural materials characterization, yet transforming a raw powder pattern into a refined crystal structure still demands considerable domain expertise. We present AGAPI-XRD, a hybrid framework integrating DiffractGPT generative structure prediction, database pattern matching against JARVIS-DFT and COD, and automated Rietveld refinement and ALIGNN-FF relaxation through a unified API at https://atomgpt.org/xrd. First, we used the AGAPI-XRD pipeline to evaluate the crystal structure of a variety of minerals in the RRUFF database that were experimentally characterized using powder x-ray diffraction. Next, we benchmarked the lattice parameter prediction fidelity of the AGAPI-XRD pipeline using a subset of the Alexandria PBE-hull dataset and the subset of RRUFF minerals that have known lattice parameters. AGAPI-XRD returns valid lattice parameters for 79.7\% of the RRUFF benchmark minerals and for 94.8--98.1\% of the Alexandria subset, while identifying a candidate structure for 93.8\% of RRUFF minerals. For this benchmark, pattern matching delivers the highest accuracy for known phases, while DiffractGPT extends structure generation to complex materials absent from existing databases. Together, AGAPI-XRD advances accessible, end-to-end automated crystal structure determination from powder XRD data.

Abstract: Two-dimensional van der Waals heterobilayers provide an attractive platform for the development of next-generation spintronic devices. Among all the structures, CoSe2/WTe2 heterobilayer exhibits maximum Curie temperature (273.87 K). The combined results establish that interface engineering makes MSe2/WTe2 heterobilayers as a promising candidates for next-generation low-dimensional spintronic applications.

### [86] [Fast Homoepitaxy on (100) \b{eta}-Ga2O3 Substrates with Large Grown-In Offcut](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08929)
*M. Brooks Tellekamp,Drew Haven,David Joyce,John Mangum,Henry Garland,Robert Lavelle,Kevin Schulte,Anna Sacchi,Matt Young,Andriy Zakutayev*

Conclusion: 大斜切角方法有效解决了(100)取向β-Ga₂O₃晶圆生长速率慢的问题，且保持了高晶体质量。研究结果验证了(100)取向晶圆在功率器件中的可规模化应用前景，强调了晶面与斜切角在低对称性半导体材料中的关键作用。

Abstract: The choice of crystalline orientation and offcut angle is non-trivial for low-symmetry $β\text{-Ga}_2\text{O}_3$, where anisotropy impacts bulk and thin film synthesis, material properties, and power device fabrication and performance. Scalable (100)-oriented $β\text{-Ga}_2\text{O}_3$ wafers are desirable for electronic devices but are not typically used due to 10-30x slower growth rates compared to other orientations. Here we report molecular beam epitaxy (MBE) growth rates equal to the fast growth direction by using (100) $Ga_2O_3$ wafers with large grown-in offcuts. The offcuts (up to 13.4°) are directly grown by Edge-defined Film-fed Growth (EFG) of 2D ribbons with rotated seed crystals, avoiding material loss from crystal boule offcut methods while maintaining high crystalline quality. Abstract: Aqueous corrosion of metals involves multiple interconnected processes. Thus, computer simulation of corrosion as a whole needs to be able to describe the individual processes and how they influence each other. Atomistic simulations are designed to obtain detailed information for small regions of space over short times. Thus there are limits to the understanding that can be obtained by atomistic simulations alone. Here is presented a method that uses generalised rate equations to extend the length and time scales that can be accessed. It is shown to reduce to either the phase field or cellular automata methods in certain limits. The generalised kinetic equations can reproduce the behaviour described by both the Nernst-Planck and Butler-Volmer equations, which are frequently used to describe corrosion. In addition, the method can describe local rearrangements of atoms such as chemical reactions. Example results are shown for illustrative 1D and 2D problems, with good agreement being found with other methods.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于自洽电荷（SCC）方案的密度泛函紧束缚（DFTB）计算在大规模模拟和高通量流程中面临迭代收敛缓慢的问题，成为主要性能瓶颈。

Method: 采用元素特异性机器学习模型，以平滑原子位置重叠（Smooth Overlap of Atomic Positions, SOAP）描述符作为特征，结合核岭回归（kernel ridge regression）算法，在参考计算数据上训练电荷预测模型，用于预测最优的初始原子电荷。

Result: 机器学习预测的初始电荷在有机分子、生物分子、水团簇、过渡金属氧化物及固态电解质等多种化学体系中，均能持续且显著地改善SCC迭代的收敛性能。

Conclusion: 该机器学习加速方法有效克服了DFTB模拟中SCC收敛慢的瓶颈，可推广至多种复杂化学体系，提升大规模和高通量模拟的计算效率。

Abstract: Semiempirical electronic structure methods such as Density-Functional Tight-Binding (DFTB) offer a computationally efficient approach to molecular and materials simulations, bridging the gap between first-principles accuracy and classical force field speed while retaining full access to electronic properties. However, DFTB calculations based on self-consistent charge (SCC) schemes can still suffer from slow convergence, particularly for complex molecular and materials systems, making the iterative procedure a significant bottleneck in large-scale simulations and high-throughput workflows. We present a machine learning approach that accelerates DFTB simulations by predicting optimal initial atomic charges. Using element-specific models based on the Smooth Overlap of Atomic Positions descriptor and kernel ridge regression, we train charge models on reference calculations and demonstrate that ML-predicted initial charges consistently and significantly improve SCC convergence across diverse chemical systems including organic molecules, biomolecules, water clusters, transition metal oxides and solid electrolytes.

</details>


### [89] [Semi-Empirical Kinetic Model for Phase Selection in Rapidly Solidified Multicomponent Concentrated Alloys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09321)

Method: 方法基于临界冷却速率的概念，将拓扑依赖的BCC、FCC、HCP类结晶路径排序与玻璃形成能力校正相结合。具体包括：引入平滑BCC乘子（smoothed BCC multiplier）的拓扑依赖粘度校正，以及基于混合焓（mixing enthalpy）、过剩熵（excess entropy）和原子尺寸分散度（atomic-size dispersion）的连续玻璃形成能力校正因子。

Result: 与实验及计算数据的对比表明，该动力学判据能够捕捉价电子浓度（valence electron concentration, VEC）准则预期的晶格类型变化，描述相分离的动力学抑制，并识别竞争性多相结晶。模型还能区分高与低玻璃形成能力的合金。

Conclusion: 该框架为快速凝固多组元熔体中的动力学相竞争提供了一种实用的初步评估方法（practical approach for preliminary evaluation），具有较好的预测能力和普适性。

Abstract: A semi-empirical kinetic framework is formulated for predicting phase selection in multicomponent concentrated alloys under rapid solidification. The approach is based on the critical cooling rate required to suppress competing crystalline pathways and combines topology-dependent ranking of BCC-, FCC-, and HCP-like crystallization pathways with a correction for glass-forming ability. The formulation includes a topology-dependent viscosity correction with a smoothed BCC multiplier and a continuous correction factor for glass-forming ability based on mixing enthalpy, excess entropy, and atomic-size dispersion. Comparison with experimental and computational data shows that the kinetic criterion captures changes in the lattice type expected from the valence electron concentration criterion, describes kinetic suppression of phase separation, and identifies competitive multiphase crystallization. The model also distinguishes alloys with high and low glass-forming ability. The proposed framework provides a practical approach for preliminary evaluation of kinetic phase competition in rapidly solidified multicomponent melts.

### [90] [Unlocking ultrafast spin dynamics in a rare-earth magnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09413)
*Paul Herrgen,Christian Holzmann,Torben Manzke,Ulrich Nowak,Peter M. Oppeneer,Manfred Albrecht,Benjamin Stadtmüller,Martin Aeschlimann*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本工作通过选择性光学激发稀土磁体中局域化的4f磁态，实现了比传统激发方式快两个数量级以上的超快退磁（38 fs），揭示了光学激发路径对超快磁动力学的决定性作用，为远程操控角动量流提供了新的光子学手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光驱动磁动力学（magneto-optics）的速度受限于角动量在电子、自旋和晶格自由度之间的传递效率。稀土磁体中，光学激发主要作用于巡游电子（itinerant electrons），而磁矩位于局域的4f态，导致该过程通常很慢。本文旨在克服这一限制。

Method: 本文采用飞秒泵浦-探测磁光光谱（femtosecond pump-probe magneto-optical spectroscopy）技术，对亚铁磁材料钆铁石榴石（GIG）中Gd3+的4f能级内跃迁（4.65 eV）进行共振激发，并解析了反铁磁耦合的Gd和Fe子晶格的后续动力学。

Result: 直接激发4f流形（manifold）引发了Gd子晶格的超快退磁（ultrafast demagnetization），特征时间为38 fs，比单质钆（elemental gadolinium）快两个数量级以上，甚至快于同一材料中Fe子晶格的响应。非共振激发则显著抑制了Gd动力学的加速，而对Fe响应影响不大。

Conclusion: 稀土体系的超快磁响应不仅由本征材料性质决定，还受光学激发路径的调控。选择性激发局域磁态为工程设计角动量流（angular-momentum flow）与远程控制非平衡态磁性（far-from-equilibrium magnetism）提供了强有力的光子学手段。

Abstract: The speed of optically driven magnetization dynamics is fundamentally determined by how efficiently angular momentum can be transferred between electronic, spin and lattice degrees of freedom. In rare-earth magnets, this process is typically slow because optical excitation primarily addresses itinerant electrons, whereas the magnetic moment resides in localized 4f states. Here we show that selective optical excitation of localized magnetic states can overcome this limitation. Using femtosecond pump-probe magneto-optical spectroscopy of ferrimagnetic gadolinium iron garnet, we resonantly excite an intra-4f transition of Gd3+ at 4.65 eV and resolve the ensuing dynamics of the antiferromagnetically coupled Gd and Fe sublattices. Direct excitation of the 4f manifold induces an ultrafast demagnetization of the Gd sublattice with a characteristic time of 38 fs, more than two orders of magnitude faster than in elemental gadolinium and even faster than the response of the Fe sublattice in the same material. By contrast, off-resonant excitation strongly suppresses the acceleration of the Gd dynamics while leaving the Fe response largely unchanged. These results demonstrate that the ultrafast magnetic response of rare-earth systems is governed not only by intrinsic material properties but also by the optical excitation pathway. Selective access to localized magnetic states therefore provides a powerful photonic handle for engineering angular-momentum flow and controlling magnetism far from equilibrium.

</details>


### [91] [Electronic manipulation of polar order in electron crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09425)
*Takashi Kikkawa,Ziyan Chen,Yuto Fujimoto,Takahiro Morimoto,Yuya Hirata,Hiroki Arisawa,Alexey A. Kaverzin,Satoshi Okamoto,Yoichi Okimoto,Naoshi Ikeda,Eiji Saitoh*

TL;DR: 本文通过在室温下对顺磁半导体LuFe₂O₄施加电流脉冲，实现了电荷有序方向（charge-ordering direction）的电子学操控与读取，并演示了基于非互易电阻（non-reciprocal resistance）的记忆操作，为电荷有序电子学（charge-ordering electronics）的实用化开辟了道路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子晶体（electron crystal）中，电荷有序模式可像原子晶体一样编码信息，但目前尚缺乏对电荷有序方向进行电子学操控与读取的有效手段。

Method: 对顺磁半导体LuFe₂O₄在室温下施加电流脉冲，测量其非互易电阻率（non-reciprocal resistivity）的变化；同时结合考虑电荷有序影响的能带间贝里曲率（inter-band Berry curvature）进行数值计算。

Result: 电流脉冲调制了LuFe₂O₄的非互易电阻率并使其符号反转，该效应在电荷有序温度以上消失；数值计算结果与实验一致；基于该现象实现了非互易电阻记忆操作（non-reciprocal resistance memory operation）。

Conclusion: 实验结果证明了电荷有序方向的可控电子学读写，为实现基于电荷有序电子学的信息存储器件提供了可能。

Abstract: When interaction among atoms or ions is strong enough, they often arrange periodically, forming a crystal. The arrangement patterns of atoms or ions can encode information, a concept that has enabled devices such as ferroelectric memories. It has been found that not only atoms or ions but also electrons in condensed matter can crystallize when Coulomb interaction is strong enough. Typical examples are charge-ordered states in solids, where different valences, or different electron numbers, of an ion spontaneously form a spatial pattern on the lattice. In such electron crystals, information is expected to be encoded into the electron-ordering patterns. Here, we demonstrate electronic manipulation and readout of charge-ordering directions in a paramagnetic semiconductor LuFe$_2$O$_4$. By applying current pulses at room temperature, we observed that the non-reciprocal resistivity of LuFe$_2$O$_4$ is modulated along with a sign reversal, which disappears above the charge-ordering temperature. A numerical calculation incorporating inter-band Berry curvature affected by the charge ordering is consistent with the experimental results. By applying the observed phenomenon, we also demonstrate a non-reciprocal resistance memory operation in the charge-ordered LuFe$_2$O$_4$. This result opens the door to realizing charge-ordering electronics.

### [92] [Unraveling atomic-resolution valence electron energy-loss spectroscopic imaging in a single-crystal CaNb2O6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09466)
*Sz-Chian Liou,Xiang-Lin Huang,Vladimir P. Oleshko,I-Ching Lin,Yin-Ping Lan,Hsin-An Chen,Guo-Jiun Shu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究利用配备混合像素直接电子探测器和球差校正扫描透射电子显微镜的能量过滤光谱仪，在单晶铌酸钙（CaNb₂O₆）中实现了从纳米到原子尺度的低损耗电子能量损失谱成像，观察到了体等离子体激元（volume plasmons）和混合等离子体激元-激子（plexcitons）等激发态，并揭示了原子分辨的对比反转及[ NbO₆]八面体对带间跃迁的直接贡献，证明了该技术在复杂晶体纳米结构表征中的强大潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管过去二十年电子光学和能谱仪设计取得了进步，但由于非弹性电子散射的非局域化（delocalization）效应，实现原子分辨率的价电子能量损失谱成像（valence-electron energy-loss spectroscopy imaging）仍然面临挑战。本研究旨在克服这一困难，探索在原子尺度上可视化复杂晶体纳米结构中的低能激发和电子性质。

Method: 采用配备混合像素直接电子探测器（hybrid-pixel direct electron detector）和球差校正扫描透射电子显微镜（spherical aberration-corrected scanning transmission electron microscopy, Cs-STEM）的能量过滤光谱仪，在从纳米到原子尺度的空间分辨率下分析单晶CaNb₂O₆中的多电子激发（many-electron excitations）和带间跃迁（interband transitions）。同时采用同轴EELS配置进行原子分辨率的零损失峰（zero-loss peak, ZLP）成像，并分析收集角（collection angle）对弹性对比度保持的影响。

Result: 在带隙以上约3.8 eV的低损耗区观察到了约6 eV和15 eV的体等离子体激元（volume plasmons, VPs），以及约7.3 eV的强关联等离子体激元与激子混合态——等离子体激元-激子（plexcitons）。原子分辨的plexciton和VP图像相对于高角环形暗场像（high-angle annular dark-field, HAADF）出现了对比反转（contrast reversal）。通过弱束（weak-beam）设置获得的ZLP和价电子能量损失谱（VEELS）图像均显示出类似Z-衬度（Z-contrast）。[NbO₆]八面体对3.2 eV至3.5 eV能量损失范围内的带间跃迁横向分布图有直接贡献。

Conclusion: Cs-STEM-EELS能够揭示与低能损失（low-energy losses）相关的原子尺度对比度，是可视化复杂晶体纳米结构中原子位点、间隙位点和点缺陷的结构、成键及电子性质的有力工具。

Abstract: Despite advancements in electron optics and spectrometer design over the past twenty years, atomic-resolution valence-electron energy-loss spectroscopy imaging remains challenging due to the delocalization of inelastic electron scattering. In this study, we used an energy-filtered spectrometer equipped with a hybrid-pixel direct electron detector and spherical aberration-corrected scanning transmission electron microscopy to analyze many-electron excitations and interband transitions in a single-crystal calcium niobate, CaNb2O6, with spatial resolution ranging from the nanometers to the atomic scale. In the low-loss region above the bandgap at about 3.8 eV, we observed volume plasmons, around 6 eV and 15 eV energy loss, as well as a mix of strongly correlated plasmons and excitons, known as plexcitons, at approximately 7.3 eV energy loss. Additionally, we employed an on-axis EELS setup for atomic-resolution zero-loss peak (ZLP) imaging and visualized energy- and atom-resolved images of plexcitons and VPs, which showed contrast reversal relative to high-angle annular dark-field images. To investigate elastic contrast preservation, we also analyzed the effect of the collection angle and minimized its influence to produce delocalized VP images. In fact, the ZLP and VEELS images obtained using the weak-beam setup demonstrate that, in both cases, the contrast resembles Z-contrast. Moreover, we found that [NbO6] octahedra directly contributed to the lateral maps of interband transitions in the range from 3.2 eV to 3.5 eV energy loss. These findings demonstrate that Cs-STEM-EELS, which examines atomic-scale contrast associated with low-energy losses, can be a powerful tool for visualizing the structure, bonding, and electronic properties of complex crystalline nanostructures, including individual atomic sites, interstitial sites, and point defects.

### [93] [Local well-posedness for nonlinear Dirac equation on $N$-star metric graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09303)
*Huichao Xing,Zhipeng Yang*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了非紧致 N 星度量图（N-star metric graph）上非线性狄拉克方程（nonlinear Dirac equation）的柯西问题（Cauchy problem），通过 Bourgain 型空间（Bourgain-type spaces）和分数阶 Nemytskii 估计（fractional Nemytskii estimates），在低正则初始数据下证明了局部适定性（local well-posedness），并建立了解的 L² 守恒律与爆破备择性（blow-up alternative）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性狄拉克方程在度量图上的动力学行为尚未被充分理解，特别是非紧致图结构带来的低正则性问题。本文旨在处理当初始数据位于低于 1/2 阶的正则空间时，如何建立局部适定性理论。

Method: 利用 Dirac-Kirchhoff 算子（Dirac-Kirchhoff operator）的谱分解（spectral resolution）构造 Bourgain 型空间 $X^{s,b}$；结合 Dirac 流的初等 $L^\infty$ 界以及迹阈值（trace threshold）以下的分数阶 Nemytskii 估计进行非线性估计。

Result: 对初始数据 $\psi_0\in H_D^s(G)\cap L^\infty(G;\mathbb{C}^2)$，其中 $0\le s<1/2$，证明了局部适定性，解存在于 $C([0,T];H_D^s(G))\cap X_T^{s,b}\cap L^\infty([0,T]\times G)$。此外，$\|\psi(t)\|_{L^2}$ 沿解守恒，并在 $H_D^s$ 与时空 $L^\infty$ 控制范数下建立了爆破备择性。

Conclusion: 本文为度量图上非线性狄拉克方程的低正则局部适定性提供了理论框架，其方法有望推广至其他类型的非线性色散方程（dispersive equations）在图上（metric graphs）的适定性问题。

Abstract: We consider the Cauchy problem for the nonlinear Dirac equation on a noncompact $N$-star metric graph $G$, \[ \mathrm{i}\partial_t ψ= Dψ- |ψ|^{p-2}ψ, \qquad ψ(0)=ψ_0, \] where $p\ge3$, $ψ:\mathbb{R}\times G\to\mathbb{C}^2$ and $D$ denotes the self-adjoint Dirac-Kirchhoff operator on $G$. Using Bourgain-type spaces defined through the spectral resolution of $D$, together with elementary $L^\infty$ bounds for the Dirac flow and fractional Nemytskii estimates below the trace threshold, we prove local well-posedness for initial data \[ ψ_0\in H_D^s(G)\cap L^\infty(G;\mathbb C^2), \qquad 0\le s<\frac12 . \] The corresponding solution belongs to \[ C([0,T];H_D^s(G))\cap X_T^{s,b}\cap L^\infty([0,T]\times G). \] Moreover, $\|ψ(t)\|_{L^2(G;\mathbb{C}^2)}$ is conserved along the solution on the existence interval. We also establish a blow-up alternative in the combined $H_D^s$ and space-time $L^\infty$ control norm.

</details>


### [94] [On Maximal Total Entropy Production Models for Steady Evaporation of a Calorically Perfect Polyatomic Gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09574)
*Niclas Bernhoff,Eddie Wadbro*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本研究针对多原子气体（polyatomic gas）在稳态蒸发过程中气液界面处流体动力学方程的边界条件展开分析，基于修改后的熵泛函（entropy functional）重新审视半空间蒸发问题，并提出了能准确拟合不同比热比下蒸发曲线（evaporation curves）的简单函数形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多原子气体在冷凝相界面处的蒸发问题涉及流体动力学方程的边界条件（boundary conditions），现有研究对此问题的精确解析描述仍不充分，尤其是对具有内自由度的分子体系。

Method: 基于先前结果，采用修改后的熵泛函（entropy functional）重新分析半空间蒸发问题；研究（修改后的）最大总熵产率（maximal total entropy production）曲线的结构，并提出拟合数值结果的简单函数形式。

Result: 所提出的函数形式及其修正系数不仅很好地拟合了本研究的数值结果，也出人意料地拟合了此前不同数值方法获得的蒸发曲线。这些依赖于比热比（ratio of specific heats）的简单函数对于不同内自由度数均表现出良好的拟合效果。

Conclusion: 对于热完全气体（calorically perfect gas）且分子行为类似刚性转子（rigid rotors）的情形，所提出的简单函数可有效描述多原子气体稳态蒸发时的界面边界条件，且对不同比热比具有普适性。

Abstract: This study investigates the boundary conditions for fluid-dynamic equations at the interface of a gas and its condensed phase during steady evaporation of a polyatomic gas. Evaporation curves illustrating the dependence of the temperature and pressure ratios on the Mach number are considered for a calorically perfect gas whose molecules behave like rigid rotors. At the condensed phase, complete absorption conditions are assumed. Also an extension to cases in which a part of the molecules is diffusely reflected at the condensed phase is also considered. We revisit the half-space evaporation problem for polyatomic gases based on previous results, applied to a slightly modified entropy functional. The structure of the (modified) maximal total entropy production curves is investigated, and simple functions that accurately fit the numerical results are proposed. Functions of the proposed form, with modified coefficients, also fit the evaporation curves previously obtained by different numerical methods surprisingly well. The approximation is performed for different numbers of internal degrees of freedom or ratios of specific heats. Simple functions that depend on the ratio of specific heats are found to fit the obtained evaporation curves for different ratios of specific heats very well.

### [95] [A Cloud-Accessible Open-Source Framework for the Electromagnetic Modelling of Applied Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09572)
*Yusen Guo,Alberto Paganini,Harold S. Ruiz*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出H-cloud形式体系，一个基于云访问与开源有限元框架，用于实用超导体的电磁建模。该方法采用Nédélec有限元离散化表述第二类超导体的非线性电磁响应，在脚本化Python工作流中显式陈述变分层面的切向场边界条件、非线性E-J幂律和全隐式时间离散残差。该实现在Firedrake平台上通过UFL和PETSc非线性求解器构建，同一脚本可在本地和云环境（如Google Colab）中无修改运行。在圆柱超导体的标准磁化基准测试中，开源工作流复现商业参考磁化回路的误差约在1%以内，相对峰值误差低于1.5%。该框架为超导体模拟、基准测试和未来优化导向建模提供了严谨、可复现且便携的路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实用超导体（applied superconductors）的电磁建模需要兼顾计算严谨性、可复现性和可及性。现有商业软件（如COMSOL）虽功能强大但封闭且昂贵，而纯科研代码往往缺乏可移植性和文档完整性。本文旨在提出一个完全开源、云端可执行且结构透明的有限元框架，使超导体非线性电磁建模的完整求解逻辑——包括变分形式、边界条件和求解器结构——对用户保持完全可见，同时支持正向模拟、伴随微分（adjoint differentiation）和偏微分方程约束优化（PDE-constrained optimisation）。

Method: 基于H-cloud形式体系（H-cloud formalism），采用Nédélec有限元（Nédélec finite elements）实现旋度一致性离散化（curl-conforming discretisation）以表述第二类超导体的非线性电磁响应。在脚本化Python工作流中，将切向场边界条件、非线性E-J幂律和全隐式时间离散残差显式陈述于变分水平（variational level）。该实现基于Firedrake平台，结合统一形式语言（UFL）和PETSc非线性求解器，同一脚本可在本地和Google Colab等浏览器环境无修改运行。

Result: 在圆柱超导体Bean态穿透条件下标准磁化基准测试中，开源工作流复现商业参考磁化回路的误差约在1%以内，相对峰值误差低于1.5%。在实用高溫超导Bi2212线材的独立COMSOL模型对比中，结果同样吻合。云端执行在免费且资源受限的硬件条件下，仅以适度增加的运行时开销保持了相同的数值解。

Conclusion: 所提出的H-cloud框架为实用超导体和功能超导体的模拟、基准测试和未来优化导向建模提供了一条严谨、可复现且便携的技术路线。该框架完全开源、可分享且在开放云环境中可直接执行，降低了超导体电磁建模的进入门槛，同时保持了对物理假设、边界条件和求解器结构的完全可见性。

Abstract: We present the H-cloud formalism, a cloud-accessible and open-source finite-element framework for electromagnetic modelling of applied superconductors. The proposed method expresses the nonlinear electromagnetic response of type-II superconductors in a curl-conforming discretisation based on Nédélec finite elements, where the tangential applied-field boundary condition, nonlinear E-J power law, and fully implicit time-discrete residual are stated explicitly at the variational level, all within a scripted Python finite-element workflow. The weak form is used as the basis for forward simulation and for extension to adjoint differentiation and PDE-constrained optimisation, while keeping the governing assumptions, boundary conditions, and solver structure fully visible to the user. The implementation is realised in Firedrake with UFL and PETSc-backed nonlinear solvers, allowing the identical script to run on local machines and in browser-accessible environments such as Google Colab without reformulating the problem. The method is verified on the canonical magnetisation benchmark of a cylindrical superconductor under Bean-like penetration conditions and then benchmarked against an independently constructed COMSOL model for a practical high temperature superconducting Bi2212 wire. Across matched mesh studies, the open-source workflow reproduces the commercial-reference magnetisation loops to within approximately \(1\%\) , with relative peak errors below 1.5%, while cloud execution preserves the same numerical solution at rather modest additional runtime considering the use of (freely available) reduced hardware resources. The proposed framework provides a rigorous, reproducible, and portable route for superconducting simulation, benchmarking, and future optimisation-led modelling of applied and functional superconductors, shareable and executable into open cloud environments.

</details>


### [96] [Tunable responsivity and bandwidth in microwave kinetic inductance detectors via readout current nonlinearity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09178)
*Maclean Rouble,Peter Day,Matt Dobbs,Joshua Montgomery,Sofiia Savchyn,Graeme Smecher*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了微波动力学电感探测器（MKIDs）在读入功率接近分叉点（bifurcation point）时，因非线性频率偏移（nonlinear frequency shift）导致的正反馈效应，实现了光响应提升约10倍，同时观察到谐振器带宽下降，并提供了通过调节激励选择反馈强度的操作状态图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MKIDs通常需要足够高的读入功率以抑制第一级放大器的噪声贡献，但在高功率下探测器谐振频率会因动力学电感（kinetic inductance）对内部循环微波电流的依赖而发生改变。本文旨在利用这种非线性频率偏移带来的正反馈效应来增强探测器的响应度（responsivity）。

Method: 将读入音调（readout tone）设置在谐振频率以下，通过调节读入功率和频率使其接近谐振器的分叉点，利用非线性频率偏移引发的正反馈效应增强探测器的光响应和微波功率响应。

Result: 实验实现了光学响应提升约10倍；同时观察到在此条件下谐振器的带宽（bandwidth）相应降低。研究表明，通过调整激励可以方便地选择反馈效应的强度，并提供了相应的可能操作状态图。

Conclusion: 当非本征噪声源（non-intrinsic noise sources）显著时，在此模式下运行MKIDs可用于提高探测灵敏度。反馈效应的强度可通过简单地调节激励来调整。

Abstract: Microwave kinetic inductance detectors (MKIDs) are generally read out with microwave readout tones of high enough amplitude to adequately suppress the noise contribution of the first-stage amplifier. At high readout power, the detector's resonant frequency is altered as a result of the dependence of the kinetic inductance on the internally circulating microwave current. With the tone placed below the resonant frequency, the nonlinear frequency shift results in a positive feedback effect that can significantly enhance the responsivity of the detector, to both optical and microwave power. We report a factor of 10 enhancement in optical response by tuning the readout power and frequency to close to the resonator's bifurcation point. A corresponding decrease in the bandwidth of the resonator is observed under these conditions. We show that the strength of the feedback effect can be easily selected by adjusting the excitation, and provide a map of possible operational states to do so. Operation of MKIDs in this mode could be used to improve sensitivity when non-intrinsic noise sources are significant.

*Younes Ghorbani,Samuel Poage,Xuehsi Gao,Luka Mitrovic,Neha Wadehra,Benjamin Gregory,Suchismita Sarker,Betul Pamuk,Andrej Singer,Darrell G. Schlom,Chun Ning Lau,Kaveh Ahadi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在TiO₂(100)和TiO₂(110)单晶衬底上外延生长RuO₂薄膜，沿不同晶向测量电子输运和超导电性。

Conclusion: 超导转变的各向异性行为和对Pauli顺磁极限的强违背表明强自旋-轨道散射（spin-orbit scattering）起关键作用，为外延工程化超导体的设计提供了新途径。

Abstract: The superconductivity in RuO2 emerges under strain. RuO2 is also an altermagnet candidate. The nature of superconductivity and its relation with neighboring orders, however, are not understood. To address this problem, we grew epitaxial RuO2 films on TiO2(100) and TiO2(110) single crystal substrates and studied the electronic transport and emergent superconductivity along various crystallographic directions. We show that the superconducting transition strongly depends on the growth orientation and the crystallographic direction of the transport in the RuO2 films. We also observe a strong violation of Pauli paramagnetic limit with in-plane applied magnetic field which we attribute to strong spin-orbit scattering. These results offer opportunities for epitaxially engineered superconductors.

### [98] [Action-Factored Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning for Scalable Quantum Device Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09422)
*Edwin De Nicolo,Rahul Marchand,Cornelius Carlsson,Pranav Vaidhyanathan,Natalia Ares*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出QADAPT框架，通过在线学习动作空间的因子化表示（factored representation）解耦多智能体，实现量子点阵列的无零样本泛化（zero-shot generalization）调谐，并在未见过尺寸的设备上保持恒定收敛步数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 合作式多智能体强化学习（cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning）适用于具有大参数空间和可剥削局部结构的问题（如量子点阵列调谐），但参数串扰（parameter cross-talk）会导致非平稳环境（non-stationary environment），使学习失稳，类似手动调谐中的困难。

Method: 提出QADAPT框架，在线学习动作空间的因子化表示，以解耦智能体（decouple agents）并最小化干扰；基于局部测量和奖励高效学习共享策略（shared policies）。

Result: 实现零样本泛化（zero-shot generalization）至未见过的量子设备尺寸；在达到目标区域所需的收敛步数（convergence steps）上保持近似恒定。

Conclusion: 该模块化策略为大规模量子处理器的快速校准提供了一条可扩展路径。

Abstract: Cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning is well suited to problems with large parameter spaces and exploitable local structure, such as the tuning of electrostatically-defined quantum-dot arrays. However, if parameter cross-talk is strong, a non-stationary environment from the perspective of any individual agent can destabilize learning - the same effect that plagues manual tuning of such systems. We propose using a factored representation of the action space, learned online, to decouple agents and minimize their interference. Our framework, QADAPT, uses this factorization to efficiently learn shared policies based on local measurements and rewards. With this modular strategy, we achieve zero-shot generalization to unseen quantum device sizes and maintain an approximately constant number of convergence steps to reach target regimes. This work provides a scalable route toward the rapid calibration of large-scale quantum processors.

### [99] [Transient Reserves, Sink Dampers, and the Failure of Eigenvalue Reasoning in the Attention Propagator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09279)
*Li Hengyu*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文基于非正规算子（non-normal operator）的预解式（resolvent）理论，系统分析了因果Transformer中注意力矩阵的有限深度瞬态动力学，发现注意力汇（attention sinks）扮演瞬态阻尼器角色，路由头（routing heads）携带超额瞬态储备，且特征值（eigenvalues）对深度乘积误差的预测偏差高达7-11个数量级，证明预解式特征是深度瞬态持久性和路由头身份的必要解释工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 因果Transformer中的注意力矩阵是行随机的，经过深度迭代且非正规。对于非正规算子，特征值仅控制渐近行为，有限深度行为则由预解量——如伪谱（pseudospectra）和Kreiss常数（Kreiss constants）——控制。本文旨在检验这一预解式视角是否能预测经过训练的Transformer中特征值无法捕捉的结构。

Method: 在预先注册的标准下，在GPT-2、Pythia-410m和Llama-3-8B三个模型上进行实验。分析方法基于两个结构事实：掩码将每个因果随机矩阵的Kreiss常数固定在√n；去偏掩码强制Perron投影因子将深度偏差动力学精确分解为去偏算子的乘积。通过检查点普查、夹止干预（clamping intervention）和交叉验证比较，系统评估预解式特征对瞬态动力学和路由头身份的预测能力。

Result: 学习到的非正规性是有符号的：路由少数（routing minority）携带超额瞬态储备，追踪前一个词元（previous-token）功能并在归纳头（induction heads）参与时加倍；汇多数（sink majority）被抑制到低于匹配混洗零假设的水平，注意力汇作为瞬态阻尼器。在深度乘积上，特征值对幸存偏差的预测误差达7-11个数量级，而匹配零假设中无此误差。检查点普查将这种组织定位于电路形成后的巩固阶段。

Conclusion: 预解式特征对于深度瞬态持久性和路由头身份是必需的，任何类型的单算子摘要都无法预测每个头的因果关键性（causal criticality）。对Llama-3-8B的夹止干预建立了从三个大规模激活维度通过汇注意力到瞬态阻尼的因果链；LayerNorm模型在其他位置实现相同功能。

Abstract: The attention matrix of a causal transformer is row-stochastic, iterated over depth, and non-normal by construction. For non-normal operators, eigenvalues control only asymptotic behavior; finite-depth behavior is controlled by resolvent quantities such as pseudospectra and Kreiss constants. We test, under pre-registered criteria, whether this resolvent view predicts anything about trained transformers that eigenvalues miss. Two structural facts organize the analysis: the mask pins the Kreiss constant of every causal stochastic matrix at $\sqrt{n}$, and deflating the mask-forced Perron projector factorizes the depth deviation dynamics exactly into a product of deflated operators. Across GPT-2, Pythia-410m, and Llama-3-8B, learned non-normality proves to be signed. A routing minority carries excess transient reserve that tracks previous-token function and doubles when induction heads engage, while the sink majority is suppressed below matched shuffle nulls, so that attention sinks act as transient dampers. On depth products, eigenvalue predictions of surviving deviations err by seven to eleven orders of magnitude, an error absent in matched nulls. Checkpoint censuses date this organization to a consolidation phase after circuit formation, and a clamping intervention on Llama-3-8B establishes a causal chain from three massive activation dimensions through sink attention to transient damping; LayerNorm models implement the same functions elsewhere. A cross-validated contest concludes that resolvent features are required for depth-transient persistence and routing-head identity, and that no single-operator summary of any kind predicts per-head causal criticality.

</details>


### [100] [Level statistics in the fractal phase of generalized Rosenzweig--Porter models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09444)
*Victor Delapalme,Leticia F. Cugliandolo,Alexander K. Hartmann,Marco Tarzia,Davide Venturelli*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了Rosenzweig-Porter随机矩阵系综的多种推广形式，利用自由概率论和复制方法计算了Thouless能量尺度下的全计数统计量，发现其具有普适标度形式，并通过数值对角化和大偏差算法验证了理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Rosenzweig-Porter（RP）随机矩阵系综是描述量子多体系统中可积性-混沌交叉（integrability-to-chaos crossover）的最小模型，其相图中存在具有分形本征态的中间区域。本文旨在探索RP模型的多种推广形式，并研究它们在Thouless能量尺度下的能级统计行为。

Method: 采用自由概率论（free probability theory）和复制方法（replica method）作为理论工具，在大系统尺寸极限下计算全计数统计量（full counting statistics）。数值验证方面，使用精确数值对角化（exact numerical diagonalization）和大偏差算法（large-deviation algorithms），将全计数统计量的计算概率分辨率拓展至10^{-40}量级。

Result: 全计数统计量在Thouless能量E_T附近呈现简单且普适的标度形式（universal scaling form），该形式在RP模型的所有推广变体中共享。数值结果与理论预测高度吻合，包括极低概率区域（最低至10^{-40}）的验证。此外，论文还将理论预测与量子随机能量模型（quantum random energy model）——展现多体局域化（many-body localization）的最简单模型——的测量结果进行了对比。

Conclusion: RP模型推广体系下的全计数统计量在Thouless能量尺度上具有普适标度行为，这一发现为理解量子混沌-局域化交叉提供了统一的理论框架。与多体局域化模型的对比分析进一步揭示了RP类模型与该领域核心问题的关联。

Abstract: The Rosenzweig--Porter (RP) random matrix ensemble has emerged as a minimal model for the integrability-to-chaos crossover in quantum many-body systems. Its phase diagram features a region with fractal eigenstates, exhibiting intermediate spectral and localization properties between the fully localized and fully delocalized regimes. In this work, we explore several generalizations of the RP model and determine their level statistics at the scale of the Thouless energy $E_T$, which characterizes the crossover. Using tools from free probability theory and the replica method, we compute the full counting statistics in the limit of large system size, and show that it takes a simple, universal scaling form around $E_T$, shared across all variations of the model. We validate our analytical predictions using exact numerical diagonalization of large samples, and large-deviation algorithms that resolve the full counting statistics down to probabilities as low as $10^{-40}$. We also contrast our predictions with measurements on the quantum random energy model, which is the simplest model displaying many-body localization.

</details>


### [101] [A multi-ensemble mean-field reduction method for networks of globally coupled phase oscillators with arbitrary parameter distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09516)
*Richard Gast,Shotaro Takasu,Helmut Schmidt,Ann Kennedy*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文针对耦合相振子系统（coupled phase oscillator systems），提出了一种适用于任意频率分布的均场约化方法（mean-field reduction method）。该方法将针对洛伦兹分布（Lorentzian frequency distributions）的强降维技巧与数据驱动的多系综方法（data-driven multi-ensemble approach）相结合，使Ott-Antonsen方程能够直接应用于经验频率分布，并实现降维后的稳定性、敏感性和分岔分析（bifurcation analyses）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解具有非均匀频率分布的耦合相振子系统的动力学特性是复杂系统理论中的一个长期难题。Ott和Antonsen的开创性工作虽然极大提升了理论理解，但仅适用于一小类频率分布，缺乏处理任意频率分布的一般性方法。

Method: 该方法利用洛伦兹分布下可实现的强维度约化（drastic dimensionality reduction），将其与数据驱动的多系综方法（data-driven multi-ensemble approach）结合。通过这种组合，使得原本局限于特定分布的Ott-Antonsen方程（Ott-Antonsen equations）能够推广到任意经验频率分布。

Result: 该方法能够对实际物理和生物系统中遇到的任意经验频率分布实现可观的维度约化，使得原本局限于特定分布的Ott-Antonsen方程可以直接用于此类系统。

Conclusion: 该均场约化方法使得对真实世界物理和生物系统进行稳定性分析（stability analysis）、敏感性分析（sensitivity analysis）和分岔分析成为可能，从而拓展了相振子系统理论分析的实际应用范围。

Abstract: Understanding the dynamical properties of coupled phase oscillator systems with heterogeneous oscillator frequencies has been a long-standing challenge of complex systems theory. While the seminal work of Ott and Antonsen dramatically improved our theoretical understanding of coupled phase oscillators for a small family of oscillator frequency distributions, we here present a mean-field reduction method for arbitrary frequency distributions. Our method leverages the drastic dimensionality reduction obtained for Lorentzian frequency distributions, and combines it with a data-driven multi-ensemble approach. As such, the method renders the Ott-Antonsen equations directly applicable to empirical distributions of phase oscillator frequencies, often achieving a drastic dimensionality reduction and allowing to study real-world physical and biological systems by means of stability, sensitivity, and bifurcation analyses.

### [102] [Molecular Tuning of Charge-Transfer Resonance in Plasmonic Nanocavities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08927)
*Hasher Irshada,Francesco Ciccarello,Konstantin Malchow,Christophe Galland,Katrine Qvortrup*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过构建等离激元纳米粒子-镜面结（plasmonic nanoparticle-on-mirror junctions），结合表面增强拉曼散射（SERS）、振动和频产生光谱（vSFG）与密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，系统研究了分子-金属纳米腔中界面电荷转移共振（charge-transfer resonance）的能量条件，发现拉曼散射的电荷转移增强受一个依赖于衬底功函数和激发能的明确界面共振条件调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 界面电荷转移过程在等离激元增强光谱学中至关重要，但分子-金属纳米腔中调控电荷转移共振的能量条件尚不明确，亟需系统性实验与理论结合的研究来阐明其机制。

Method: 采用等离激元纳米粒子-镜面结结构，嵌入系统设计的联苯硫醇衍生物单分子层；通过SERS、vSFG光谱及DFT计算，结合不同激发波长、衬底组成与分子电子结构的系统变化，定量评估等离激元增强电荷转移激发与分子轨道排列之间的能量关系。

Result: 电荷转移增强的拉曼散射受一个明确的界面共振条件调控，该条件依赖于衬底功函数和激发能量；在SERS和vSFG中观察到相同的共振条件，验证了该框架的一致性。

Conclusion: 建立了可实验操作的框架，用于探测和工程化等离激元分子结中的电荷转移过程，为分子等离激元学（molecular plasmonics）、电荷载流子光物理及纳米尺度界面光谱学提供了机制性见解。

Abstract: Interfacial charge-transfer processes play a critical role in plasmon-enhanced spectroscopy, yet the energetic conditions governing charge-transfer resonance within molecule-metal nanocavities remain poorly understood. Here, plasmonic nanoparticle-on-mirror junctions incorporating systematically engineered biphenylthiol derivatives monolayers were used to investigate how frontier orbital alignment influences chemical enhancement mechanisms. A molecular library spanning a broad range of electronically tuned acceptor states was examined using surface-enhanced Raman scattering (SERS), vibrational sum frequency generation (vSFG) spectroscopy, and density functional theory calculations. By combining different excitation wavelengths with controlled variation of substrate composition and molecular electronic structure, the energetic relationship between plasmon-enhanced charge transfer excitation and molecular orbital alignment was quantitatively evaluated. The results reveal that charge-transfer enhancement of Raman scattering is governed by a well-defined interfacial resonance condition dependent on substrate work function and excitation energy. We further probe a subset of molecular-metal systems by nanocavity-enhanced vSFG and identify the same resonance conditions as in SERS, consistent with expectations. These findings establish an experimentally accessible framework for probing and engineering charge-transfer processes in plasmonic molecular junctions and provide mechanistic insight relevant to molecular plasmonics, charge carrier photophysics, and nanoscale interfacial spectroscopy.

</details>


### [103] [Quantum phases in endofullerene zigzag chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09396)
*Tobias Serwatka,Muhammad Shaeer Moeed,Roger G. Melko,Pierre-Nicholas Roy*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group）计算，研究了弯曲（锯齿形）内嵌富勒烯链中偶极分子的量子相，发现链角γ从60°到180°时LiF呈现铁电序，在γ=60°附近几何阻挫（geometric frustration）驱动反铁电Néel序转变，并指出捕获该重取向需超越最近邻偶极耦合近似；水分子中o-D2O再现两种有序相，而p-H2O因大转动常数（rotational constants）在任何链角下均不形成有序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索弯曲（锯齿形）内嵌富勒烯链中偶极分子的量子相行为，特别是链角γ对有序相的影响，以揭示几何阻挫和偶极耦合范围在量子相变（quantum phase transition）中的作用。

Method: 采用大规模密度矩阵重整化群（density matrix renormalization group, DMRG）计算，系统扫描链角γ（60°到180°）和有效偶极矩参数，并考虑超越最近邻（nearest-neighbor）的偶极耦合贡献。

Result: LiF在60°<γ≤180°范围内保持铁电序（ferroelectric order），临界有效偶极矩随链弯曲而增大；γ=60°等边构型附近出现反铁电Néel序（antiferroelectric Néel-ordered phase），且该重取向要求包含次近邻（next-nearest-neighbor）偶极耦合。o-D2O重现两种有序相，而p-H2O因大转动常数在任何链角下均不形成有序。

Conclusion: 弯曲几何增强了配位效应，但能否形成偶极有序相取决于分子的转动自由度；由于锯齿形链是二维晶格的最窄条带，内嵌富勒烯层（endofullerene layers）可能承载远超以往铁电序的丰富偶极有序量子相。

Abstract: We employ large-scale density matrix renormalization group calculations to study the quantum phases of dipolar molecules confined in bent (zigzag) endofullerene chains, as a function of the chain angle $γ$. For LiF, ferroelectric order persists across the full range $60^\circ < γ180^\circ$, with the critical effective dipole moment increasing as the chain bends and parallel alignment becomes less favorable. Near the equilateral configuration ($γ= 60^\circ$), geometric frustration drives a transition to an antiferroelectric Néel-ordered phase in which neighboring dipoles anti-align along the chain axis. We show that capturing this reorientation requires including dipolar couplings beyond the nearest-neighbor approximation, since next-nearest-neighbor interactions become equally strong at $γ= 60^\circ$. For confined water, o-D$_2$O reproduces both ordered phases, whereas p-H$_2$O -- owing to its large rotational constants -- develops no order at any chain angle despite the enhanced coordination of the bent geometry. Because a zigzag chain is the narrowest stripe of a two-dimensional lattice, these results suggest that engineered endofullerene layers could host a rich variety of dipole-ordered quantum phases beyond the ferroelectric ordering observed in previous work.

</details>

### [104] [A strong-coupling theory for polarizable symmetrically charged walls with counterions only](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08851)
*Ladislav Šamaj,Alexandre P. dos Santos,Emmanuel Trizac*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文针对平行极化平面壁间的对称带电体系，在强耦合（strong-coupling, SC）区研究了由反离子介导的有效壁间相互作用（压力）随距离的依赖关系。提出了一种基于维格纳（Wigner）单层或双层结构的SC理论，克服了以往维里（virial）SC单粒子理论在中大介电跳变下的不足，并通过蒙特卡洛（Monte-Carlo）模拟验证了理论在介观耦合常数（Ξ > 10）下的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往维里SC单粒子理论仅在距离d小且介电跳变小时有效，在中等或大介电跳变下即使处于SC区域也表现不足。本文旨在提出一种新的SC理论，以更准确地描述反离子介导的壁间有效相互作用。

Method: 提出维格纳型SC理论（Wigner-type SC theory），将粒子视为在其基态单层或双层维格纳结构（Wigner structures）附近作简谐偏离（harmonic deviations），并采用蒙特卡洛（Monte-Carlo）模拟进行验证。

Result: 蒙特卡洛模拟结果与维格纳SC理论预测在介观耦合常数Ξ > 10时表现出很好的一致性，表明该理论即使在中等耦合常数下也适用。

Conclusion: 所提出的维格纳型强耦合理论能够有效弥补以往维里SC理论在中大介电跳变下的不足，为处理介电壁间反离子体系的相互作用提供更可靠的理论框架。

Abstract: A pair of parallel polarizable planar walls at distance d is considered. The walls are symmetrically charged with a uniform surface charge density, neutralized by mobile point counterions moving between them. The case of repulsive particle images is studied in the strong-coupling (SC) regime. Of interest is the dependence of the effective inter-wall interaction (pressure), mediated by the mobile counterions, as a function of the distance d. It is shown that previous virial SC single-particle theories work well at small d when the dielectric jump is small; for intermediate and large dielectric jumps they are inadequate even in the SC region. Here, we propose a Wigner-type SC theory based on harmonic deviations of particles from their ground-state monolayer or bilayer Wigner structures formed inside the space between the dielectric walls. Our Monte-Carlo simulations are in very good agreement with the Wigner SC predictions, even down to moderate coupling constants ($Ξ> 10$).

</details>


### [105] [Generic behavior of ultrastability and anisotropic molecular packing in co-deposited organic semiconductor glass mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08889)
*Shinian Cheng,Yejung Lee,Junguang Yu,Lian Yu,Mark D. Ediger*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过实验测量六种共沉积有机半导体玻璃混合物（50:50重量比）的热稳定性和各向异性分子堆积，发现所有二元体系均表现出高动力学稳定性和显著降低的焓（超稳定行为），且混合物的双折射可由两种纯组分玻璃的双折射预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有机电子器件的寿命和性能受到其活性层（气相沉积有机半导体玻璃混合物）稳定性和结构的强烈影响，理解这些混合玻璃的稳定性和分子堆积结构对于器件设计至关重要。

Method: 采用差示扫描量热法（differential scanning calorimetry）和光谱椭圆偏振法（spectroscopic ellipsometry），对六种50:50重量比的共沉积有机半导体玻璃混合物进行热稳定性及各向异性分子堆积的表征。

Result: 所有六种二元体系均表现出高动力学稳定性和显著低于相应液冷玻璃混合物的焓（即超稳定行为），即使两组分的玻璃化转变温度相差超过90 K时依然成立；此外，共沉积玻璃混合物的双折射（各向异性堆积的度量）可由两种纯组分玻璃的双折射预测。

Conclusion: 这些关于稳定性和结构的结果预计适用于其他共沉积有机半导体玻璃混合物，前提是两组分在玻璃中混合良好且各自能形成超稳定玻璃，因此该发现对设计具有更长器件寿命和更高运行效率的新型电子器件具有重要意义。

Abstract: Vapor-deposited glass mixtures of organic semiconductors commonly serve as active layers in organic electronic devices, whose lifetime and performance are strongly influenced by the stability and structure of these mixed glasses. Here, we study the stability and anisotropic molecular packing of six co-deposited organic semiconductor glass mixtures with 50:50 weight ratio, by differential scanning calorimetry and spectroscopic ellipsometry. We find that all six binary systems exhibit high kinetic stability and significantly reduced enthalpy relative to the corresponding liquid-cooled glassy mixtures (ultrastable behavior), even for systems where the glass transition temperatures of the components differ by more than 90 K. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the birefringence of a co-deposited glass mixture, a measure of its anisotropic packing, can be predicted from the birefringence of glasses of the two pure components. These results for stability and structure are expected to be applicable to other co-deposited organic semiconductor glass mixtures, so long as the two components mix well in the glass and individually can form ultrastable glasses. Therefore, our findings are significant for designing novel electronic devices with enhanced device lifetime and increased operational efficiency.

### [106] [Shear Unfreezing Explains Yielding, Plasticity and Neck Initiation of Glassy Polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09160)
*Peihan Lyu,Zhaoyu Ding,Masao Doi,Xingkun Man*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文基于 Doolittle 方程和 Onsager 变分原理（Onsager variational principle）发展了一个玻璃态聚合物（glassy polymers）的极简理论，通过剪切解除冻结（shear unfreezing）机制统一解释了屈服（yielding）、塑性（plasticity）和颈缩（necking）等非线性力学响应，并给出了屈服应力的解析表达式和颈缩起始的相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管材料的屈服、塑性和颈缩对其力学性能至关重要，但目前仍缺乏一个简洁统一的物理图景来解释这些非线性响应是如何产生的。

Method: 基于 Doolittle 方程构建一个依赖于体积（volume-dependent）的松弛时间（relaxation time）的极简理论，并利用 Onsager 变分原理推导本构关系（constitutive relation）。

Result: 该理论通过剪切解除冻结机制解释了恒定应变率加载下的屈服、塑性和颈缩起始；推导出了屈服应力作为应变率和温度函数的解析表达式；并在同一参数空间中预测了颈缩起始的相图，提供了超越经典 Considère 准则（Considère criterion）的机制。

Conclusion: 该工作为玻璃态材料的非线性拉伸行为建立了一个统一的理论框架。

Abstract: Yielding, plasticity, and necking are central to the mechanical performance of materials, yet a concise unified physical picture of how these nonlinear responses arise remains lacking. We develop a minimal theory for glassy polymers based on a classical volume-dependent relaxation time following the Doolittle equation, and derive the constitutive relation using the Onsager variational principle. Surprisingly, this simple theory explains yielding, plasticity, and neck initiation under constant strain rate loading via a shear unfreezing mechanism: as the sample is stretched, volume-increasing activated molecular mobility drives shear deformation from an initially frozen state to an unfrozen state. The theory yields an analytical expression for the yielding stress as a function of strain rate and temperature. It also predicts a phase diagram for necking initiation in the same parameter space, providing a mechanism beyond the classical Considère criterion. Our results establish a unified framework for nonlinear tensile behavior in glassy materials.

The model is validated using solid lipid nanoparticles labeled with several BODIPY dyes. This experimental validation paves the way for quantitative PA characterization of nanomaterials and rational design of PA contrast agents.

### [108] [Dispersion Polymerization in an Elastomeric Solvent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09387)
*Senthilkumar Duraivel,Reagan J Dreiling,Tyler E Ball,Harsha Koganti,Jay Fu,Ethan E. O'Banion,Brett P. Fors,Eric R. Dufresne*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一种弹性介导的聚合诱导相分离（elastically mediated PIPS）新机制，通过在可变形弹性体网络中进行受控聚合，建立了固态分散聚合方法——弹性体溶剂分散聚合（DiPolES），成功制备了尺寸和形状可控的聚合物微球。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统液相聚合成像诱导相分离（PIPS）受限于溶剂兼容性和形态多样性，难以同时实现微球制备与形态调控。

Method: 将光引发转移终止剂介导的聚合（photoiniferter-mediated polymerization）引入聚二甲基硅氧烷（PDMS）弹性体网络中，以弹性体网络同时充当溶剂和物理稳定剂，实现固态分散聚合（DiPolES）。

Result: 成功制备了粒径0.85–3微米、形状为球形或椭球形的均匀PMMA微球；该方法可推广至丙烯腈、2-乙烯基吡啶等多种单体；实时成像显示粒子形成经历快速成核和生长伴随网络空化过程；单体负载控制粒径，弹性体网络弹性调节粒子从孤立球体向异质簇的转变；施加单轴应变可直接制备椭球形粒子。

Conclusion: DiPolES是一种通用、可扩展的固态分散聚合策略，突破了传统液相PIPS的限制，为制备形态可控的弹性体复合材料和微球提供了新路径。

Abstract: Polymerization-induced phase separation (PIPS) provides a powerful route to generate structured polymeric materials by coupling chemical conversion with thermodynamic demixing. PIPS in liquid-state systems underlies dispersion polymerization, serving as a cornerstone technique for microparticle production, yet is constrained by solvent compatibility and limited range of morphologies. Here, we establish an elastically mediated PIPS regime that bridges these two limits by conducting controlled polymerization within a deformable elastomeric network. This approach, termed Dispersion Polymerization in an Elastomeric Solvent (DiPolES), serves as a solid-state analogue of dispersion polymerization in which an elastomeric network simultaneously serves as solvent and physical stabilizer. Using photoiniferter-mediated polymerization of methyl methacrylate (MMA) within poly(dimethyl siloxane) (PDMS) elastomeric solvent, DiPolES enables robust fabrication of elastomeric composites containing uniform PMMA microparticles with tunable size (0.85 to 3 μm) and shape (spheroidal and ellipsoidal). The strategy is generalizable beyond the PDMS/MMA system and is applicable to diverse monomers, such as acrylonitrile and 2-vinyl pyridine, which can be extracted from the elastomeric solvent, enabling high-yield production of microparticles. Real-time imaging and compositional analysis reveal that particle formation proceeds through rapid nucleation at low monomer conversion, followed by growth accompanied by cavitation of the surrounding network. Monomer loading governs the particle size, while solvent elasticity modulates the transition from isolated uniform spheroids to heterogeneous clusters. Interestingly, applying uniaxial strain during DiPolES enables production of ellipsoidal particles without any post-processing.

</details>


### [109] [Universal scaling of conformations of tangentially driven ring polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09436)
*Antonio Lamura,Marisol Ripoll*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过布朗动力学（Brownian Dynamics）模拟，本研究发现吸附在表面的环形聚合物（ring polymers）由于切向活动性（tangential activity）与排除体积相互作用（excluded-volume interactions）的共同作用，会整体膨胀，这与三维线性或环形聚合物因活性诱导坍缩的行为截然不同。该膨胀行为可由依赖于活性的Flory指数（Flory exponent）普遍标度化，且高活性下有效持久长度（effective persistence length）可表征柔性活性环的构象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
