Method: 采用布朗动力学（Brownian Dynamics）模拟方法，研究表面吸附活性环形聚合物在不同活性水平下的构象统计特性。

Result: 活性环在表面因切向活动性和排除体积相互作用而整体膨胀，与三维线性及环形聚合物活性诱导坍缩形成鲜明对比；该膨胀行为可通过与活性相关的Flory指数（Flory exponent）进行普适标度化描述；高活性下，活性柔性环的构象可用有效持久长度（effective persistence length）表征。

Conclusion: 活性环聚合物在受限表面环境下的膨胀行为与三维体系中的坍缩行为完全不同，表明空间维度与几何约束显著改变活性聚合物的标度性质；活性依赖的Flory指数和有效持久长度提供了普适的定量描述框架。

Abstract: The interplay of tangential activity and excluded-volume interactions in ring polymers adsorbed to a surface, consistently results in the overall swelling of the ring configurations. This is in strong contrast to the case for three dimensional linear and ring polymers, where activity induces frequently collapsed structures. By means of Brownian Dynamic simulations, we investigate how the scaling properties of such active rings can be universally characterized by an activity-dependent Flory exponent, as a generalization of the equilibrium behavior. At high activity, an effective persistence length characterizes the conformations of active flexible rings.

</details>


### [110] [A Boosted Energy Extraction from the CapMix Process by Grafting with Titratable Polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09554)
*Mamta Yadav,Clifford E. Woodward,Jan Forsman*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过接枝可滴定聚合物（titrating polymers）到电极表面，利用电容混合（capacitive mixing）技术，在无需膜的条件下显著提升盐度梯度能的捕获效率。通过大正则蒙特卡洛模拟和经典聚合物密度泛函理论计算，揭示了离子吸附与电荷调节（charge regulation）的耦合机制，并验证了该策略在废水处理中同步回收能源的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 盐度梯度能（salinity gradient energy）可将离子化学势差（chemical potential differences）转化为可用电能，是可持续能源的重要来源。电容混合（capacitive mixing）技术无需膜即可实现该转化，但其性能受限于电极界面的离子调控能力。因此，亟需开发新方法以强化电极界面的离子调节能力，提升能量转换效率。

Method: 在电极表面接枝可滴定聚合物，用电容混合（capacitive mixing）方式实现能量转换。采用大正则蒙特卡洛（Grand Canonical Monte Carlo, GCMC）模拟，并结合精确镜像电荷埃瓦尔德求和（exact image-charge Ewald summations）。同时运用经典聚合物密度泛函理论（classical polymer Density Functional Theory, DFT）进行补充计算，验证机制的可靠性。

Result: 接枝聚合物电极相较于裸电极输出显著更高的能量，驱动力来源于电荷调节（charge regulation）效应对河水和海洋之间pH差异的利用。该效应在高接枝密度（high grafting densities）和适中链长（moderate chain lengths）时达到最优，且在合理参数范围内表现出较好的鲁棒性（robustness）。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了在废水处理（如酸性或碱性废水）中同步回收电能的实际方法，将环境修复（environmental remediation）与可再生能源回收（renewable energy recovery）相结合，为盐度梯度能的高效捕获提供了有前景的策略。

Abstract: Salinity gradient energy offers a sustainable route to convert ionic chemical potential differences into usable power. Capacitive mixing enables this conversion without membranes, but suffers from limited ion regulation at electrode interfaces. Here we show that by grafting electrode surfaces with titrating polymers, the performance can be substantially improved. Using Grand Canonical Monte Carlo simulations with exact image-charge Ewald summations, we demonstrate how the coupled effects of ion adsorption and charge regulation in response to an external potential can be harnessed. Grafted electrodes are shown to deliver substantially more energy relative to bare surfaces, driven by charge regulation effects that exploit the pH difference that typically exists between rivers and the ocean. While the effect is in principle maximized at high grafting densities and moderate chain lengths, the performance is fairly robust to variations of these parameters, within reasonable bounds. Complementary classical polymer Density Functional Theory calculations confirm these trends, validating the mechanistic framework. This work also establishes a practical approach to harvest electrical energy during wastewater neutralization, where acidic (or alkaline) effluents serve as complementary reservoirs, and offers a promising strategy to couple environmental remediation with renewable energy recovery.

</details>


### [111] [Delayed Arm Retraction Controls the Nonlinear Oscillatory Response of Long-Chain-Branched Polymer Melts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09561)
*Dario Nichetti,Alessio Zaccone*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一种分子管子理论（molecular tube theory），通过引入支点力传递（branch-point force transmission）和延迟的臂回缩（delayed arm retraction）机制，解释了长链支化聚合物（long-chain-branched polymers）在非线性振荡响应中出现的非线性指数（Nonlinearity Index, NLI）特征最大值现象，并揭示了该峰值源于主链取向与支臂松弛之间的竞争。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长链支化（long-chain branching）会显著改变缠结聚合物熔体的非线性振荡响应，但此前缺乏能够解释实验中观测到的非线性指数（NLI）特征最大值的分子理论。

Method: 在线性聚合物非线性管子取向描述（nonlinear tube-orientation description）的基础上进行扩展，引入支点力传递（branch-point force transmission）和延迟的臂回缩（delayed arm retraction）两个关键机制，构建分子管子理论（molecular tube theory）。

Result: 理论成功预测了NLI先出现特征最大值随后衰减的行为，并识别出稀疏与密集两种不同的长链支化非线性区域；同时引入一个结构参数（architecture parameter），用于调控非线性峰的高度和宽度。

Conclusion: 该理论框架为非线性傅里叶流变学（nonlinear Fourier rheology）提供了分子层面的解释，直接将非线性谐波响应（nonlinear harmonic response）与聚合物结构（polymer architecture）联系起来。

Abstract: Long-chain branching profoundly modifies the nonlinear oscillatory response of entangled polymer melts by introducing arm-retraction pathways absent in linear polymers. We present a molecular tube theory that explains the characteristic maximum of the Nonlinearity Index (NLI) observed experimentally in long-chain-branched polymers. The theory extends the recently developed nonlinear tube-orientation description of linear polymers by incorporating branch-point force transmission and delayed arm retraction. The backbone initially develops nonlinear orientation as in the corresponding linear polymer, whereas long-arm retraction subsequently relaxes the stored branch-point tension and progressively erases backbone orientational memory. This competition produces a characteristic NLI maximum followed by a post-peak decay. The theory predicts two distinct nonlinear regimes corresponding to sparse and dense long-chain branching and introduces an architecture parameter governing the height and width of the nonlinear peak. The resulting framework provides a molecular interpretation of nonlinear Fourier rheology and directly links the nonlinear harmonic response to polymer architecture.

</details>

### [112] [Higgsless Lagrangian SCFTs and Strongly Finite VOAs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08813)
*Siqi Chen,Anirudh Deb,Leonardo Rastelli*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过SCFT/VOA对应关系，从四维N=2超共形场论中分类并构造了新的强有限但对数顶点算子代数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强有限但非有理顶点算子代数（VOAs）的已知例子极少，这阻碍了相关数学理论的发展；SCFT/VOA对应关系为此类VOA的生成提供了自然途径。

Method: 利用SCFT/VOA对应关系，对不具有Higgs分支模空间（Higgs branch moduli space）的四维N=2拉格朗日超共形场论（SCFTs）进行组合分类，并从中构造对应的顶点算子代数。

Result: “无Higgs”拉格朗日SCFT的集合极为稀疏：除自由矢量多重态及其离散规范群（discrete gaugings）外，仅包含一个SO/USp箭图（quiver）无穷序列和三个零星例子；对其中两个零星例子构造了VOA，验证其为强有限且对数的。

Conclusion: 该分类结果为强有限但对数VOA提供了新的具体构造，丰富了该非半单表示范畴的理论研究素材。

Abstract: Vertex operator algebras (VOAs) are well studied in both mathematics and physics. The best understood class is that of strongly rational VOAs, whose representation category is maximally well behaved: indeed, it is a modular tensor category. At the next level of complexity are strongly finite but non-rational VOAs. Their representation category is not semisimple (it is ``logarithmic''), but maintains nice structural properties. Only a few families of examples in this class are known, a fact that may have hindered the development of a comprehensive mathematical theory. The SCFT/VOA correspondence provides a natural way to generate more examples: strongly finite but non-rational VOAs are expected to arise from four-dimensional ${\cal N}=2$ Lagrangian superconformal field theories (SCFTs) that do not admit a Higgs branch moduli space of vacua. We tackle the combinatorial task of classifying all such ``Higgsless'' Lagrangian SCFTs. To our surprise, this set turns out to be rather sparse. Free vector multiplets and their discrete gaugings are immediate examples. The interacting Higgsless theories comprise one infinite sequence of SO/USp quivers and three sporadic examples. We construct and study the novel VOAs associated to two of the sporadic examples, and confirm that they are indeed strongly finite and logarithmic.

</details>


### [113] [Anomaly mediation in Seiberg-Witten theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08903)
*Cyrus Tearlach Robertson Orkish,Daniel Stolarski*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了反常介导的超对称破缺（AMSB）耦合到具有SU(2)规范群的𝒩=2超对称理论。尽管在微扰描述中AMSB项等价于一个超对称质量项并保持𝒩=1超对称性（SUSY），但非微扰瞬子贡献完全破坏了超对称性。在红外（IR）描述中，理论与𝒩=1类比类似，出现单极凝聚和禁闭，但有效拉格朗日量完全破坏超对称性，且凝聚体值不同。在一定合理假设下，当超对称破缺标度越过强耦合标度时，真空必须改变为微扰上相同的𝒩=1保持形变对应的真空，这种变化无法由弱耦合有效IR理论描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究反常介导的超对称破缺（AMSB）耦合到具有SU(2)规范群的𝒩=2超对称理论时，非微扰效应如何影响超对称性的保持与破缺，以及真空构型和全局对称性的变化。

Method: 通过微扰分析（AMSB项等价于伴随手征多重态的𝒩=1超对称质量项）与非微扰瞬子贡献（instanton contributions）相结合的方法，对比紫外（UV）和红外（IR）描述，分析超对称破缺、单极凝聚（monopole condensation）和真空结构变化。

Result: 非微扰瞬子贡献完全破坏了超对称性；红外描述中有效拉格朗日量完全破坏超对称性，凝聚体值与𝒩=1类比不同；当超对称破缺标度越过强耦合标度时，真空必须改变为微扰上相同的𝒩=1保持形变的真空，但该变化无法由弱耦合有效IR理论描述，且并非相变（phase transition），真空在任意有限超对称破缺标度下处于同一普适类（universality class）。

Conclusion: 反常介导的超对称破缺与非微扰效应的耦合可以微妙地改变理论的真空场构型和全局对称性，即使理论与𝒩=1类比在红外定性相似，但超对称性完全破缺且真空结构存在本质差异。

Abstract: We study the coupling of anomaly mediated supersymmetry breaking (AMSB) to $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric theories with $SU(2)$ gauge group. Perturbatively, $\mathcal{N}=1$ supersymmetry (SUSY) is preserved in the UV description with the AMSB terms being equivalent to a supersymmetric mass term for the adjoint chiral multiplet, as considered in the original Seiberg-Witten papers. We show, however, that nonperturbative instanton contributions break supersymmetry completely. In the IR description, the theory with AMSB is qualitatively similar to its $\mathcal{N}=1$ analog, exhibiting monopole condensation and confinement. However, the effective Lagrangian breaks supersymmetry completely, and the values of the condensates are different from their $\mathcal{N}=1$ analogs. Under physically reasonable assumptions, it can be shown that the vacua must change to those of the perturbatively identical $\mathcal{N}=1$-preserving deformation as the SUSY-breaking scale crosses the strong coupling scale. This change must be caused by effects that cannot in principle be described within the effective weakly coupled IR theory. It is not a phase transition, and the vacua appear to lie in the same universality class at any finite SUSY-breaking scale. Nonetheless, this work highlights the subtle manner in which AMSB coupling to nonperturbative effects can change the vacuum field configuration and the global symmetries of a theory.

</details>

*Armen Poghosyan,Hasmik Poghosyan*

Method: 从Liouville理论和A₂ Toda理论中环面上一点共形块的Zamolodchikov类递归关系出发，推导其在光渐近极限下的递归关系。

Result: 在Liouville理论中，光极限递归重现了已知的高斯超几何函数表达。在A₂ Toda理论中，该递归提供了一种高效的新计算方法，且与文献已有结果完全一致。

Abstract: In this paper, we review the Zamolodchikov-like recursion relations for torus one-point conformal blocks in both Liouville and $A_2$ Toda theories. Starting from these relations, we derive the corresponding recursion relations in the light asymptotic limit. In Liouville theory, the light-limit recursion reproduces the known expression for the one-point light conformal block in terms of the Gauss hypergeometric function. For $A_2$ Toda theory, our recursion relation provides a new, efficient method for explicit calculations, and we have verified that it is in full agreement with previously known results in the literature.

### [115] [Cherednik integrable system: eigenfunctions at generic eigenvalues](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09203)
*A. Mironov,A. Morozov,A. Popolitov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文展示了对N体Cherednik可积系统（由A型DAHA启发）构建通解的方法，其通解含有N!支幂级数，每支与Noumi-Shiraishi类型的幂级数类似，但整体结构比对称Macdonald多项式情形更为复杂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对称Macdonald多项式（symmetric Macdonald polynomials）仅在特定本征值下为N体三角Ruijsenaars-Schneider可积系统的本征函数；为了构造任意本征值下的本征函数，Noumi和Shiraishi通过递归与解析延拓得到了一个幂级数解（即三元组中的通用解）。本文旨在将这一方法推广到另一可积系统——由A型DAHA（double affine Hecke algebra）启发的N体Cherednik系统。

Method: 采用与Noumi-Shiraishi类似的递归（分支规则，branching rule）与解析延拓（analytic continuation）程序，对非对称Macdonald多项式（non-symmetric Macdonald polynomials）情形进行处理。

Result: Cherednik系统的通用本征函数具有更复杂的结构：其包含N!个分支，每个分支均为Noumi-Shiraishi类型的幂级数，而非像对称Macdonald情形中那样仅为一个简单的幂级数。文中还给出了特定情形下的显式公式作为示例。

Conclusion: Noumi-Shiraishi方法可推广至Cherednik系统，但所得通解结构更为复杂（多分支幂级数），这反映了非对称Macdonald多项式与对称Macdonald多项式之间的本质差异。

Abstract: Symmetric Macdonald polynomials of $n$ variables provide eigenfunctions of the $N$-body trigonometric Ruijsenaars-Schneider integrable system at particular eigenvalues. In order to construct eigenfunctions with arbitrary eigenvalues, M. Noumi and J. Shiraishi used a recursion in $N$ (branching rule) for the symmetric Macdonald polynomials and analytically continued them. This generated a power series, which is a part of triad (universal solution). In the present paper, we demonstrate that a similar procedure is available for another integrable system, $N$-body Cherednik system inspired by the DAHA of type $A$, which has non-symmetric Macdonald polynomials as its polynomial eigenfunctions. However, in this system, the generic eigenfunction is more complicated: it is not just a simple power series as in the Noumi-Shiraishi case, but has an involved structure with $N!$ branches, each of them being a power series of the Noumi-Shiraishi type. As an illustration, we also provide explicit formulas for particular cases.

</details>


### [116] [Quantum field nucleating and Wigner functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09233)
*Joonas Hirvonen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 提出一种基于维格纳函数（Wigner function）的实时间框架，用于描述量子场论（quantum field theory）中亚稳态（metastable state）的衰变，并导出一个包含量子隧穿（quantum tunneling）和跨垒成核（over-the-barrier nucleation）的非微扰成核率公式。应用于一个与当前模拟实验相关的简单热学例子后，发现其一圈修正结果与 Linde 的高温公式本质不同，而是 Affleck 公式在量子场论中的推广，并在高温极限下退化为有效场论（effective field theory）和 Langer 的经典成核率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有描述热真空衰变（thermal vacuum decay）的成核率公式（如 Linde 的高温结果）缺少对量子效应的完整考虑，且“量子—经典”转变的物理本质存在争议。需要发展一个能够统一描述量子隧穿与经典热成核、并在非微扰水平上给出正确预言的实时框架。

Method: 利用维格纳函数构建量子场论中亚稳态衰变的实时描述，引入非微扰的成核率公式，并结合微扰展开进行逐阶评估；随后将其应用于一个与模拟实验相关的简单热学例子，计算一圈（one-loop）修正。

Result: 得到的一圈成核率公式与 Linde 的高温结果存在本质差异：其前因子（prefactor）包含量子效应，且在高温下渐近为另一种形式；该公式是 Affleck 成核率公式在量子场论中的推广，并在高温极限下退化为有效场论方法和 Langer 经典成核率。此外，结果揭示“量子—经典”转变的高温侧本质上仍是量子力学的，尽管其瞬子（bounce）背景具有经典的 O(d)×S¹ 对称性。

Conclusion: 所提实时框架能够更完整地描述量子场论中亚稳态衰变，修正了 Linde 高温公式的局限性；热真空衰变中“量子—经典”转变的高温端仍然保留量子力学本质，对理解经典与量子成核的边界具有重要理论意义。

Abstract: We present a novel real-time framework for the decay of metastable states in quantum field theories using Wigner functions. The framework introduces a nonperturbative nucleation rate formula that captures both quantum tunneling and over-the-barrier nucleation, alongside steps to evaluate it perturbatively. We apply it to a simple thermal example with direct relevance to current analog experiments. Our derived one-loop nucleation rate fundamentally differs from the widely cited high-temperature result by Linde: The prefactor contains quantum effects and also asymptotes to a differing form at high temperatures, where the quantum effects become negligible. Rather, the result is a generalization of Affleck's rate formula to quantum field theories, asymptoting to the effective field theory approach, and Langer's rate, at high temperatures. The example also reveals that the high-temperature side of the ``quantum-to-classical'' transition of thermal vacuum decay is still inherently quantum mechanical, even though the bounce background possesses the classical, $\mathrm{O}(d)\times S^1$, symmetry.

</details>

Method: 采用 Fefferman-Graham 展开（Fefferman-Graham expansion）在有限截断曲面附近进行分析，从“复杂性=任何事物”框架出发推导出形变对广义复杂性的修正。

Abstract: This work is motivated by the proposed relationship among finite cut-off holography and generalized $T\bar T$ deformations, and examines holographic complexity within the framework of the "complexity = anything" proposal. Employing a Fefferman-Graham expansion near the finite cut-off surface, the deformation-induced correction to generalized complexity is derived and shown to allow a systematic expansion in terms of generalized Willmore-type functionals. The resulting formulation broadens earlier findings for the complexity-volume proposal to encompass arbitrary geometric complexity measures. Furthermore, the structure of the correction allows a natural interpretation as multiple-flavor Lorentzian threads, where distinct thread sectors correspond to different curvature invariants in the complexity functional. These results show a geometric connection among finite cut-off holography, generalized complexity, and the emergence of non-local computational structures in holographic quantum field theories.

### [118] [Scalar fields, impurities and supersymmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09406)
*D. Bazeia,A. C. Lehum,G. S. Santiago*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 论文在二维时空（two-dimensional spacetime）中，利用spurion超场（spurion superfield）发展了刚性$\mathcal{N}=(1,1)$超空间（superspace）形式，将多标量场模型与局域杂质耦合，建立了描述杂质背景下相互作用标量场的系统框架，并推导了相应的BPS方程、能量密度、边界条件及Bogomol'nyi界（Bogomol'nyi bound），展示了杂质对BPS构型与局域能量密度的影响。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用刚性$\mathcal{N}=(1,1)$超空间形式，通过引入spurion超场以显式超对称的方式将多标量场模型与局域杂质耦合；利用超对称作为组织原理，通过保留投影算符（preserved projector）选择与杂质兼容的一阶方程，进而推导耦合BPS方程、能量密度、边界条件及Bogomol'nyi界。

Result: 局域杂质会改变BPS构型（BPS profiles）并重新分布局域能量密度，但总BPS能量由拓扑边界项（topological boundary term）固定，保持不变。通过一个、两个和三个标量场的代表性模型，分析了相应的BPS构型及其局域能量密度分布。

Conclusion: 所提出的spurion超场方法为处理杂质背景下的多标量场BPS系统提供了一个系统且超对称协变的框架，揭示了杂质仅重新分布而非改变总BPS能量的物理性质。

Abstract: We develop a rigid $\mathcal{N}=(1,1)$ superspace formulation for multifield scalar models coupled to localized impurities through spurion superfields in two-dimensional spacetime. The spurionic completion gives a manifestly supersymmetric action and provides a systematic framework for describing interacting scalar fields in the presence of impurity backgrounds. In this setting, supersymmetry acts as an organizing principle for a controlled bosonic half-BPS sector, with the preserved projector selecting the impurity-compatible first-order equations. We derive the corresponding coupled BPS equations, energy density, boundary conditions, and Bogomol'nyi bound, showing that localized impurities deform the BPS profiles and redistribute the local energy density while leaving the total BPS energy fixed by the topological boundary term. We illustrate the formalism through representative one-, two-, and three-field models, analyzing the resulting BPS configurations and their local energy density profiles.

### [119] [Circuit and Krylov complexity of primordial perturbations of modified gravity in inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09408)

Motivation: 旨在探究暴胀宇宙学中原始曲率扰动的量子复杂性（quantum complexity）诊断，通过对比规范标量场暴胀与修正引力模型 f(φ,R) 的差异，揭示修正引力对量子复杂度演化的影响。

Method: 从曲率扰动的二次作用量出发，推导了压缩强度 r_k 和压缩角 φ_k 的演化方程；利用这些量计算了电路复杂度（circuit complexity）与 Krylov 空间诊断（Krylov-space diagnostics），包括 Krylov 复杂度、Krylov 熵、Lanczos 系数 b_n，以及在开放系统扩展中包含的有效耗散贡献 c_n。

Result: 数值结果表明，f(φ,R) 耦合增强了压缩强度；由于双模压缩态的 Krylov 复杂度由平均对数量 K = sinh² r_k 直接控制，压缩强度的增强反而导致 Krylov 复杂度及相关 Krylov 空间量的增长变小；此外，电路复杂度在 f(φ,R) 框架下展现出更显著的演化，尤其是在视界外出（horizon exit）之后。

Conclusion: 该工作为修正引力 f(φ,R) 的量子复杂性提供了新的见解。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate quantum complexity diagnostics of primordial curvature perturbations within the inflationary paradigm. We compare canonical scalar-field inflation with the modified gravity model $f(φ,R)$, focusing on the evolution of the two-mode squeezed state generated by the coupling between the $\vec{k}$ and $-\vec{k}$ momentum sectors. Starting from the quadratic action for curvature perturbations, we derive the evolution equations for the squeezed strength $r_k$ and squeezed angle $φ_k$, utilizing them to evaluate both circuit complexity and Krylov-space diagnostics. Specifically, we compute the Krylov complexity, Krylov entropy, Lanczos coefficients $b_n$, and an effective dissipative contribution $c_n$ within an open-system extension. Our numerical results demonstrate that the $f(φ,R)$ coupling enhances the squeezed strength relative to the canonical scalar field inflation. Since the Krylov complexity of the two-mode squeezed state is directly controlled by the mean pair number ($K=\sinh^2 r_k$), this enhancement leads to a smaller growth in Krylov complexity and related Krylov-space quantities. Furthermore, circuit complexity displays a more pronounced evolution in the $f(φ,R)$ framework, particularly after the horizon exit regime. Ultimately, our work sheds new light on the quantum complexity of modified gravity $f(φ,R)$.

</details>


### [120] [Unified description of color-electric and color-magnetic strings in hybrid vacua of $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09485)
*E. Ievlev,D. Vasilev,A. Yung*

TL;DR: 本文研究4D 𝒩=2超对称QCD中r-真空（r-vacua）支持的非阿贝尔弦（non-Abelian strings），推导了世界面理论的精确扭曲超势（twisted superpotential），并建立了2D-4D BPS谱对应关系，精确匹配了二维kink与四维受限单极子/夸克的质量，从而为混合真空（hybrid vacua）中的夸克/单极子禁闭提供了统一的物理图像。

Result: 关键结果为：二维kink（two-dimensional kinks）的质量与四维受限单极子（confined monopoles）或夸克（confined quarks）的质量之间实现了精确匹配。此外，提供了混合真空中夸克/单极子禁闭的物理图像。

Conclusion: 本文为非阿贝尔弦上的二维有效理论建立了统一框架，并通过2D-4D BPS谱对应揭示了混合真空中夸克和单极子的禁闭机制，深化了对超对称QCD非微扰动力学的理解。

Abstract: We study non-Abelian strings supported in $r$-vacua of 4D $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric QCD (SQCD) with gauge group $U(N)$ and $N_f$ quark hypermultiplets ($N_f\ge N$), where $r<N$ (scalar) quarks develop vacuum expectation values. At the quantum level, $N-r-1$ monopoles in the orthogonal sector of the gauge group also form a condensate. This leads to the formation of flux tubes (strings) that carry both color-electric and color-magnetic fluxes and confine quarks and monopoles, respectively. We present a unified description of the 2D effective theory living on the world sheet of this non-Abelian string. In particular, we derive the exact twisted superpotential of the world sheet theory, which is deformed by the presence of non-perturbative gaugino condensate in 4D hybrid vacua, using the Gaiotto-Gukov-Seiberg method of resolvents. Next, we extrapolate the 2D-4D correspondence of BPS spectra of the world sheet theory and 4D SQCD (known for quark vacua) to hybrid vacua. Namely, our key result is the precise matching between the masses of the two-dimensional kinks and the four-dimensional confined monopoles or quarks. In addition, we provide a physical picture of the quark/monopole confinement in hybrid vacua.

### [121] [Factorization Algebras and Quantum Groups from Generalized Poisson Sigma Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09486)

Method: 利用位移手征泊松结构（shifted chiral Poisson structures）作为靶空间数据定义广义泊松西格玛模型；运用导出代数几何中的相关概念系统构造界面、富化边界和缺陷；采用Koszul对偶性方法分析边界代数。

Conclusion: 广义泊松西格玛模型为高维全纯-拓扑场论提供了统一的框架，并与形变量子化、导出代数几何以及量子群结构建立了深层联系。该框架的普适性通过不同领域的例子得到了验证。

Abstract: In this work we introduce and study a family of holomorphic--topological field theories, which we call generalized Poisson sigma models. These theories are higher-dimensional analogues of the two-dimensional Poisson sigma model, with target data encoded by shifted chiral Poisson structures. We investigate their relationship with deformation quantizations of holomorphic--topological factorization algebras. Along the way, we give a systematic construction of extended objects, including interfaces, enriched boundaries and defects based on relevant notions in derived algebraic geometry. We employ Koszul-duality methods to study boundary algebras, yielding various versions of quantum groups. ### [122] [Monodromy and geometry of heavy-light Virasoro blocks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09500)
*Mikhail Belakovskiy,Vladimir Belavin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过经典单值性方法（classical monodromy method）与全息坐标下体几何之间的关系，建立了从AdS体时空（bulk）计算重-轻共形块（heavy-light conformal blocks）的一般框架，推导出内部测地线网络的方程独立于重背景，并首次计算出完整的非真空5点HHLLL块。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在半经典极限下，共形块由体时空中的测地线网络（geodesic network）长度计算，但目前对重-轻块的计算方法尚不完善，尤其是在多算子和非真空情况下缺乏统一框架。

Method: 将经典单值性方法与全息坐标下的体几何联系起来，证明单值性矩阵（monodromy matrix）的本征向量编码了体测地线的端点；由此导出轻作用量（light action）和内部测地线网络的方程，并证明内部网络方程独立于重背景。对两个重算子的情形，从初等欧几里得几何重新推导出相同方程作为独立几何验证。

Result: 首次计算出完整的非真空5点HHLLL共形块（此前仅在超轻近似下已知）；建立了从体时空计算重-轻块的一般框架，并明确了其可计算性的阈值。

Conclusion: 所提出的构造为从AdS体时空计算重-轻共形块提供了统一方法，同时限定了该方法的可计算范围，对未来更高点重-轻块的计算具有指导意义。

Abstract: The AdS/CFT correspondence relates gravity in anti-de Sitter space to a boundary conformal field theory, and in its AdS$_3$/CFT$_2$ instance the Virasoro symmetry of the boundary theory organizes correlation functions into conformal blocks. In the semiclassical limit these blocks are computed by lengths of geodesic networks in the bulk, most sharply in the heavy-light regime, where heavy operators source a background probed by light ones. We relate the classical monodromy method to this bulk geometry in holographic coordinates, showing that the eigenvectors of the monodromy matrix encode the endpoints of bulk geodesics. This yields the light action and the equations determining the internal geodesic network; crucially, the internal network equations are independent of the heavy background. For two heavy operators we rederive the same equations from elementary Euclidean geometry, which provides an independent geometric check. As an application we compute the full non-vacuum 5-point HHLLL block, so far known only in the superlight approximation. More broadly, our construction gives a general framework for computing heavy-light blocks from the bulk, while at the same time fixing its threshold of computability.

### [123] [Perusing confining pseudoreal theories: a story of emerging massless spin-1 bosons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09531)
*Giacomo Cacciapaglia,Konstantinos Kollias*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文对极小渐近自由赝实理论（minimal asymptotically free pseudoreal theories）进行了系统研究，识别出哪些理论流向共形动力学（conformal dynamics），哪些理论因非平凡凝聚动力学（condensate dynamics）而发生禁闭（confinement），并预测了禁闭相中无质量自旋-1态和Nambu-Goldstone玻色子的存在数量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子场论（quantum field theory）是粒子相互作用标准模型的基础，求解它是当代理论物理学的主要任务之一。包含一种或两种无质量Weyl费米子（massless Weyl fermions）的极小渐近自由赝实理论流向尚未被充分理解的红外动力学（infrared dynamics），亟需系统分析。

Method: 对所有赝实理论（pseudoreal theories）进行全面研究，通过分析其红外行为，区分流向共形动力学的理论与发生禁闭且伴随非平凡凝聚动力学的理论。

Result: 识别出部分理论流向共形动力学；其余理论发生禁闭。在禁闭理论中，除一种单物种理论外，其余均存在一个无质量自旋-1态（massless spin-1 state）；唯一禁闭的双物种理论则可能包含两个无质量自旋-1态和一个Nambu-Goldstone玻色子（Nambu-Goldstone boson）。

Conclusion: 这些预测可通过格点模拟（Lattice simulations）、泛函重整化群（functional renormalization group）以及超对称类比（supersymmetric analogs）等方法进一步检验。

Abstract: Solving quantum field theory, which is at the basis of the standard model of particle interactions, is one of the main tasks of contemporary theoretical physics. Minimal asymptotically free pseudoreal theories, containing one or two species of massless Weyl fermions in pseudoreal representations of the gauge group, flow towards a poorly understood infrared dynamics. We provide a comprehensive study of all pseudoreal theories, identifying the ones that likely flow towards a conformal dynamics, while we show that the remaining ones confine with a non-trivial condensate dynamics. Among the latter, all but one one-species theories feature a massless spin-1 state. Instead, the only confining two-species theory likely features two massless spin-1 states and one Nambu-Goldstone boson. These predictions could be further tested, for instance by use of Lattice simulations, the functional renormalization group, and supersymmetric analogs.

Method: 采用大电荷自举方法，结合标量、流和应力张量作为探针，仅考虑宇称偶交换算符，基于最小假设分析Regge轨迹的色散关系。

Result: 在最小假设下，自举要求至少存在一条满足共形超流体标准戈德斯通模态色散关系的Regge轨迹；在额外假设下，该轨迹唯一，且所有非戈德斯通轨迹只在标量-标量道中产生贡献。

Conclusion: 大电荷自举方法有效约束了三维U(1)对称CFT中算符谱的结构，揭示了戈德斯通模Regge轨迹的必要性与潜在唯一性。

Abstract: We study the large-charge bootstrap in three-dimensional CFTs with a global U(1) symmetry using scalar, current, and stress-tensor probes, restricting to parity-even exchanged operators. Under minimal assumptions, the bootstrap requires at least one Regge trajectory with the dispersion relation of the standard Goldstone mode of the conformal superfluid. With additional assumptions, this trajectory is unique, while all non-Goldstone trajectories contribute only to the scalar-scalar channel at this order.

### [125] [Massless fermionic current of Schwinger pairs in 3D de Sitter spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09594)
*Manizheh Botshekananfarda,Clément Stahl*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在(1+2)维德西特时空中，研究了由恒定电场产生的无质量费米子对及其诱导电流，首次导出了有限表达式，并分析了强场与弱场下的不同行为，揭示了维度和自旋对红外物理的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在德西特（de Sitter，dS）时空背景下研究U(1)规范场引发的真空中粒子对产生，是探索弯曲时空量子场论（quantum field theory in curved backgrounds）的重要场景。本文旨在填补(1+2)维dS时空中无质量费米子诱导电流的解析表达空白，并澄清自旋与红外物理之间的相互作用。

Method: 假设Bunch–Davies真空（Bunch-Davies vacuum），采用绝热正规化（adiabatic regularization）方法，推导(1+2)维dS时空中由恒定电场诱导的无质量费米子电流。

Result: 首次得到了dS₃中费米子诱导电流的有限表达式。产生的费米子形成与外加电场方向相反的净电流。强场区呈现半经典标度行为，在平直时空极限下恢复标准施温格行为（Schwinger behavior）；弱场区电流与电场强度呈线性关系，且未出现玻色子情形中的红外超导电性（infrared hyperconductivity）。整个参数空间中电流保持单调，未出现dS₄中的符号反转现象。

Conclusion: 本文结果突出了维度在dS时空量子效应中的关键作用，并阐明了自旋与红外物理的相互影响。该工作为后续研究反冲效应（backreaction effects）、拓扑质量费米子（topologically massive fermions）以及含时电磁背景提供了自洽的基础。

Abstract: Pair creation from the vacuum in the presence of a U(1) gauge field in de Sitter $(\mathrm{dS})$ spacetime provides an important setting for exploring quantum field theory in curved backgrounds. In this work, we investigate massless fermion production and the associated induced current generated by a constant electric field in (1+2)-dimensional $\mathrm{dS}$ spacetime. Assuming the Bunch--Davies vacuum and employing adiabatic regularization, we derive, for the first time, a finite expression for the induced current of massless fermions in $\mathrm{dS}_{3}$. The produced fermions generate a net current opposite to the external electric field. In the strong-field regime, the induced current exhibits the expected semiclassical scaling and reproduces the standard Schwinger behavior in the flat-spacetime limit. In the weak-field regime, the current is linear in the electric-field strength. This behavior is characteristic of the fermionic nature of the particles, since the corresponding bosonic case exhibits infrared hyperconductivity, which is absent in our study. We further show that the induced current remains monotonic throughout the parameter space and, unlike in $\mathrm{dS}_4$, does not exhibit any sign change. Our results thus highlight the role of dimensionality and clarify the interplay between spin and infrared physics in $\mathrm{dS}$. This work provides a consistent basis for future investigations including backreaction effects, topologically massive fermions, and time-dependent electromagnetic backgrounds.

### [127] [Neutrino-induced hyperon final-state interactions as constraints on the in-medium hyperon potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09273)
*Jaroslaw Nowak*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文提出利用加速器中微子（neutrino）与40Ar靶核的带电流（charged-current）相互作用产生的超子（hyperon）信号，来约束超子单粒子势（hyperon single-particle potentials）U_Λ和U_Σ，进而缓解中子星物质中的“超子疑难（hyperon puzzle）”。研究展示了中微子实验对超子势的测量精度、系统误差来源，以及将低密度约束推广到中子星状态方程（EOS）后得到的最大质量M_max=2.21 M⊙。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超子单粒子势U_Y(ρ)决定了超子在原子核中的传播以及在高密物质中出现的密度门槛，直接影响中子星状态方程的软化程度和最大质量，导致“超子疑难”。目前缺乏独立的低密度约束手段来区分不同潜在的U_Y形式，因此需要新的实验途径来检验这些势能参数。

Method: 利用SBND和DUNE能区的带电流中微子/反中微子与40Ar的相互作用，在核内产生Λ和Σ超子。通过分析俘获Λ的分支比和逃逸超子的动量谱随U_Λ和U_Σ的变化关系，结合卡介子（kaon）标记的末态相互作用（FSI）Σ+标记技术，提取约束信息。将这些势能参数嵌入GM1相对论平均场（relativistic mean-field）状态方程中，并在已建立的超核和Σ原子深度处评估中子星性质。采用Fisher矩阵（Fisher forecast）进行探测器级精度估计。

Result: 固定低密度指数γ时，Fisher分析给出δU_Λ≈0.3 MeV、δU_Σ≈3–4 MeV；但U_Λ(ρ_0)与γ存在99.8%的反关联，边缘化γ后δU_Λ退化为约5.6 MeV（施加±0.2先验时降至1.3 MeV），而δU_Σ不受影响。超子-核子末态相互作用截面（YN截面）对U_Λ引入-5/+2 MeV的系统偏差，对U_Σ引入约150 MeV的大偏差；输运模型中的出射位移/梯度处方（exit-shift/gradient transport prescription）对U_Λ产生-6 MeV偏移。结合地面与重离子先验的联合拟合给出M_max=2.21^{+0.04}_{-0.15} M⊙，主要由外部c_Λ先验决定。

Conclusion: 中微子-氩反应能够作为超子单粒子势的低密度探针，提供几MeV而非亚MeV精度的U_Λ约束。U_Σ的测量受YN末态相互作用不确定性的严重影响，即使去除Σ+标签也无法消除偏差。低密度U_Λ锚定是一个稳健的约束手段，但精度受γ关联和系统误差的限制。

Abstract: Hyperon single-particle potentials $U_Y(ρ)$ control propagation in nuclei and hyperon onset in dense matter, where they soften the neutron-star equation of state and reduce the maximum mass -- the ``hyperon puzzle''. We show that charged-current accelerator (anti)neutrino interactions on $^{40}$Ar, producing $Λ$ and $Σ$ inside the nucleus, can constrain these potentials. At SBND and DUNE energies, the trapped-$Λ$ fraction and escaping-hyperon momenta vary monotonically with $U_Λ$ and $U_Σ$, with a kaon-vetoed FSI-$Σ^+$ tag adding sensitivity. Inserted in a GM1 relativistic mean-field equation of state at established hypernuclear/$Σ$-atom depths, the same potentials give $M_{\rm max} = 1.94\,M_\odot$ and $Λ_{1.4}=1034$, below the heaviest pulsars and above the GW170817 bound typical of GM1-class mean fields. A detector-level Fisher forecast yields $δU_Λ\simeq 0.3\,$MeV and $δU_Σ\simeq 3$-$4\,$MeV for fixed low-density exponent $γ$. Since hyperons are produced below saturation, $U_Λ(ρ_0)$ and $γ$ are 99.8\% anti-correlated; marginalising over $γ$ degrades the anchor to $δU_Λ\simeq 5.6\,$MeV ($1.3\,$MeV with a $\pm 0.2$ prior), while $δU_Σ$ is unchanged. For $U_Λ$, comparable systematics arise from hyperon-nucleon final-state cross sections ($-5/{+}2\,$MeV) and the exit-shift/gradient transport prescription ($-6\,$MeV). For $U_Σ$, the same $YN$ uncertainty biases the fit by $\mathcal{O}(150)\,$MeV; removing the $Σ^+$ tag does not cure this, because the $Λ$ momentum spectrum carries most $U_Σ$ information and is itself $YN$-sensitive. The low-density $U_Λ$ anchor is a robust handle, at several-MeV rather than sub-MeV precision. A joint fit with terrestrial and heavy-ion priors gives $M_{\rm max} = 2.21^{+0.04}_{-0.15}\,\,$Msun, set mainly by the external $c_Λ$ prior.

</details>


### [128] [In-medium hyperon potentials and the quarkyonic hyperon onset: charged $Σ$'s in $β$-equilibrium and the neutrino connection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09280)
*Jaroslaw Nowak*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 该论文通过夸克物质（quarkyonic matter）机制统计性地解决了中子星超子谜题（hyperon puzzle），在Fujimoto–Kojo–McLerran (FKM) 框架中引入介质势（in-medium potentials）并受超核数据和中微子诱导超子末态相互作用（FSI）约束。研究发现：超子阈值被动力学上移且对超子势（U_Y）敏感度加倍；Σ⁻超子在2 M☉核心中被禁止；TOV软化效应显著小于传统强子模型；最大质量星中核心奇异度（core strangeness）由超子势和YNN三体力交叉项控制；中微子数据对c_Λ不敏感导致后验分布先验主导（prior-dominated）；Mmax对U_Y的微分敏感度比平均场模型低一个数量级，可区分两种理论方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子星超子谜题是致密星物态方程（equation of state, EoS）研究中的核心难题：若引入超子自由度，理论预言的星体最大质量（Mmax）会显著低于约2 M☉的观测值。已有解决方案包括强超子势或引入夸克物质相变，但统计力学解释尚不明确。本文旨在用夸克物质（quarkyonic matter）框架，在FKM机制中系统引入介质势修正，以从统计力学角度量化超子阈值的移位及其对中子星可观测量的影响。

Method: 采用FKM的IdylliQ模型并加入介质势（in-medium potentials），利用超核实验数据和由中微子诱导超子末态相互作用（FSI）进行约束。理论计算包括：对S=-1超子的阈值条件μB^onset进行势修正（含中子势的自洽处理）；结合β平衡（beta equilibrium）下轻子化学势μe的条件，分析Σ⁻的涌现（onset）；通过在FKM ansatz族和现实相互作用星中延续kᵧ ≥ k_bu方案（即超子与夸克态动量一致）计算TOV软化（TOV softening）；利用SBND和DUNE的FSI精度预估对超子势参数（U_Λ(n₀)和c_Λ）进行后验约束。

Result: (i) 修正后的超子阈值中U_Y（超子势）权重为2，且dn_onset/dU_Y ≈ 0.3 n₀每10 MeV，杠杆效应加倍。(ii) 中子势U_N在自洽条件下要求U_N(n_onset) ≲ +96 MeV才能维持保护。(iii) β平衡下Σ⁻涌现条件为μe ≥ 258 MeV + U_Σ⁻ − U_N，在2 M☉核心中永远无法达到，Σ⁻从首个涌现超子变为被禁止，Σ序反转（ordering inversion）。(iv) TOV软化在FKM族中小于0.05 M☉，在现实相互作用星中小于0.025 M☉，比强子模型小4–8倍。(v) 当U_Λ(n₀) = −28 MeV且YNN三体力交叉项c_Λ超过阈值c_Λ^*时，最大质量星无超子；中微子数据可约束U_Λ(n₀)但对c_Λ不敏感，后验概率P(超子自由核心) = 0.90，几乎等同先验的0.89。

Conclusion: 夸克物质机制为超子谜题提供了一种统计力学上自洽的解决方案，其核心在于超子动量空间被d夸克填充所阻塞，而非依赖强排斥势。FKM修正后的阈值敏感度特征——U_Y权重加倍以及Mmax对U_Y的微分敏感度比平均场模型低一个数量级——可作为区分两类理论方案的诊断工具。SBND和DUNE的联合测量有望约束U_Λ(n₀)，但对YNN三体力c_Λ的敏感度不足，导致后验分布先验主导；未来的重离子碰撞数据可能打破这一僵局。

Abstract: Quarkyonic matter resolves the neutron-star hyperon puzzle statistically: neutrons fill low-momentum $d$-quark phase space, shifting the $S=-1$ threshold from $\muB=M_Y$ to $2M_Y-M_N$ and suppressing residual softening by $1/\Nc^3$ in the Fujimoto--Kojo--McLerran (FKM) mechanism. We dress FKM's IdylliQ model with in-medium potentials, constrained by hypernuclear data and neutrino-induced hyperon FSI, and find: (i) the dressed onset, $\muB^{\rm onset}=(2M_Y{-}M_N)+2U_Y-\UN$, carries $U_Y$ at weight 2, with $dn_{\rm onset}/dU_Y\simeq0.3\,\nz$ per $10\MeV$, twice the leverage. (ii) A self-consistent neutron potential enters at weight $-2$, so protection needs $\UN(n_{\rm onset})\lesssim+96\MeV$. (iii) With leptons in $β$ equilibrium, the $Σ^-$ ($dds$) onset becomes $\mue\ge258\MeV+\US-\UN$, never reached inside a $2\,\Msun$ core: $Σ^-$ switches from first hyperon to forbidden and the $Σ$ ordering inverts. (iv) The $\kY\ge\kbu$ continuation gives TOV softening below $0.05\,\Msun$ in the FKM ansatz family and below $0.025\,\Msun$ for the realistic interacting star, $4$--$8$ below hadronic models. In the family this is a ceiling; generally it is a floor, since hyperons above $\kbu$ are omitted. (v) In an interacting low-density sector calibrated to $\Mmax=2.12\,\Msun$, core strangeness is controlled by $(\UL(\nz),c_Λ)$: at $\UL(\nz)=-28\MeV$, the maximum-mass star is hyperon-free once the supra-saturation $YNN$ turn-over exceeds a few-MeV threshold $c^*_Λ$. Projected SBND+DUNE FSI precision pins $\UL(\nz)$ but leaves $c_Λ$ -- to which neutrino data are blind -- decisive: with the heavy-ion prior, $P({\rm hyperon\mbox{-}free\ core})=0.90$, versus $0.89$ from priors alone, prior-dominated rather than measured. The sharpest observable is differential: $d\Mmax/dU_Y$ is an order of magnitude smaller than in mean-field models, discriminating the two resolutions.

</details>


### [129] [Stochastic Similarity Renormalization Group](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08830)
*Rongzhe Hu,Xin Zhen,Furong Xu,Junchen Pei*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文将量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）技术融入相似性重整化群（SRG），提出了一种随机SRG框架（SRGQMC），能够执行自由空间两体与介质中多体演化。通过将连续幺正变换映射到有符号随机游走者系综，该框架避免了多体流方程的组合张量空间爆炸。以现实核子-核子（NN）相互作用和Richardson配对模型为基准测试，该方法在四体层次[IMSRG(4)]上首次实现了计算突破，为高阶介质内SRG（IMSRG）计算提供了可行途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 确定性多体流方程面临组合张量空间爆炸（combinatorial tensor-space explosion）问题，尤其在高阶相关体层次（如IMSRG(4)）计算代价过高，亟需一种可扩展的新方法以突破这一计算瓶颈。

Method: 将量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）技术整合到相似性重整化群（SRG）中，构建随机SRG框架（SRGQMC）；通过将连续幺正变换（continuous unitary transformation）映射为有符号随机游走者（signed random walkers）的系综演化，避免了多体流方程的直接张量积分。

Result: 在自由空间两体层面，SRGQMC与确定性SRG结果一致；在介质中多体层面，与IMSRG(2)/(3)结果吻合。确定性方法无法实现的IMSRG(4)计算，借助随机技术首次成功完成，显著逼近全组态相互作用（full configuration-interaction）极限。

Conclusion: 该随机SRG框架为高阶IMSRG计算提供了一条实用进路，有望将介质内重整化群处理的精度扩展至四体及以上相关层次。

Abstract: By integrating the quantum Monte Carlo technique into the similarity renormalization group (SRG), we have developed a stochastic SRG framework (SRGQMC) capable of both free-space two-body and in-medium many-body evolutions. This approach circumvents the combinatorial tensor-space explosion of many-body flow equations by mapping continuous unitary transformations onto an ensemble of signed random walkers. We benchmark the SRGQMC against deterministic free-space SRG evolutions of realistic nucleon-nucleon (NN) interactions, as well as against in-medium SRG (IMSRG) many-body calculations with the Richardson pairing model at two- and three-body levels [IMSRG(2)/(3)]. While a deterministic extension to the four-body level [IMSRG(4)] remains unfeasible due to prohibitive computational costs, we have achieved the first IMSRG(4) calculation by using the stochastic technique, demonstrating a substantial improvement toward the full configuration-interaction limit. This stochastic framework provides a practical pathway to higher-order IMSRG calculations.

</details>


### [130] [Ab initio calculations of $^{229}$Th band-to-band internal conversion rate in $^{229}$ThO$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08941)
*Udeshika C. Perera,H. B. Tran Tan,H. W. T. Morgan,Eric Hudson,Daniel A. Rehn,Andrei Derevianko*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文通过从头计算（ab initio）方法，计算了 $^{229}$ThO$_2$ 中能量约为 8.35 eV 的同质异能跃迁（isomeric transition）的带间内转换（band-to-band internal-conversion）速率。研究发现，当核跃迁能量超过 ThO$_2$ 的电子带隙时，同质异能核可通过共振激发价带电子至导带而发生非辐射衰变。计算得到的内转换寿命在 1–16 μs 范围内，且随带隙接近核跃迁能量而显著增加。文章指出，选择带隙略低于核跃迁能量的固态宿主材料，可优化基于内转换电子读出的固态核钟性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: $^{229}$Th 核同质异能态（isomer）的能量约为 8.35 eV，恰好落在真空紫外（VUV）波段，是唯一已知可通过激光直接操控的原子核激发态，因此被视为构建固态核钟（solid-state nuclear clock）的理想候选体系。理解该同质异能态在固态宿主（如 ThO$_2$）中的非辐射衰变机制（即内转换过程）对于评估核钟性能及设计读出方案至关重要。

Method: 该方法将内转换过程表示为布里渊区求和（Brillouin-zone sum），对垂直带间跃迁（vertical interband transitions）进行加权，权重为局域在 Th 原子近核区（Th-centered）的超精细矩阵元（hyperfine matrix elements），这些矩阵元直接由全电子全势线性化增广平面波布洛赫旋量（all-electron full-potential linearized augmented-plane-wave Bloch spinors）计算得到。引入有限核磁化模型（finite nuclear magnetization model）以正则化短程超精细相互作用并计及玻尔-魏斯科普夫效应（Bohr-Weisskopf effect）。还使用剪刀修正（scissor shifts）以匹配实验报道的 ThO$_2$ 带隙值。

Result: 应用剪刀修正后，计算得到的内转换寿命在 1–16 μs 范围内。寿命随带隙接近核跃迁能量 $\omega_{\rm nuc}$ 而显著增加，因为共振带间相空间（resonant interband phase space）随之减小。对于实验报道的较大 ThO$_2$ 带隙值，计算寿命与测量得到的转换电子穆斯堡尔寿命（conversion-electron Mössbauer lifetime）[Nature 648, 300 (2025)] 相当。

Conclusion: 分析表明，选择带隙略低于 $\omega_{\rm nuc}$ 的固态宿主材料，可以优化基于内转换电子读出的固态核钟性能。

Abstract: We present an ab initio calculation of the band-to-band internal-conversion rate of the $\hbarω_{\rm nuc} \approx 8.35$ eV isomeric transition in $^{229}$ThO$_2$. Because the nuclear transition energy exceeds the electronic band gap of ThO$_2$, the isomer can decay nonradiatively by resonantly promoting a valence electron into the conduction band. We formulate this process as a Brillouin-zone sum over vertical interband transitions weighted by local Th-centered hyperfine matrix elements, which are evaluated directly from all-electron full-potential linearized augmented-plane-wave Bloch spinors. A finite nuclear magnetization model is included to regularize the short-range hyperfine interaction and to account for the Bohr-Weisskopf effect. After applying scissor shifts to span the experimentally reported ThO$_2$ band gaps, we find calculated internal-conversion lifetimes in the range of $1-16~μ{\rm s}$. The lifetime increases strongly as the band gap approaches $ω_{\rm nuc}$ because the resonant interband phase space at the nuclear transition energy is reduced. For the larger reported ThO$_2$ gaps, the calculated lifetime is comparable to the measured conversion-electron Mössbauer lifetime [Nature 648, 300 (2025)]. Our analysis implies that choosing solid-state hosts with band-gap values slightly lower than $ω_{\rm nuc}$ can optimize solid-state nuclear clock performance with internal-conversion electron readout.

</details>

### [131] [A diagrammatic field theory of quantum error correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08911)
*Steven Rayan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个基于融合空间码（fusion-space codes）的场论框架用于量子纠错，在幺正融合范畴（unitary fusion categories）中阐述了可诊断足迹代数与综合征可容许交换代数的核心区别，建立了精确可纠正性的纤维化Knill-Laflamme条件，并在Ising理论中通过显式构造展示了足迹互补逻辑诊断和译码模糊性，最后证明了条件性的Peierls型阈值定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子纠错（quantum error correction）需要统一的场论框架来理解由拓扑序（topological order）和融合范畴（fusion categories）所描述的量子系统中的错误检测与纠正机制，特别是如何区分可安全测量的可观测量与可能泄露逻辑信息的可观测量。

Method: 采用场论方法，以融合空间码为核心，引入足迹投影算符（footprint projector）记录错误的局域可见信息；定义诊断足迹代数（diagnostic footprint algebra）与综合征可容许交换代数（syndrome-admissible commuting algebra）并建立其区分准则；证明精确可纠正性等价于纤维化Knill-Laflamme条件（fibrewise Knill-Laflamme conditions），从而得到先测量后恢复的因子化结构；在可收缩真空局域性假设下，给出标量作用在码空间上的范畴充分判据。

Result: 在Ising理论中，四个σ穿刺点（punctures）的构造表明对电荷足迹可作为互补逻辑诊断，实现精确的单比特Clifford阴影（shadow）；六σ码允许综合征可容许的对电荷测量和针对显式马约拉纳双线性错误（Majorana bilinear error）的精确恢复；第二个双线性错误具有相同测量足迹但相差一个逻辑比特翻转，产生了非平凡的足迹纤维和真实的译码歧义；证明了条件性Peierls型阈值定理（Peierls-type threshold theorem）：在有限连通区域增长、局域随机噪声、小残余分量的局域可中和性以及分量级译码器平衡条件下，错误率低于非零常数时失败概率满足指数衰减界。

Conclusion: 该工作连通了量子纠错与表示论（representation theory）和代数几何（algebraic geometry）中的深层次结构，包括管代数（tube algebras）、Hopf代数、Yangian型结构、Higgs丛（Higgs bundles）、谱曲线（spectral curves）、Jacobian簇和abelian簇等，为未来将量子纠错与高阶代数结构相结合的研究方向奠定了基础。

Abstract: We develop a field-theoretic framework for quantum error correction centred on fusion-space codes in unitary fusion categories. Admissible clusters determine total-charge sectors and orthogonal footprint projectors recording locally visible data left by error histories. The central distinction is between diagnostic footprint algebras and syndrome-admissible commuting algebras: the latter can be measured without revealing logical information and resolve chosen error representatives into measured sectors. For such algebras, exact correctability is equivalent to fibrewise Knill--Laflamme conditions, yielding a measure-then-recover factorization. Under a contractible-vacuum locality hypothesis, closed neutral composites give a categorical sufficient criterion for scalar action on the code. In the Ising theory, four $σ$ punctures show that pair-charge footprints can be complementary logical diagnostics and realize an exact one-qubit Clifford shadow. A proper six-$σ$ code instead admits a syndrome-admissible pair-charge measurement and exact recovery from an explicit Majorana bilinear error. A second bilinear has the same measured footprint but differs by a logical bit flip, producing a concrete nontrivial footprint fibre and genuine decoding ambiguity. We also formulate conformal-block likelihood data and compute geometry-dependent Ising four-point weights. For growing code families, we prove a conditional Peierls-type threshold theorem: bounded connected-region growth, local stochastic noise, local neutralizability of small residual components, and componentwise decoder balance imply $\Pr_L(\mathrm{fail})\le C|Ω_L|e^{-cL}$ below a nonzero constant error rate. We conclude with representation-theoretic and algebro-geometric directions involving tube and Hopf algebras, Yangian-type structures, Higgs bundles, spectral curves, Jacobians, and abelian varieties.

</details>


### [132] [A complete ultrametric on von Neumann's incomplete tensor products](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09627)
*Andrew Lesniewski*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在冯·诺依曼无穷张量积（infinite tensor product of Hilbert spaces）理论中引入一种伪超度量（pseudo-ultrametric）$d$，定义在$C_0$-序列的等价类集$\Gamma$上，证明其满足强三角不等式且完备；通过商空间$(\widetilde\Gamma,d)$得到完备超度量空间。作为应用，研究乘积酉算子（product unitary）对等价类的位移，并发展出一种规范不变度量$\tilde d$，将其解释为退相干指数（decoherence exponent），用于刻画Everett分支中两分支随环境监测而变得可区分的多项式速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重新审视并严格化冯·诺依曼的无穷张量积理论，为量子力学中的Everett分支（Everettian branching）或多世界诠释提供一个数学上精确的度量框架，用以刻画不同分支之间的“距离”及其在动力学演化下的变化。

Method: 在$C_0$-序列等价类集$\Gamma$上定义伪超度量$d$，其值为任意代表元构成的级数$\sum_j|\langle\varphi_j,\psi_j\rangle-1|$的收敛指数（convergence exponent）；通过商掉$d=0$的关系得到超度量空间$(\widetilde\Gamma,d)$。进一步基于冯·诺依曼弱等价（weak equivalence）构造规范不变度量$\tilde d$，将其与拟局部代数（quasi-local algebra）上的乘积态（product states）的拟等价（quasi-equivalence）相匹配。

Result: 证明了$d$在等价类上良定义，满足强三角不等式且完备。若酉算子$U$满足$\inf_{\|x\|=1}|\langle x,Ux\rangle-1|>0$（如有限维空间中$1\notin\sigma(U)$），则乘积酉$\bigotimes_j U$将每个类位移至最大距离$1$。规范不变度量$\tilde d$下，位移与类相关，可取$[0,1]$中的任意值。

Conclusion: 将$\tilde d$解释为退相干指数，它度量了在环境被监测部分不断扩大时，宇宙态矢量的两个分支在操作上变得可区分的多项式速率，为Everett分支的退相干机制提供了一种数学描述。

Abstract: We revisit von Neumann's theory of infinite tensor products of Hilbert spaces. On the set $Γ$ of equivalence classes of $C_0$-sequences, which labels the incomplete tensor products inside the complete tensor product, we introduce a natural pseudo-ultrametric $d$: the distance between two classes is the convergence exponent of the series $\sum_j|\langle\varphi_j,ψ_j\rangle-1|$ formed from any pair of representatives. We show that $d$ is well defined on equivalence classes, satisfies the strong triangle inequality, and is complete. Distinct classes may lie at distance zero, so $d$ separates points only after passing to the quotient $\widetildeΓ$ of $Γ$ by the relation $d=0$; the pair $(\widetildeΓ,d)$ is then a complete ultrametric space. As an application, we show that a product unitary $\bigotimes_j U$ whose factor $U$ satisfies $\inf_{\|x\|=1}|\langle x,Ux\rangle-1|>0$ (in particular, a unitary on a finite dimensional space with $1\notinσ(U)$) displaces every class to the maximal distance $1$. Guided by the intended application -- a caricature of Everettian branching, in which the sectors of the infinite tensor product play the role of worlds -- we also develop a gauge-invariant variant $\tilde d$ of the metric, based on von Neumann's weak equivalence and matched to the quasi-equivalence of product states on the quasi-local algebra. The displacement of a class under a product unitary, measured by $\tilde d$, is class dependent and realizes every value in $[0,1]$. We interpret $\tilde d$ as a decoherence exponent: it measures the polynomial rate at which two branches of the universal state vector become operationally distinct as ever larger portions of the environment are monitored.

</details>


### [133] [The Apparatus Strikes Back: Momentum Conservation and the Cost of Spatial Superpositions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08819)
*Lucas C. Céleri,Diogo O. Soares-Pinto,Daniel A. Turolla Vanzella*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文从动量守恒和制备装置的量子本质出发，识别出一个普适约束：任何在空间上制备质点相干叠加的协议，必然使质点与装置质心自由度纠缠，导致反冲位移，从而限制叠加态的相干性。该约束可表达为对装置温度和刚性锚定的定量界，并对当前物质波干涉、引力介导纠缠及普朗克尺度量子力学测试有重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 制备大质量粒子在空间上的相干叠加是现代量子科学的核心目标，但其实验难度通常归因于环境退相干机制。本文旨在识别一个不依赖实验细节的普适约束，该约束源于动量守恒和制备装置的量子本性。

Method: 通过考虑动量守恒与质量偶极矩（mass dipole moment）的守恒，推导出粒子与装置质心自由度之间的必然纠缠；利用反冲位移必须小于装置质心态的相干长度这一条件，导出对装置温度和刚性锚定的定量约束。

Result: 得到普适定量界：即使质量为宏观的装置，其反冲也可能对远低于普朗克质量（Planck mass）的粒子空间叠加相干性施加出人意料的强约束；该界适用于现有物质波干涉实验、引力介导纠缠（gravitationally mediated entanglement）提案及普朗克尺度附近量子力学测试。

Conclusion: 所识别的反冲约束应被视为保守估计（conservative estimate），并在特定条件下可解释为虚假退相干（false decoherence）的一个实例。

Abstract: Preparing massive particles in coherent spatial superpositions is a central objective of modern quantum science, motivated by applications ranging from fundamental tests of quantum mechanics and gravity to quantum-enhanced sensing. The experimental difficulty of realizing such superpositions is usually attributed to environmental decoherence mechanisms whose impact depends on the details of the experimental implementation. Here we identify a universal constraint arising from momentum conservation and the quantum nature of the preparation apparatus. Any protocol that places a particle of mass $m$ in a spatial superposition with separation $d$ necessarily entangles the particle with the center-of-mass degree of freedom of the apparatus responsible for the splitting. The resulting recoil displacement, fixed by conservation of the mass dipole moment, reduces the coherence of the particle when the apparatus is not included as part of the quantum system. For an apparatus of mass $M$, preserving coherence requires the recoil displacement to remain smaller than the coherence length of the apparatus center-of-mass state, leading to a quantitative bound expressible as a constraint on its temperature and on how rigidly the apparatus is anchored to the laboratory frame. We analyze the implications of this bound for current matter-wave interferometry experiments, proposals for gravitationally mediated entanglement, and tests of quantum mechanics near the Planck scale. Our main result, which may seem counterintuitive, is that the recoil of even heavy macroscopic apparatuses can pose a surprisingly strong constraint on the coherence of spatial superpositions of particles with masses well below the Planck mass. Finally, we discuss why the resulting limitation should be regarded as a conservative estimate and under which conditions it can be interpreted as an instance of false decoherence.

</details>


### [134] [Nonlinear particle detectors across the Rindler firewall](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09660)
*Matheus H. Zambianco,Eduardo Martín-Martínez*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Unruh-DeWitt探测器与量子标量场的复合可观测量（包括场动量的二次耦合和局域能量密度耦合）耦合时的响应行为，特别是跨越Rindler防火墙时的表现。

Method: 建立了一个分布论（distributional）框架来评估对应的探测器响应函数，并将其应用于穿越Rindler防火墙的探测器。

Result: 导数耦合模型恢复有限响应；二次动量耦合导致分布乘积的病态定义和不可避免的形式发散（$δ(0)$-type divergences）；局域能量密度响应与二次动量响应密切相关。

Conclusion: 标准锐利防火墙模型与非线性探测器耦合到局域可观测量不相容；这些病态源于Rindler视界处关联的不连续切断，而非探测器模型本身。

Abstract: We investigate Unruh-DeWitt detectors coupled to composite observables of a quantum scalar field, including quadratic coupling to the field momentum and coupling to the local energy density. We develop a distributional framework for evaluating the corresponding detector response functions and apply it to detectors crossing the Rindler firewall. While we recover the finite response of the derivative-coupling model, we show that quadratic momentum coupling leads to ill-defined products of distributions and unavoidable formal $δ(0)$-type divergences. Since the local energy-density response is closely tied to the quadratic momentum response, our results provide strong evidence that the standard sharp firewall model is incompatible with nonlinear detector couplings to local observables. Our analysis further suggests that these pathologies originate from the discontinuous severing of correlations across the Rindler horizon, rather than from the detector model itself.

### [135] [Non-Local Magic from the Entanglement Spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07808)
*Gianpaolo Torre,Fabio Franchini,Salvatore Marco Giampaolo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过纠缠谱（entanglement spectrum）的Walsh–Hadamard自关联表示非局域魔力（non-local magic），证明其可被纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）上界约束，并给出了体率态（volume-law states）以及一维有能隙与临界系统基态中非局域魔力的精确标度行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非局域魔力作为表征真正非局域非稳定子关联（non-local non-stabilizer correlations）的基本资源，其直接计算除小系统外是棘手的数值问题，且对其理解仍然有限。

Method: 利用纠缠谱的Walsh–Hadamard自关联（Walsh–Hadamard autocorrelations）推导出非局域魔力的显式表示，揭示其背后的调和结构（harmonic structure），从而实现对不同场景下行为的系统分析。

Result: 证明了非局域魔力可由纠缠熵给出上界；对于体率态以及一维有能隙（gapped）和临界（critical）系统的基态，导出了非局域魔力的精确解析标度结果。

Conclusion: 纠缠谱的谱组织（spectral organization）是控制非局域魔力的关键要素，该工作为进一步的系统性解析研究提供了框架。

Abstract: Non-local magic has recently emerged as a fundamental resource for characterizing genuinely non-local non-stabilizer correlations. However, its direct calculation is an intractable numerical problem, except for small systems, and its understanding remains limited. We derive a representation of non-local magic in terms of the Walsh--Hadamard autocorrelations of the entanglement spectrum. Our representation makes the underlying harmonic structure explicit and enables a systematic analysis of its behaviors for various scenarios. We prove that non-local magic can be upper-bounded by an entanglement entropy and we derive exact analytical results for broad classes of quantum states, characterizing the scaling of non-local magic for volume-law states, as well as ground states of one-dimensional gapped and critical systems. Our results identify the spectral organization of the entanglement spectrum as the key ingredient governing non-local magic and provide a framework for further systematic analytical investigation.

### [136] [Superconducting singlet-triplet qubits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09508)
*Anatoliy Lotkov,Maria Spethmann,Daniel Loss*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出超导单重态-三重态（SST）量子比特，基于约瑟夫森结中的平行排列双量子点，无需自旋-轨道耦合即可实现自旋自由度操控，具有全连接性、低控制线路开销和对电荷/磁通噪声的线性保护，有望用于未来量子处理器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有混合器件中的Andreev自旋量子比特依赖自旋-轨道相互作用（spin-orbit interaction）来释放自旋自由度，限制了材料选择范围；本文旨在提出一种无需自旋-轨道相互作用的替代方案，使混合器件的优势可推广至更广泛的材料体系。

Method: 提出超导单重态-三重态（superconducting singlet-triplet, SST）量子比特结构，采用约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）中平行排列的双量子点（double quantum dots），利用超导相位耦合实现量子比特态的操控和读出。

Result: SST量子比特无需自旋-轨道相互作用即可操控自旋自由度，与Andreev自旋量子比特一样可通过电路量子电动力学（circuit QED）进行控制和读出，并支持全连接（all-to-all connectivity）；仅需N条磁通线即可对N个量子比特执行任意单量子比特和双量子比特门，控制线路开销小；同时具有对电荷噪声和磁通噪声的线性保护。

Conclusion: SST量子比特兼具混合器件的优势和更宽的材料兼容性，结合低控制开销与噪声防护特性，使其成为未来量子处理器的有前景候选方案。

Abstract: Hybrid devices integrating quantum dots with Josephson junctions are gaining interest because they combine spin-based quantum computing with circuit quantum electrodynamics (circuit QED) methods. In particular, Andreev spin qubits have shown significant experimental progress including strong two-qubit coupling, and are predicted to exhibit all-to-all connectivity. Here we propose superconducting singlet-triplet (SST) qubits that rely on parallel-aligned double quantum dots in Josephson junctions. While Andreev spin qubits require spin-orbit interaction to unlock the spin degree-of-freedom, SST qubits do not require spin-orbit interaction, making the advantages of hybrid devices available to a wider range of materials. Similar to Andreev spin qubits, the qubit states couple to the superconducting phase across the junction, which allows for control and readout using circuit QED, and supports all-to-all connectivity. Only $N$ flux lines are required to perform any single- and two-qubit gate among $N$ qubits, and thus the overhead of control lines is small. Finally, linear protection from charge or flux noise makes these qubits interesting candidates for a future quantum processor.

### [137] [Complete measurement of tunnel- and valley-coupling parameters in a silicon double quantum dot](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09638)
*Daniel J. King,Minyoung Kim,J. Reily,Jonathan C. Marcks,Mark Friesen,Benjamin D. Woods,M. A. Eriksson*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文完整表征了硅量子点（quantum dot）中谷内和谷间隧穿耦合（intravalley and intervalley tunnel couplings），重点揭示了其复相位——即谷相位（valley phases）。研究表明，谷相位控制双量子点反交叉能隙比值等可测量参数，并随栅极电压和量子阱原子结构变化，填补了对谷耦合样本变异及其依赖物理参数（如自旋-轨道耦合、谷-轨道混合、朗德g因子）理解的关键空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究对谷内和谷间隧穿耦合进行了完整表征，特别关注其复相位部分——即谷相位。分析依赖于量子点栅极电压的调控以及量子阱底层原子结构的影响，通过测量双量子点（double quantum dot）量子态间反交叉（anticrossing）处的能隙比来揭示谷相位的可观测效应。

Result: 谷相位被证明能够控制双量子点量子态间反交叉处的能隙比例等可测量参数。谷相位本身随量子点栅极电压的变化而演化，并依赖于量子阱的底层原子结构。

Conclusion: 对谷相位的认识完善了硅量子点隧穿耦合的整体图景，填补了对样本范围谷耦合变异（sample-wide variations of valley couplings）及其依赖物理参数理解的关键空白。这些参数包括自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）、谷-轨道混合（valley-orbit mixing）和朗德g因子（Landé g-factors）。

Abstract: Tunneling is essential in the initialization, measurement, and control of quantum dot qubits. In silicon, such tunneling connects not only the qubit states but also valley minima in the conduction band on opposite sides of the Brillouin zone, with large consequences for the quantum dot behavior. Here we present a full characterization of the intravalley and intervalley tunnel couplings, including their complex phases -- the valley phases. These phases are shown to control measurable parameters, including the ratios of the gaps at anticrossings between quantum states of a double quantum dot. The valley phases themselves evolve as a function of the quantum dot gate voltages and depend on the underlying atomic structure of the quantum well. Knowledge of the valley phases completes the picture and fills a key gap in our understanding of sample-wide variations of valley couplings and the physical parameters that depend on them, including spin-orbit coupling, valley-orbit mixing, and Landé $g$-factors.

### [138] [Non-Equilibrium Economics: A Physicist's Point of View](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09620)
*Jean-Philippe Bouchaud*

Main category: econ.TH

TL;DR: 本文从物理学视角论证，在经济这类大型复杂相互作用系统中，均衡（equilibrium）概念很可能是例外而非普遍规律。通过一系列程式化"玩具"模型（toy model），展示过度波动、内生性危机与崩盘、通货膨胀膨胀和持续不平等如何自发产生于真正的非均衡动力学（out-of-equilibrium dynamics），而无需借助大规模外生冲击。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解经济体系中泡沫与崩盘等极端事件的起源是经济理论的核心问题之一。主流经济理论以均衡概念为基石，但经济体是否本质上不稳定，以及能否"稳定不稳定的经济体"，仍有待深入探讨。

Method: 采用物理学视角，通过一系列程式化"玩具"模型，分析大型复杂相互作用系统中的非均衡动力学行为，并归纳出三种反复出现的通用机制：历史依赖的多重均衡陷阱、动态无法达到均衡导致的振荡与混沌、以及自发演化至脆弱边缘稳定态的自组织临界性（self-organized criticality）。

Result: 识别出三种通用机制：多重均衡导致的历史依赖与锁定；动态无法收敛至均衡引发的振荡与混沌；系统自发趋向脆弱边缘稳定态的自组织临界性。研究表明，过度波动、内生性危机、通胀膨胀及持续不平等均可由非均衡动力学自然产生，无需外生大冲击。

Conclusion: 这些发现目前属于现象学场景（phenomenological scenarios）而非经过校准的理论，尚不存在"确凿证据"。但作者主张，举证责任应转移到均衡（equilibrium）阵营一方。

Abstract: Financial and economic history is strewn with bubbles and crashes, booms and busts, crises and upheavals of all sorts. Understanding the origin of these events is arguably one of the most important problems in economic theory: are economies intrinsically unstable, and can one ``stabilize unstable economies''? In this review I argue, from a physicist's vantage point, that the concept of equilibrium -- so central to mainstream economic thinking -- is likely to be the exception rather than the rule in large, complex, interacting systems. Drawing on a series of stylized ``toy'' models, I show how excess volatility, endogenous crises and crashes, inflation swells and persistent inequalities can all emerge naturally from genuinely out-of-equilibrium dynamics, without invoking large exogenous shocks. Three generic mechanisms recur throughout: trapping in a multiplicity of history-dependent equilibria; the impossibility of dynamically reaching equilibrium, leading to oscillations and chaos; and the spontaneous evolution towards fragile, marginally stable states -- the self-organized criticality paradigm. I stress that these are phenomenological scenarios rather than calibrated theories: there is, at this stage, no ``smoking gun''. But the burden of proof, I contend, should be on the equilibrium camp.

</details>

### [139] [A certified refinement and asymptotic analysis of the Kuznetsov-Sahinidis diameter bound for Lennard-Jones clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09555)
*Guillaume Lecomte*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文针对 Kuznetsov 和 Sahinidis（2025）提出的 Lennard-Jones 团簇直径界进行了严格改进，利用子集不等式与已知极小值构建逐层认证估计，在 5 ≤ N ≤ 200 范围内对 92 个尺寸实现了一层的收紧，并导出了该界的渐近形式 ρ_KS = N - Θ(√N)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lennard-Jones 团簇的全局优化问题中，先验直径界（a priori diameter bound）直接决定了确定性求解器（deterministic solver）的搜索区域；收紧该界可缩小搜索空间，提升求解效率。Kuznetsov 和 Sahinidis（2025）给出的直径界存在可改进空间，且其渐近行为未被完全确定。

Method: 利用 Kuznetsov 和 Sahinidis 自身的子集不等式（subset inequality）与已知极小值 V_5^*、V_6^* 构建认证估计，替代原方法中每单位宽度层采用最松内能 -C(n,2) 的做法。通过最小化种群分布（population profiles）上的逐层界，并采用中心递减分布（centred decreasing profiles）作为候选最小值；使用重排不等式（rearrangement inequality）实现无排列松弛（arrangement-free relaxation），所有比较在定向舍入算术（directed-rounding arithmetic）下重新验证。

Result: 对 5 ≤ N ≤ 200 的 92 个尺寸实现了较原始界一层的收紧。导出了该界的渐近形式 ρ_KS = N - Θ(√N)，完善了 Kuznetsov 和 Sahinidis 遗留的问题；改进本身的增益以 Θ(√N) 层增长，并给出了精确渐近常数。下游测试表明，在唯一可解的小尺寸（N ≤ 6）上，直径框（diameter box）并非确定性求解器的资源瓶颈；改进影响的较大尺寸（N ≥ 38）尚无求解器可运行。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一个严格收紧的先验界的理论注记（theoretical note），而非解决某个开放全局优化问题。改进机制源于对层能量估计的精细化，且通过重排不等式实现了对所有分布形式的认证封闭。

Abstract: Kuznetsov and Sahinidis (J. Glob. Optim., 2025) prove distance bounds that confine optimal Lennard-Jones clusters and shrink the search region of deterministic solvers; their diameter bound charges each unit-width layer the loosest internal energy $-\binom{n}{2}$. We replace this by a certified estimate built from their own subset inequality and the proven minima $V_5^*$, $V_6^*$, and minimize the resulting layer bound over population profiles. Centred decreasing profiles supply candidate minima; an arrangement-free relaxation, whose only classical ingredient is the rearrangement inequality for sequences, closes every certificate over all profiles; and all comparisons are re-verified in directed-rounding arithmetic. For $5 \le N \le 200$ this certifies a one-layer improvement of the published bound at 92 sizes. The improvement resolves no open global-optimization case: it is a rigorous tightening of a published a priori bound, with a precise account of the mechanism. A direct downstream test on the only tractable sizes ($N \le 6$) finds the diameter box is not the binding resource for a deterministic solver there, and no solver runs at the sizes the refinement affects ($N \ge 38$); we therefore present the result as a theoretical note. We also derive the asymptotic form of the bound, $ρ_{KS} = N - Θ(\sqrt{N})$, resolving a point left open by Kuznetsov and Sahinidis; the gain of the refinement itself grows like $Θ(\sqrt{N})$ layers, with an exact asymptotic constant.

</details>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [140] [Commissioning and Low Latency Operation of the Graph Neural Network Electromagnetic Calorimeter Trigger at the Belle II Experiment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09347)
*M. Neu,F. Baptist,I. Haide,Y. Unno,J. Becker,T. Ferber,K. Arai,Y. -T. Lai,T. Koga,M. Maushart,H. Nakazawa,V. Savinov,K. Unger*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报告了Belle II实验中基于图神经网络（GNN）的电磁量能器触发模块（GNN-ETM）的调试与运行。该模块将量能器触发单元处理为图节点（graph nodes）进行聚类和特征提取，通过硬件-算法协同设计（hardware-algorithm co-design）优化了基于FPGA的架构，实现了1.053微秒的系统延迟，并通过寄存器传输级（RTL）仿真验证了与离线参考模型的比特级一致性。在线监测功能可测量瞬时触发率，使该模块成为完全可运行、低延迟且具备在线控制与监测能力的触发模块。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能物理实验（high-energy physics experiment）的实时触发系统需要低延迟（low-latency）和高精度的在线数据处理能力。Belle II实验的第一级触发系统（first-level trigger）对延迟有严格限制，传统方法难以同时满足聚类（clustering）与特征提取（feature extraction）的复杂性和实时性要求。

Method: 采用图神经网络（graph neural network, GNN）方法，将电磁量能器（electromagnetic calorimeter）的触发单元（trigger cells）作为图节点处理，在图结构上进行聚类和特征提取。基于FPGA架构，通过硬件-算法协同设计（hardware-algorithm co-design）进行系统优化，并开发了慢控制驱动（slow-control drivers）和在线监测（online monitoring）功能。

Result: 实现了1.053微秒的系统总延迟，满足Belle II第一级触发系统的延迟要求。通过寄存器传输级（register-transfer-level, RTL）仿真验证了硬件实现，与离线参考模型达到比特级一致（bit-accurate agreement）。在线监测可测量瞬时触发率（instantaneous trigger rates），为触发级性能研究提供定量依据。

Conclusion: GNN-ETM是一个完全可运行（fully operational）、低延迟的触发模块，具备在线控制和监测能力，与Belle II第一级触发系统的延迟要求兼容。该成果展示了图神经网络在高能物理实时触发系统中的可行性。

Abstract: We present the commissioning and operation of the Graph Neural Network Electromagnetic Calorimeter Trigger Module (GNN-ETM) of the Belle II experiment at the SuperKEKB collider. The GNN-ETM processes calorimeter trigger cells as graph nodes to perform clustering and feature extraction. We fully integrate the system with the successive stages of the first-level trigger, develop slow-control drivers, and add online monitoring capabilities. We optimise the existing FPGA-based architecture through hardware-algorithm co-design, achieving an overall system latency of 1.053 us. Our hardware implementation is validated through register-transfer-level simulations, achieving bit-accurate agreement with the offline reference model. Online monitoring enables the measurement of instantaneous trigger rates, providing a quantitative basis for trigger-level performance studies. In summary, we report on the GNN-ETM as a fully operational, low-latency trigger module with online control and monitoring capabilities, compatible with the latency requirements of the Belle II first-level trigger system.

</details>


### [141] [Constraints on Sub-MeV Dark Matter from Solar Reflection with DAMIC-M](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09352)
*K. Aggarwal,I. Arnquist,N. Avalos,X. Bertou,N. Castello-Mor,C. Centeno-Lorca,A. E. Chavarria,A. R. Chriss,J. Cuevas-Zepeda,A. Dastgheibi-Fard,C. De Dominicis,O. Deligny,J. Duarte-Campderros,E. Estrada,R. Gaıor,E. -L. Gkougkousis,T. Hossbach,L. Iddir,B. J. Kavanagh,B. Kilminster,I. Lawson,A. Letessier-Selvon,H. Lin,P. Loaiza,A. Lopez-Virto,R. Lou,H. Lumengo-Kidimbu,S. Munagavalasa,J. Noonan,D. Norcini,S. Paul,P. Perez-Cobo,P. Privitera,P. Robmann,B. Roach,D. Rosenmerkel,M. Settimo,R. Smida,M. Traina,R. Vilar,R. Yajur,D. Venegas-Vargas,C. Zhu,Y. Zhu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究利用DAMIC-M原型探测器的硅跳线电荷耦合器件（silicon skipper CCDs）获取约1.3公斤·天的数据，首次对太阳反射暗物质（solar-reflected dark matter, SRDM）给出了实验约束。在重媒介子和超轻媒介子两种基准下，在0.1 MeV质量点分别得到90%置信度的上限，其中超轻媒介子的限制可与世界领先结果竞争，填补了恒星冷却界限与标准晕搜索之间的参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统直接探测实验依赖于银河系标准晕中的暗物质（dark matter）通量，对亚MeV质量的暗物质粒子灵敏度有限。太阳可作为天然暗物质加速器，将银河系晕粒子散射至逃逸速度以上，产生增强通量，拓展直接探测的动力学范围进入亚MeV质量区间。因此有必要利用太阳反射暗物质机制对低质量暗物质进行实验约束。

Method: 利用DAMIC-M原型探测器在Modane地下实验室获取约1.3公斤·天数据，采用硅跳线电荷耦合器件（silicon skipper charge coupled devices, CCDs）进行探测。通过分析低能电子反冲（low-energy electron recoils）的空间扩散信号特征，对暗物质-电子散射截面进行约束。研究考虑了重媒介子（heavy mediator）和超轻媒介子（ultralight mediator）两种相互作用基准模型。

Result: 在90%置信水平下给出暗物质-电子散射截面上限，0.1 MeV质量点时达到$\barσ_e\sim 3.16 \cdot 10^{-37} \rm{cm^2}$。超轻媒介子基准下的结果可与世界领先约束相竞争。这些结果探及恒星冷却界限（stellar-cooling bounds）与地面标准晕搜索之间此前无法触及的参数空间。

Conclusion: DAMIC-M原型探测器的数据首次对太阳反射暗物质模型提供了实验约束，证明了利用硅跳线CCD技术探测亚MeV质量暗物质的可行性。所得限制在超轻媒介子情景下达到世界领先水平，填补了低质量暗物质直接探测参数空间中的空白区域。

Abstract: The Sun acts as a natural dark matter accelerator. Galactic halo particles scattering in the solar plasma emerge with velocities well beyond the Galactic escape speed, providing a boosted flux that extends the kinematic reach of direct detection experiments into the sub-MeV mass regime. We present constraints on solar-reflected dark matter (SRDM) from the DAMIC-M prototype detector using $\sim$1.3~kg-day of data acquired with silicon skipper charge coupled devices (CCDs) at the Modane Underground Laboratory. Exploiting the spatial diffusion signature of low-energy electron recoils, we derive 90% C.L. upper limits on the DM-electron scattering cross section for both heavy- and ultralight-mediator benchmarks, reaching $\barσ_e\sim 3.16 \cdot 10^{-37} \rm{cm^2}$ at $0.1$ MeV. For the ultralight mediator, our limits are competitive with the world-leading constraints, achieved with an integrated exposure of $\sim1.3$~kg-day. These results probe the parameter space between stellar-cooling bounds and terrestrial limits from standard halo searches, a region inaccessible to direct detection experiments relying solely on the standard halo flux.

</details>


### [142] [Search for soft unclustered energy patterns in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV using data scouting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09621)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文利用CMS实验在LHC上收集的127 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据，通过数据流扫描（data scouting stream）方法降低强子触发阈值，搜索软非簇射能量模式（SUEPs）。观测结果与标准模型（standard model）本底预测一致，但对胶子融合产生的重标量媒介子导致的SUEP类信号给出了迄今最严格的排除限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SUEP信号由隐藏谷模型（hidden-valley model）在大't Hooft耦合（'t Hooft coupling）下预言，其特征是大量低动量、空间分布弥散的软粒子，传统触发阈值难以有效捕获；因此需要采用低阈值的触发策略以提高信号接受度（acceptance）。

Method: 基于CMS实验在质心能量13 TeV、积分亮度127 fb⁻¹的质子-质子对撞数据，仅记录高 Level 触发（high-level trigger）重建结果以降低强子活动阈值，利用数据流扫描流实现低阈值采集。

Result: 观测数据与标准模型本底预测在误差范围内一致；对胶子融合（gluon fusion）产生重标量媒介子（heavy scalar mediator）进而衰变为SUEP类信号的产生截面给出了目前最严格的排除上限。

Conclusion: 当前数据未发现SUEP信号存在证据，但低阈值数据流扫描方法有效拓展了对隐藏谷模型参数空间的探测能力，并设定了该信号模型下最强的实验约束。

Abstract: A search for soft unclustered energy patterns (SUEPs) is conducted using proton-proton collision data corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 127 fb$^{-1}$ at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV, collected via the data scouting stream of the CMS experiment at the LHC. Only the results of the high-level trigger reconstruction are recorded to enable a lower threshold on the hadronic activity. This increases the acceptance for SUEP signatures, which are predicted by hidden-valley models with a large 't Hooft coupling. The observed results are consistent with the standard model background prediction. The most stringent limits to date are set on the gluon fusion production of heavy scalar mediators resulting in SUEP-like signals.

</details>

### [143] [Seeing inside a Plasmonic Nanogap: Few-molecule Orientation and Preferential Adsorption](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08922)
*Francesco Ciccarello,Nobuaki Oyamada,Thwahira Shirin Alampara,Konstantin Malchow,Christophe Galland*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出利用等离激元增强非线性振动光谱（plasmon-enhanced nonlinear vibrational spectroscopy）作为研究金属纳米结（metallic nanojunctions）内分子-表面相互作用的有效工具，通过双共振纳米腔（dual-resonant nanocavities）中同时产生的振动和频与差频（vibrational sum- and difference-frequency generation），实现了对分子取向（molecular orientation）和偏好性吸附（preferential binding）的分辨，并发现非共振二阶非线性响应（non-resonant second-order nonlinear response）受分子-表面相互作用调控，而非金属表面的本征属性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分子-表面相互作用（molecule-surface interactions）广泛存在于异相催化（heterogeneous catalysis）、聚合物科学（polymer science）和电化学（electrochemistry）等领域，尤其对于分子电子学（molecular electronics）和近场光谱学（near-field spectroscopy）中使用的金属纳米间隙（metallic nanogaps）至关重要。然而，由于这类双界面（double interfaces）的埋藏特性，现有方法难以监测界面特异性（side-specific）相互作用及间隙内分子的相对取向（relative molecular orientation）。

Method: 作者引入了等离激元增强非线性振动光谱（plasmon-enhanced nonlinear vibrational spectroscopy），利用双共振纳米腔（dual-resonant nanocavities）同时激发振动和频产生（vibrational sum-frequency generation）与振动差频产生（vibrational difference-frequency generation）。该方法可实现对两个金表面中特定表面的分子取向和偏好性吸附进行分辨，并具备少量分子（few-molecule）级别的灵敏度。

Result: 该方法成功分辨了分子在金属纳米结内的取向及对其中一个金表面的偏好性吸附。此外，研究还发现非共振（电子）二阶非线性响应（non-resonant (electronic) second-order nonlinear response）并非金属表面的本征属性，而是由分子-表面相互作用（molecule-surface interaction）所决定。

Conclusion: 该发现提供了一种强大的分析工具，可作为拉曼光谱（Raman spectroscopy）的附加模块简便实现，得益于市面上已有的中红外量子级联激光器（mid-infrared quantum cascade lasers）。

Abstract: Molecule-surface interactions are central to many research and technological areas, spanning from heterogeneous catalysis and polymer science to electrochemistry. Of particular relevance are metallic nanogaps used in molecular electronics and near-field spectroscopy. Due to the buried nature of these double interfaces, few methods exist to monitor side-specific interactions and relative molecular orientation inside the gap. In this work, we introduce plasmon-enhanced nonlinear vibrational spectroscopy as an efficient tool to investigate surface molecular adsorption within metallic nanojunctions. By exploiting simultaneous vibrational sum- and difference-frequency generation in dual-resonant nanocavities, we resolve molecular orientation and preferential binding to one of the two gold surfaces, with few-molecule sensitivity. We also discover that the non-resonant (electronic) second-order nonlinear response is not an intrinsic property of the metal surface, but is instead governed by the molecule-surface interaction. Our findings provide a powerful analytical tool, easily implementable as an add-on to Raman spectroscopy, thanks to commercially available mid-infrared quantum cascade lasers.

</details>
