### [144] [Energetics of fractional anomalous Hall crystals in rhombohedral graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08822)
*Félix Desrochers,Ashvin Vishwanath*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过变分波函数和蒙特卡罗方法，在菱形五层石墨烯（R5G）中证明分数量子反常霍尔晶体（FAHC）是能量上竞争性的候选态，并建立了其稳定性原理：每个晶体映射到一个母体量子霍尔液体，动能则倾向于匹配R5G墨西哥帽色散的有限动量极小值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分数量子反常霍尔晶体（FAHC）此前仅限于理论推测或工程模型，尚未在真实物理系统中被确证。本研究旨在回答FAHC能否在现实材料中作为能量竞争态出现这一核心问题。

Method: 以菱形五层石墨烯（rhombohedral pentalayer graphene, R5G）为平台，构造变分波函数（variational wavefunctions），该波函数是最近提出的理想R5G模型的精确零模态。在恢复真实色散（realistic dispersion）和屏蔽库仑相互作用（screened Coulomb interactions）后，利用蒙特卡罗（Monte Carlo）方法评估其能量。

Result: FAHC在能量上与整数反常霍尔晶体（integer anomalous Hall crystals）和费米液体（Fermi liquids）具有竞争力。其稳定性遵循一个简单原理：每个晶体映射到一个母体量子霍尔液体（parent quantum Hall liquid）以确定相互作用能，动能则偏好匹配R5G墨西哥帽色散（Mexican-hat dispersion）有限动量极小值的晶体周期。弱周期势可选择性地降低并钉扎（pin）公度分数量子晶体。

Conclusion: 该图像预测了整数和分数量子反常霍尔稳定性窗口随扭转角（twist angle）和位移场（displacement field）的演化，并与近期实验比较。研究结果支持一种“连续模型与相互作用优先”的路径，用于在菱形石墨烯中实现分数量子反常霍尔态。

Abstract: Fractional anomalous Hall crystals (FAHCs) replicate the topological order of the fractional quantum Hall effect in the continuum without requiring any external magnetic field. They spontaneously break continuous translation symmetry like a Wigner crystal, but are distinguished by each unit cell holding a fixed fractional number of electrons. Until now, these states have been confined to theoretical speculation or engineered models, leaving open the question of whether they can plausibly emerge in actual physical systems. Here, we establish them as energetically competitive candidate states in a realistic material setting. We study rhombohedral pentalayer graphene (R5G) with variational wavefunctions that are exact zero modes of a recently proposed ideal model of R5G. We evaluate their energies using Monte Carlo, after reinstating realistic dispersion and screened Coulomb interactions. We find FAHCs to be energetically competitive with integer anomalous Hall crystals and Fermi liquids, and their stability follows a simple principle. Each crystal maps onto a parent quantum Hall liquid that fixes its interaction energy, while the kinetic energy favors crystal periods that match the finite-momentum minimum of R5G's Mexican-hat dispersion. A weak periodic potential can then selectively lower and pin the commensurate fractional crystals. This picture predicts how the integer and fractional quantum anomalous Hall stability windows evolve with twist angle and displacement field, which we compare to recent experiments. These results support a continuum-and-interactions-first route to fractional anomalous Hall states in rhombohedral graphene.

</details>


### [145] [The monopole plasma resonance: a smoking gun of 3D $U(1)$ quantum spin liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08826)
*Anish Koley,Saranyo Moitra,Inti Sodemann Villadiego*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本论文指出，在三维 U(1) 量子自旋液体（如偶极量子自旋冰）中，涌现磁单极子携带物理电荷并形成低温等离子体，由此产生类似金属的尖锐等离子体共振，可作为探测该物态的实验指纹，并以 Ce₂Zr₂O₇ 为例讨论了最优观测条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找可清晰识别三维 U(1) 量子自旋液体（3D U(1) spin liquid）的实验特征，以解决该类物态在材料中难以检测的问题。

Method: 通过理论分析，研究偶极量子自旋冰（dipolar quantum spin ice）中涌现磁单极子（emergent monopole）的对称性变换性质及其与涌现规范场（emergent gauge field）的耦合，从而推导体系的电动力学响应。

Result: 该体系在直流（DC）输运下表现为电绝缘体（electrical insulator），但在甚低频率下可呈现类似金属的尖锐等离子体共振（plasma resonance），该共振源于磁单极子形成的低温等离子体（plasma）。

Conclusion: 该等离子共振可作为检测三维 U(1) 自旋液体的清晰实验指纹，并在候选材料 Ce₂Zr₂O₇ 中讨论了实现该现象的最优条件。

Abstract: Certain 3D $U(1)$ spin liquids, such as those arising in dipolar quantum spin ice, have an emergent monopole which is the source of an emergent magnetic field that transforms under symmetries like an electric polarization. As a consequence, these monopoles carry a physical electric charge in their cores and form a plasma at low temperatures. Due to the monopole coupling to emergent gauge fields, the full system behaves as an electrical insulator for DC transport, but can display a sharp plasma resonance analogous to a metal at very low frequencies. This can serve as a clear fingerprint to detect these states in materials. We discuss the optimal conditions to observe this phenomenon in the 3D $U(1)$ spin-liquid candidate Ce$_2$Zr$_2$O$_7$.

</details>


### [146] [Magnetic Field Control of the Néel Vector and Magnon Visibility in Altermagnetic MnTe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08829)
*Tobias Weber,Niclas Heinsdorf,Shane Smolenski,Sawyer Beltz,Alexandre Ivanov,Andrea Piovano,Victor Mecoli,Sean Knapp,Ruiqi Tang,Amir Henderson,A. K. M. Ashiquzzaman Shawon,Taylor Pierce-James,Na Hyun Jo,Denis Karaiskaj*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本论文通过非弹性中子散射和线性自旋波理论，研究了交变磁性α-MnTe在磁场下的自旋波谱。发现面内磁场可连续重取向奈尔矢量，虽不改变磁振子能量和线宽，但通过横向动量投影显著改变谱强度，表明该材料可实现可重构磁振子耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁性（altermagnetism）即使在没有净磁化的情况下，也能导致电子和磁振子激发的动量依赖自旋劈裂。本研究旨在探索交变磁体α-MnTe的自旋波谱在磁场下的行为，特别是磁场如何影响其磁振子激发及其可重构性。

Method: 采用非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering）进行实验测量，并结合线性自旋波理论（linear spin-wave theory）进行理论分析，系统研究面内磁场对α-MnTe自旋波谱的影响。

Result: 面内磁场通过克服弱晶体各向异性（weak crystalline anisotropy）连续重取向奈尔矢量（Néel vector），该重取向基本不改变磁振子能量和线宽，但通过横向动量投影（transverse-momentum projection）显著改变测量的谱强度。

Conclusion: 结果表明，反铁磁序的软取向自由度（soft orientational degree of freedom）与强交换主导的手性磁振子谱（chiral magnon spectrum）之间存在清晰分离，使α-MnTe成为可重构磁振子耦合的平台，外部磁场可调谐激发与极化探针的相互作用，而不显著改变其频率或相干性。

Abstract: Altermagnetic order gives rise to momentum-dependent spin splitting of electronic and magnonic excitations even in the absence of a net magnetization. Here, we investigate the magnetic field dependence of the spin-wave spectrum of altermagnetic $α$-MnTe using inelastic neutron scattering and linear spin-wave theory. An in-plane magnetic field continuously reorients the Néel vector by overcoming the weak crystalline anisotropy, while remaining small compared with the dominant exchange scale. We find that this reorientation leaves the magnon energies and line widths essentially unchanged, but strongly modifies the measured spectral intensity through the transverse-momentum projection. Our results demonstrate a clear separation between the soft orientational degree of freedom of the antiferromagnetic order and the robust exchange-dominated chiral magnon spectrum. This combination establishes $α$-MnTe as a platform for reconfigurable magnon coupling, in which external fields tune how excitations interact with polarized probes without substantially altering their frequency or coherence.

</details>


### [147] [Loop-current orderings in SU($N$) two-leg fermionic ladder through duality symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08862)
*M. Habchy,F. Rose,P. Lecheminant*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究半填充SU($N$)双腿费米子梯子模型中环电流有序相的形成，通过低能方法发现非微扰对偶对称性，将两种自发破缺时间反演对称性的环电流相与传统的密度波相对偶，并在引入SU($N$)洪德耦合时通过微扰重整化群稳定了这些相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索半填充SU($N$)双腿费米子梯子模型中环电流有序相的形成机制，并揭示其与密度波相之间的对偶关系及其稳定性条件。

Method: 采用低能方法（low-energy approach）发现非微扰对偶对称性（non-perturbative duality symmetries），并结合微扰重整化群方法（perturbative renormalization group approach）分析相稳定性。

Result: 发现在半填充SU($N$)双腿费米子梯子模型中存在四种竞争序，其中两种为自发破缺时间反演对称性的环电流有序相；通过格点上精确的密度-电流对偶对称性，证明了这些环电流相与传统的密度波相（电荷密度波和键密度波）互为对偶；对于$N>2$的情况，引入SU($N$)洪德耦合（Hund's interaction）后，这些相可在半填充Hubbard梯子模型中被稳定。

Conclusion: 环电流有序相可通过密度-电流对偶对称性与传统密度波相联系，且当$N>2$并引入洪德耦合时，这些非常规相在微扰重整化群框架下是稳定的。此外，文章还讨论了轻微掺杂对这些相的影响。

Abstract: We investigate the formation of loop-current ordered phases in half-filled SU($N$) two-leg fermionic ladders. Using a low-energy approach, we uncover the existence of non-perturbative duality symmetries relating four competing orders. Two of these orders correspond to loop-current ordered phases that spontaneously break the time-reversal symmetry and describe charge currents circulating in a staggered pattern either around the plaquettes or along the diagonals of the ladder. These unconventional phases are shown to be dual to conventional (charge and bond) density-wave phases through an exact density-current duality symmetry existing on the lattice. From a perturbative renormalization group approach, we find that these phases for $N>2$ are stabilized in a half-filled SU($N$) two-leg Hubbard ladder with an additional SU($N$) Hund's interaction. The effect of a small doping on these phases is also discussed.

Abstract: Materials characterized by competing interactions often exhibit a large number of nearly degenerate periodic states. Here we show that layered UAgBi$_2$ hosts a cascade of field- and temperature-induced magnetic transitions. Based on specific heat, thermal expansion, and neutron diffraction, we construct a phase diagram that reveals at least seven nearly degenerate magnetic states in UAgBi$_2$. The observed multi-step magnetization process can be understood by square-wave structures with distinct propagation vectors $\mathbf{k}$=(0, 0, \textit{k}) in the presence of strong easy-axis anisotropy that confines the moments along the \textit{c} axis. Our findings are consistent with a magnetic devil's staircase described by the axial next-nearest neighbor Ising (ANNNI) model and place UAgBi$_2$ as a rare realization of the devil's staircase in a 5\textit{f}-electron system.

### [149] [Topological phase transition driven by Hatsugai-Kohmoto interaction on the Kagome lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09182)
*Zhuo-Xuan Yang,Jiangfan Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过将Kane-Mele型自旋轨道耦合与Hatsugai-Kohmoto相互作用结合，在Kagome晶格上构建了一个精确可解模型。在1/3填充下，发现了由电子相互作用驱动的连续拓扑量子相变：弱关联的$\mathbb{Z}_2$拓扑绝缘体转变为强关联绝缘体（$\mathbb{Z}_2$平庸但具有非平庸自旋陈数$C_s=2$）；在半填充下，该模型展现出非费米液体到莫特绝缘体的转变，从而在单一可解框架内统一了关联驱动的拓扑相变与莫特相变。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在Kagome晶格上，将Kane-Mele型自旋轨道耦合与Hatsugai-Kohmoto相互作用相结合，构建了一个精确可解的模型。通过对不同填充（1/3填充和半填充）下的基态性质进行解析分析，研究了相互作用驱动的相变行为。

Result: 在1/3填充下，观测到从弱关联$\mathbb{Z}_2$拓扑绝缘体（topological insulator）到强关联绝缘体的连续拓扑量子相变；该强关联绝缘体虽在$\mathbb{Z}_2$拓扑意义上是平庸的，但具有非平庸的自旋陈数$C_s=2$（spin Chern number）。相变表现出与二维狄拉克费米子（two-dimensional Dirac fermions）普适类一致的临界标度行为。在半填充下，同一模型产生从非费米液体（non-Fermi liquid）到莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）的转变。

Conclusion: 该研究证明，关联驱动的拓扑相变和莫特相变可以在一个可解框架内实现统一。Kagome Hatsugai-Kohmoto模型为研究相互作用拓扑系统提供了一个有价值的基准模型（benchmark）。

Abstract: The interplay between band topology and strong correlations is central to modern condensed matter physics, but exact solutions are rare. Here, we present an exactly solvable model on the Kagome lattice by combining a Kane-Mele-type spin-orbit coupling with the Hatsugai-Kohmoto interaction. At 1/3 filling, we uncover a continuous topological quantum phase transition driven by electron interaction. A weakly correlated $\mathbb{Z}_2$ topological insulator gives way to a strongly correlated insulator that, while $\mathbb{Z}_2$-trivial, hosts a nontrivial spin Chern number $C_s=2$. The transition exhibits critical scaling consistent with the universality class of two-dimensional Dirac fermions. At half-filling, the same model yields a non-Fermi-liquid to Mott-insulator transition, demonstrating that correlation-driven topological and Mott transitions can be unified within a single solvable framework. Our results establish the Kagome Hatsugai-Kohmoto model as a valuable benchmark for interacting topological systems.

### [150] [Effective theories for many-body systems with nonuniform symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09427)
*Aleksander Głódkowski*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文发展了一个统一的理论框架（unified framework），用于描述具有非均匀对称性（nonuniform symmetries）的多体系统。研究表明，非均匀对称性不引入新的低能无隙模式，而是通过额外的辅助场产生运动学约束（kinematic constraints），从而重塑红外动力学，并在自发对称破缺和有限温度下分别导致修正的色散关系和流体力学约束，进而产生诸如横波Tkachenko振荡和反常慢扩散等新物理现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管均匀对称性（uniform symmetries）下的低能动力学已得到充分理解——包括Goldstone定理和流体力学（hydrodynamics）对应关系——但非均匀对称性（nonuniform symmetries）的低能效应仍知之甚少，因为这类对称性的生成元不与时空平移对易，且不引入额外的无隙模式，而是约束已有自由度。动机在于弥补这一理论空白。

Method: 论文发展了一个统一框架，将非均匀对称性的效应理解为引入额外的辅助场（additional fields），这些场在低能下并非独立，可被消去，从而产生运动学约束（kinematic constraints），进而重构有效理论。该方法统一处理了零温度下的自发对称破缺情形和有限温度下的流体力学（hydrodynamics）情形。

Result: 在自发对称破缺系统中，该机制修正了有效理论，通常使剩余模式的色散关系（dispersion relations）变软；在有限温度下，表现为对宏观流（macroscopic currents）的流体力学约束。由此产生了新的物理现象，包括集体激发谱的修正（如量子涡旋晶体中的横波Tkachenko振荡）以及非常规输运现象（如偶极守恒系统中的反常慢扩散和软化声模）。

Conclusion: 非均匀对称性虽不产生新的无隙模式，但通过运动学约束显著影响多体系统的低能动力学，导致定性的新物理现象。该统一框架为理解此类对称性在零温和有限温度下的效应提供了系统的方法。

Abstract: The low-energy dynamics of many-body systems is governed by gapless modes whose properties are dictated by symmetry. Their existence follows from Goldstone's theorem, while their effective description at zero temperature is determined by the pattern of symmetry breaking. At finite temperature, an analogous role is played by hydrodynamics, which describes the universal behavior of many-body systems over long times and large distances. These principles are well understood for uniform symmetries, which act homogeneously in spacetime and lead to a correspondence between massless Goldstone modes and broken generators, as well as gapless hydrodynamic modes and conserved charges. However, this simple picture changes in the presence of nonuniform symmetries, whose generators do not commute with spacetime translations. The low-energy implications of these symmetries remain less understood, as they do not introduce additional gapless modes but instead constrain the dynamics of the existing degrees of freedom. In this thesis, we develop a unified framework for many-body systems with nonuniform symmetries and show that their effects can be understood in terms of additional fields that are not independent at low energies and can be eliminated, leading to kinematic constraints that reshape the infrared dynamics. In systems with spontaneous symmetry breaking, this mechanism modifies the effective theory and often softens the dispersion relations of the remaining modes. At finite temperature, it manifests in hydrodynamics as constraints on macroscopic currents. As a result, nonuniform symmetries give rise to qualitatively new physical phenomena, including modified spectra of collective excitations, exemplified by transverse Tkachenko oscillations in quantum vortex crystals, and unconventional transport phenomena, such as anomalously slow diffusion and softened sound modes in dipole-conserving systems.

</details>

*Shingo Kuniyoshi,Rikuto Oiwa,Satoru Hayami*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过引入与旋转兼容的规范对称性（canonical symmetries），即粒子数规范变换 Gπ/2 和粒子-空穴变换 CA，在传统多极框架基础上添加两个额外标签，以此对不同体数（body numbers）和粒子数变化（particle-number changes）的算子进行分类。

Result: 该方法实现了十六重分类（sixteenfold classification），能够系统性地组织多体多极空间中非零期望值的选择定则、诱导多极（induced multipoles）以及对称性允许的耦合。

Conclusion: 该框架为多体算子空间提供了更精细的结构刻画，有效弥补了传统多极框架的不足，为多体系统中对称性约束下的物理现象分析提供了系统化工具。

Abstract: The conventional multipole framework provides a standard symmetry-based language for one-body electronic degrees of freedom, but fails to distinguish physically distinct sectors in many-body operator space. We show that canonical symmetries compatible with rotations provide this structure through two additional 2 labels associated with the particle-number gauge transformation Gπ/2 and the particle-hole transformation CA. These labels separate operators with different body numbers and particle-number changes, leading to a sixteenfold classification that organizes selection rules for nonzero expectation values, induced multipoles, and symmetry-allowed couplings in many-body multipole space.

</details>

Abstract: We investigate the evolution of spin correlations and the nature of the multi-stage magnetic transition in the quasi-two-dimensional easy-plane van der Waals magnet $\rm CrCl_3$. By combining broadband ferromagnetic resonance (FMR) spectroscopy and DC SQUID magnetometry on mechanically exfoliated micro-flakes with non-local dynamical mean-field theory (DFT+DMFT) calculations, we analyze both long- and short range magnetic order in CrCl$_3$. Theoretically, we show the existence of highly stable local magnetic moments at room temperature, with a giant room temperature lifetime $τ$ of 130--300 ps due to a wide Mott bandgap. Below room temperature, a rapid growth of the in-plane correlation length $ξ$ signals the formation of strong short range magnetic order consistent with the experimental observations. We also obtain a temperature-driven crossover of the interlayer exchange interaction, which changes from positive (ferromagnetic) at high temperatures to negative (antiferromagnetic) in the low-temperature ordered phase.

Abstract: I critically overview my research on strongly correlated fermion systems for almost five decades. It concentrated on: (i) the first derivation of what is now called the t--J model, comprising both the limit of Anderson kinetic exchange of spin--spin interaction in the Mott--Hubbard insulator and taking into account real-space pairing, subsequently applied to high-temperature superconductivity; (ii) the concept of spin-dependent heavy mass of quasiparticles in heavy-fermion systems, and (iii) the first nontrivial model of statistical thermodynamics of the Mott--Hubbard transition. Some related questions such as introduction of atomicity in the chemical bonding (iv), and specific properties of correlated nanosystems within the rigorous EDABI (v) approach are also briefly elaborated at the end.

### [154] [Symmetry-Protected Pinch Curves in Classical Spin Liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09470)
*Takumi Fukushima,Han Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文引入了一类新的经典自旋液体——“夹点曲线自旋液体”（pinch-curve spin liquids），其中结构因子（structure factor）中的夹点奇异点（pinch singularities）在动量空间中形成一维代数曲线（algebraic curves），而非传统离散点。通过反演对称性（inversion symmetry）保护，进一步揭示了其代数可编程性、潜在微观机制以及红外高斯定律跃迁（infrared Gauss-law transition）现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典自旋液体（classical spin liquids）中已观察到局域约束（local constraints）导致的广泛简并（extensive degeneracy）与涌现规范结构（emergent gauge structures），表现为自旋结构因子中的夹点奇异点。本文旨在探索夹点奇异点能否进一步延伸形成连续曲线结构，并系统研究其对称性保护、几何可编程性及相应物理效应。

Method: 通过解析推导反演对称性对夹点曲线（pinch curves）的保护机制，将三维动量空间中的奇异性条件简化为两个实代数约束（real algebraic constraints）。构建具有直线与弯曲夹点轨迹（pinch loci）的晶格自旋模型（lattice spin models），并利用蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）验证预测的结构因子。

Result: 成功识别了产生直线与弯曲夹点轨迹的基本机制，构建了相应的晶格模型，模拟结果与理论预测相符。进一步发现夹点曲线中可发生红外高斯定律跃迁——尽管奇异轨迹仍保持一维，但主导局域约束及相关结构因子的各向异性标度（anisotropic scaling）发生改变。

Conclusion: 夹点曲线自旋液体拓展了经典自旋液体的奇异性拓扑分类，反演对称性在其中起关键保护作用，且该体系具备代数可编程性与新颖的红外跃迁行为，为进一步研究非传统自旋液体中的涌现规范场提供了新视角。

Abstract: Classical spin liquids are correlated paramagnets in which local constraints generate extensive degeneracy and emergent gauge structures, often observable as pinch-point singularities in spin structure factors. Here we introduce pinch-curve spin liquids, in which the pinch singularities form one-dimensional algebraic curves in momentum space. Inversion symmetry protects these curves by reducing the singularity condition to two real algebraic constraints in three dimensions, and the geometry of the pinch locus is algebraically programmable. We identify elementary mechanisms for generating straight and curved pinch loci, construct lattice spin models that realize them, and test the predicted structure factors using Monte Carlo simulations. We further show that pinch curves can host an infrared Gauss-law transition: the leading local constraint and the associated anisotropic scaling of the structure factor change, even though the singular locus remains one-dimensional.

</details>


### [155] [Quantum Chaos with a Macroscopic Zero-Mode Sector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09504)
*Cheryne Jonay,Kun W. Kim,Frank Pollmann,Alexander Altland*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文发现具有手征对称性（chiral symmetry）的约束自旋链（constrained spin chains）能够避免混沌多体谱（chaotic many-body spectra）密集填充能窗的预期，通过混沌能级排斥（chaotic level repulsion）在零能量处产生一个尖锐的能隙（sharp gap），从而支撑一个指数级大的对称保护零模（symmetry-protected exact zero modes）流形。作者在东西向动力学约束链（East-West kinetically constrained chain）中验证了这一机制，构建了最小随机矩阵描述（random-matrix description），并提出通过线性响应谱学（linear-response spectroscopy）探测该能隙的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混沌多体系统通常预期其能谱密集填充整个能量窗口，但近期研究表明某些约束系统可能打破这一预期，本文旨在揭示手征对称性如何使约束自旋链在零能量处产生大能隙和零模流形，并阐明其背后的物理机制。

Method: 采用东西向动力学约束链（East-West kinetically constrained chain）作为具体模型进行数值验证；发展了一个极简的随机矩阵理论（random-matrix theory）描述来刻画能隙的产生机制；提出通过线性响应谱学（linear-response spectroscopy）来实验检测该零能隙。

Result: 具有手征对称性的约束自旋链中存在一个指数级大的对称保护精确零模（exact zero modes）流形，这些零模与周围谱之间由零能量处的尖锐能隙（sharp gap）隔开；该能隙由混沌能级排斥（chaotic level repulsion）产生，其宽度正比于零模数目乘以平均能级间距（mean level spacing）。

Conclusion: 手征对称约束自旋链提供了一种在混沌多体系统中产生保护性零模和大能隙的新机制，该机制可通过线性响应谱学实验检测，为理解约束量子系统中的奇异谱结构和对称保护现象提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: Chaotic many-body spectra are expected to densely fill their energy window. We show that constrained spin chains with chiral symmetry evade this expectation by hosting an exponentially large manifold of symmetry-protected exact zero modes separated from the surrounding spectrum by a sharp gap at zero energy. The gap is generated by chaotic level repulsion, with width set by the number of zero modes times the mean level spacing. We verify this mechanism in an East-West kinetically constrained chain, develop a minimal random-matrix description, and show how the gap can be detected through linear-response spectroscopy.

</details>


### [156] [A nonstandard statistics for strongly correlated systems: Two simple examples](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09542)
*Józef Spałek,Piotr Kuterba,Mateusz Wójcik,Danuta Goc-Jagło,Maciej Fidrysiak,Leszek Spałek,Włodzimierz Wójcik*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文分析了强关联费米子统计的两种情形——非费米液体（NFL）和统计自旋液体（SSL），计算了各自的熵和统计分布函数，并重点研究了在二维方格半满填充下系统向莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）转变时，SSL统计与正常费米液体（Fermi liquid）统计之间的本质差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联费米子系统因其偏离传统费米液体行为而受到关注，但不同关联情形下的统计性质尚未被充分阐明。本文旨在通过分析非费米液体（non-Fermi liquid, NFL）和统计自旋液体（statistical spin liquid, SSL）两种情形，揭示其在莫特绝缘体转变点附近的统计分布差异。

Method: 通过引入两种不同的强关联费米子统计约束——NFL情形排除同一准动量态（quasimomentum state）上的双重自旋占据，SSL情形允许自旋跳跃并与空穴（hole）态混合——计算系统的熵（entropy）和相应的统计分布函数（statistical distribution function）。分析基于二维方格（two-dimensional square lattice）填充数 $n\in[0,1]$ 和相对温度 $k_B T/|t|$，其中 $t<0$ 为最近邻跳跃积分。

Result: 在半满填充（$n\to1$）的极限条件下，巡游费米子系统会转变为莫特绝缘体（Mott-insulator）态。该极限条件下，SSL统计与代表正常费米液体（normal Fermi-liquid）态的无关联费米子统计之间存在定性差异。

Conclusion: SSL统计在莫特绝缘体极限下展现出的统计行为与正常费米液体有本质不同，表明强关联效应在统计层面不可忽略，为理解强关联费米子系统的物态分类提供了新的统计视角。

Abstract: We discuss two different cases of strongly correlated fermions statistics. The first of them is the non-Fermi liquid (NFL) case, $i.e.$, that of fermions with exclusion of doubly occupancy of quasimomentum states $\{\bf k\}$ with opposite spins ($\uparrow\downarrow$). The second is that of statistical spin liquid (SSL) case, in which the fermion spins hop around and mix with the holes (unoccupied) states. For both cases we calculate the system entropy and the corresponding statistical distribution function, analyzed for a two-dimensional square-lattice filling $n\in [0,1]$ and relative temperature $k_B T/|t|$, where $t<0$ is the nearest neighbor hopping integral. We are particularly interested in the situation when the system of itinerant fermions reduce to the Mott-insulator state for the half-filled band ($n\to1$). This limiting situation signals a qualitative difference between the present SSL statistics and that of uncorrelated fermions representing normal Fermi-liquid state.

</details>


### [157] [Thermalization in a Height-Conserving Quantum Dimer Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.09580)
*Junsheng Feng,Jie Ren,Zheng Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文在方形晶格上的高度守恒量子二聚体模型（height-conserving quantum dimer model）中，通过解析绕数（winding numbers）、四子格高度（sublattice heights）和晶格动量（lattice momentum），隔离每个碎片化扇区（fragmented sector）中最大的连通Krylov分量，发现谱统计（spectral statistics）在不同动量扇区从近泊松（near-Poisson）到Wigner-Dyson分布变化，但本征态纠缠熵（eigenstate entanglement entropy）在所有扇区均呈现与热化一致的窄穹顶曲线，表明强约束量子系统中谱关联与本征态热化不必遵循相同的普适特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强约束量子系统的热化常被认为非常微妙：广泛的守恒律和动态冻结态（frozen states）会将希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）碎裂成多个不连通扇区。一个自然的问题是，一旦移除冻结态，单个扇区内部的动力学是否仍然能够热化。本文旨在回答该问题。

Method: 以方形晶格上高度守恒量子二聚体模型为研究对象，该模型的局域plaquette翻转（plaquette flips）保持一个涌现高度场（emergent height field）守恒。通过解析绕数、四个子格高度和晶格动量，隔离每个碎裂扇区中最大的连通Krylov分量，并分析其谱统计、纠缠熵和连通性。

Result: 两种标准混沌诊断（chaos diagnostics）表现出不同行为：在不同动量扇区中，能级间距统计（level-spacing statistics）从近泊松分布到Wigner-Dyson分布变化；然而在每个扇区中，本征态纠缠熵均坍缩到一条狭窄的穹顶形曲线上，该曲线是本征态热化（eigenstate thermalization）的特征。仅在选定的扇区中存在少量低纠缠离群值（low-entanglement outliers）打破这一热化模式。

Conclusion: 强运动学约束（strong kinematic constraints）可能导致谱关联（spectral correlations）与本征态热化不必遵循相同的普适特征——这是约束量子混沌（constrained quantum chaos）的一种表现。

Abstract: Strongly constrained quantum systems, in which local rules forbid most configurations, play a central role in condensed matter and lattice gauge theory. Their thermalization is often thought to be delicate: extensive conservation laws and dynamically frozen states can shatter the Hilbert space into many disconnected sectors. A natural question is whether, once the frozen states are removed, the dynamics within a single sector still thermalizes. We address this in the height-conserving quantum dimer model on the square lattice, whose local plaquette flips conserve an emergent height field. Resolving the winding numbers, the four sublattice heights, and lattice momentum , we isolate the dominant connected Krylov component of each fragmented sector and analyze its spectral spectral statistics, entanglement, and connectivity. The two standard chaos diagnostics then show different behavior:across momentum sectors the level-spacing statistics range from near-Poisoon to Wigner-Dyson, yet in every sector the eigenstate entanglement entropy collapses onto a narrow, dome-shaped curve characteristic of eigenstate thermalization. Only a handful of low-entanglement outliers interrupt this thermal pattern, in selected sectors. Thus, strong kinematic constraints can lead to a situation where spectral correlations and eigenstate thermalization need not follow the same universal signatures -- a manifestation of constrained quantum chaos.

</details>
